### ApexClass @ 35.0 ×1

Components: `force-app/main/default/classes/LegacyService.cls-meta.xml`

_Candidates for ApexClass between API 35.0 and 67.0 — Almanac did not read this source. Confirm each against the actual code before acting._
_**Full procedure:** after confirming corpus candidates against the source, apply Gate 1 + Gate 2 validation (upgrade-guide.md §4b)._

- **[breaking]** The postFeedElement method overload that uploads a binary file while creating a feed post has been removed. Code must now upload files separately before attaching them to posts. _(v36-apex-012, Spring '16)_
  - Test: Refactor any code using postFeedElement(communityId, feedElement, feedElementFileUpload) to first upload files via ContentVersion, then attach using the new postFeedElement method with the files property in FeedElementCapabilitiesInput.
- **[breaking]** Five ConnectApi.Recommendations methods lacking the channel parameter have been removed and replaced with versions requiring the channel argument. _(v36-apex-013, Spring '16)_
  - Test: Update calls to getRecommendationsForUser, getScheduledRecommendations, and createScheduledRecommendation to use the new overloads that include the channel parameter.
- **[breaking]** Feed posts can no longer upload a binary file and create the post in a single call. Files must be uploaded separately first, then attached via the new FilesCapabilityInput and FileIdInput classes. _(v36-apex-014, Spring '16)_
  - Test: Refactor any Chatter in Apex code that creates feed posts with inline file uploads to use a two-step process: upload the file first, then attach it using ConnectApi.FilesCapabilityInput with the file ID.
- **[breaking]** Two ConnectApi output class properties were removed: EmailMessageCapability.textBody (replaced by body) and FeedElementCapabilities.content (replaced by files). Code referencing these properties will fail at v36+. _(v36-apex-015, Spring '16)_
  - Test: Before upgrading past 36.0, search for references to ConnectApi.EmailMessageCapability.textBody and ConnectApi.FeedElementCapabilities.content; migrate to the body and files properties respectively.
- **[breaking]** The Recent Items component's entityNames property in FlexiPage XML now requires JSON array syntax instead of comma-separated strings. Existing pages using the old format will fail validation. _(v36-packaging-001, Spring '16)_
  - Test: Update any FlexiPage XML files containing Recent Items components to use JSON array format for entityNames (e.g., change 'Account,obj__c' to '["Account","obj__c"]').
- **[breaking]** The ActivitiesSettings.allowUsersToRelateMultipleContactsToTasksAndEvents field becomes read-only starting in API v36.0, preventing any code from modifying Shared Activities enablement via the Metadata API. _(v36-packaging-003, Spring '16)_
  - Test: Audit any Metadata API deployments or tooling that sets allowUsersToRelateMultipleContactsToTasksAndEvents and remove those assignments before upgrading to API 36.0.
- **[breaking]** The ConnectApi.ManagedTopics method getManagedTopics(communityId, managedTopicType, recordId, depth) that accepts a single recordId is no longer supported starting in v38.0; callers must switch to the new overload that accepts a list of topic IDs. _(v38-apex-003, Winter '17)_
  - Test: Replace calls to getManagedTopics with a single recordId with the new getManagedTopics overload that takes a recordIds list parameter before upgrading past API version 38.0.
- **[breaking]** Picklist metadata types are restructured in v38.0: Picklist splits into StandardValueSet and ValueSet, GlobalPicklist becomes GlobalValueSet, GlobalPicklistValue and PicklistValue become CustomValue, and GlobalPicklistTranslation splits into StandardValueSetTranslation and GlobalValueSetTranslation. _(v38-packaging-002, Winter '17)_
  - Test: Update package.xml files, deployment scripts, and any tooling that references the old picklist metadata type names before moving to API 38.0.
- **[breaking]** The PermissionSet.userLicense field is deprecated and unavailable from v38.0 onward; use the new license field instead, which accepts both permission set licenses and user licenses. _(v38-packaging-005, Winter '17)_
  - Test: Update any tooling or scripts that reference PermissionSet.userLicense to use the license field before deploying at API 38.0 or later.
- **[breaking]** CustomField.globalPicklist is removed and Translations.globalPicklists is replaced by customValue; picklist translations now require GlobalValueSetTranslation and StandardValueSetTranslation types. _(v38-packaging-006, Winter '17)_
  - Test: Refactor metadata packages that use globalPicklist on CustomField or globalPicklists on Translations to use the new GlobalValueSet and corresponding translation types.
- **[breaking]** The Product2Id field on WorkOrderLineItem becomes read-only at API 38.0; setting PricebookEntryId now auto-populates Product2Id, and direct writes to Product2Id via API or code fail. _(v38-rest-003, Winter '17)_
  - Test: Before upgrading past 37.0, search Apex and integrations for writes to WorkOrderLineItem.Product2Id and refactor them to use PricebookEntryId. Verify page layouts show the Product field (PricebookEntryId). If editable Product2Id is required, maintain a Visualforce page at API 37.0.
- **[breaking]** The Id field on LoginEvent is no longer populated starting in API version 40.0; code must use the new UniqueKey field as the primary key instead. _(v40-soql-006, Summer '17)_
  - Test: Update all SOQL queries, Apex code, and external integrations that reference LoginEvent.Id to use UniqueKey instead before upgrading to API 40.0.
- **[breaking]** The CustomApplication metadata type was restructured significantly: fields were renamed (customShortcut→customShortcuts, tab→tabs, workspaceMappings→workspaceConfig), moved into new subtypes (ServiceCloudConsoleConfig, AppPreferences), and several subtypes were deleted or replaced (DomainWhitelist, PagesToOpen, CustomApplicationComponents→AppComponentList). _(v42-packaging-002, Spring '18)_
  - Test: Review any deployment scripts, metadata parsing code, or CI pipelines that interact with CustomApplication metadata. Update field references from old names (tab, customShortcut, workspaceMappings) to new names, and adjust for the new subtype hierarchy.
- **[breaking]** Several BotVersion metadata fields (apexClass, botVariable, field, leftOperandBotVariable, LocalMlDomain, operandType, sobjectType, value) were removed starting in API 44.0 and replaced with new fields for invocation actions and conversation variables. _(v44-packaging-005, Winter '19)_
  - Test: Update any deployment scripts or metadata packages that reference the removed BotVersion fields to use the replacement fields before deploying at API 44.0 or higher.
- **[breaking]** ProfileActionOverride can no longer be defined directly on Profile metadata; it must be accessed through CustomApplication instead, and Home page assignments now require a corresponding app assignment. _(v45-packaging-008, Spring '19)_
  - Test: Refactor any Profile metadata that defines ProfileActionOverride to instead define it within CustomApplication, and ensure Home page assignments include app associations.
- **[breaking]** JavaScript remoting calls to @RemoteAction methods now validate that string arguments declared as Id parameters conform to the 15/18-character Salesforce ID format, throwing RemoteObjectException for malformed values. _(v48-vf-004, Spring '20)_
  - Test: Review Visualforce pages using JavaScript remoting with Id-typed parameters; ensure client-side code never passes arbitrary or user-controlled strings without validation, and add error handling for the new RemoteObjectException.
- **[breaking]** The @JsonAccess annotation now defaults both serialization and deserialization to sameNamespace instead of the previous defaults (always for deserialization, sameNamespace for serialization). Classes at v49+ can no longer be deserialized by code outside their namespace unless explicitly annotated. _(v49-apex-004, Summer '20)_
  - Test: Before upgrading classes past v48, identify any cross-namespace JSON deserialization dependencies and add explicit @JsonAccess(deserializable='always') where external callers must deserialize your types.
- **[breaking]** The ManagedContentMediaNodeValue.altUrl property is removed; applications must now retrieve thumbnail information from the thumbnailUrl property instead. _(v49-rest-015, Summer '20)_
  - Test: Search for references to ConnectApi.ManagedContentMediaNodeValue.altUrl and replace them with thumbnailUrl before upgrading to v49.0.
- **[breaking]** Several metadata fields are deleted in API 51.0: AnalyticsSettings fields (canSubscribeDashboardWidgets, enablePowerInsights, enableWaveTemplate, enableSmartDataDiscovery), SiteSettings.enableWebruntimeBYOTemplate, SecuritySettings fields (enableSetPasswordInApi, isTLSv12Required, isTLSv12RequiredCommunities), and SessionSettings.securityCentralKillSession. _(v51-packaging-013, Spring '21)_
  - Test: Search package.xml, deployment scripts, and metadata files for these field names. Remove or conditionally exclude them when deploying to API 51.0+.
- **[breaking]** DescribeFieldResult.getReferenceTo() now returns cross-object references even when the running user lacks access to the referenced object, whereas v50 and earlier returned an empty list in that scenario. _(v51-sharing-002, Spring '21)_
  - Test: Review code that checks getReferenceTo() results to handle security; logic assuming an empty list means no relationship may now receive references the user cannot actually access.
- **[breaking]** The System.Site.getBaseInsecureUrl() method is no longer available starting with API version 52.0. Code referencing this method will fail compilation when upgraded. _(v52-apex-007, Summer '21)_
  - Test: Replace calls to getBaseInsecureUrl() with an alternative approach such as getBaseUrl() or Site.getBaseSecureUrl() before upgrading classes past v51.
- **[breaking]** Platform cache methods in Cache.Session and Cache.Org now throw Cache.InvalidParamException when given keys containing non-alphanumeric characters, whereas earlier versions threw a different exception type or none at all for the cacheBuilder variant. _(v53-apex-003, Winter '22)_
  - Test: Audit cache key values and catch blocks before upgrading past 53.0; ensure keys are alphanumeric-only and update exception handling from OrgCacheException to InvalidParamException where applicable.
- **[breaking]** The serviceResourceId property on ConnectApi.ShiftsFromPatternInput is removed starting in v53.0; code must switch to the new serviceResourceIdList property instead. _(v53-apex-004, Winter '22)_
  - Test: Before upgrading past 53.0, refactor any code referencing ShiftsFromPatternInput.serviceResourceId to use serviceResourceIdList with a list value.
- **[breaking]** The isAccessible() method on DescribeSObjectResult now correctly returns false when users lack permissions for custom settings and custom metadata types, whereas earlier versions incorrectly returned true. _(v54-apex-004, Spring '22)_
  - Test: Review code that calls isAccessible() on custom settings or custom metadata types; logic relying on the prior permissive behavior may now fail permission checks after upgrading past 54.0.
- **[breaking]** Methods annotated with @AuraEnabled can no longer share the same name with different parameter signatures within a class; the compiler now rejects such overloads. _(v55-apex-005, Summer '22)_
  - Test: Before upgrading past 55.0, search for overloaded @AuraEnabled methods and rename them to unique method names, then update any LWC or Aura components calling the renamed methods.
- **[breaking]** ConnectApi.ProductDetail no longer returns the entitlement property and ConnectApi.ProductOverview no longer returns the prices property. Code referencing these properties will fail at compile or runtime. _(v58-rest-003, Summer '23)_
  - Test: Before upgrading past API 57.0, search Apex for references to ProductDetail.entitlement and ProductOverview.prices and remove or replace them. Also update any references to the renamed classes.
- **[breaking]** The getProducts method in ConnectApi.CommerceCatalog no longer returns pricing data regardless of the excludePrices parameter; you must now call ConnectApi.CommerceStorePricing separately to retrieve prices. _(v58-rest-002, Summer '23)_
  - Test: Before upgrading to 58.0, locate any code calling CommerceCatalog.getProducts that depends on pricing fields in the response and refactor it to call CommerceStorePricing for price data.
- **[breaking]** The URL.getSalesforceBaseUrl() method no longer compiles when a class targets API version 59.0 or higher. Developers must migrate to getOrgDomainUrl() or getCurrentRequestUrl() before upgrading. _(v59-apex-008, Winter '24)_
  - Test: Search your codebase for getSalesforceBaseUrl() calls and replace them with getOrgDomainUrl() (for org domain) or getCurrentRequestUrl() (for full request URL) before bumping any class past v58.0.
- **[breaking]** The async DML methods (Database.insertImmediate(), Database.insertAsync(), etc.) now enforce strict type checking and throw a TypeException if you pass standard or custom sObjects instead of external/big objects. Additionally, these operations no longer count against DML statement and row limits. _(v60-apex-009, Spring '24)_
  - Test: Before upgrading past 60.0, search for usages of Database.insertImmediate/insertAsync and verify only external or big objects are passed; add try-catch for TypeException if mixed-object scenarios existed, and review any limit-monitoring code that tracked these operations.
- **[breaking]** Autolaunched flows invoked from Apex classes using 'with sharing' now inherit and enforce those sharing rules instead of running in system context without sharing. Queries may return fewer records and operations may fail due to permission constraints. _(v62-flow-004, Winter '25)_
  - Test: Before upgrading flows to v62+, review autolaunched flows called from 'with sharing' Apex classes to ensure they function correctly under restricted data access. Test with users who have limited sharing visibility.
- **[breaking]** Modifying a Set during iteration in a for or foreach loop now throws a System.FinalException, whereas earlier versions silently allowed it with unpredictable outcomes. _(v62-apex-002, Winter '25)_
  - Test: Audit code for patterns that add or remove Set elements mid-iteration; refactor to collect changes in a separate collection and apply them after the loop completes.
- **[breaking]** Apex now consistently throws a DmlException when code attempts to reparent a master-detail child record whose relationship definition disallows reparenting. Previously, the operation could silently succeed depending on the order fields were assigned. _(v63-apex-007, Spring '25)_
  - Test: Before upgrading Apex to v63.0, search for DML updates that reassign master-detail fields and verify the relationship allows reparenting or add try-catch handling for the new DmlException.
- **[breaking]** Serializing custom or built-in exception objects via JSON.serialize() now throws an error instead of producing incomplete output. Code that previously relied on exception serialization will fail at runtime after upgrading to v63+. _(v63-apex-008, Spring '25)_
  - Test: Search for JSON.serialize() calls that might receive exception objects and refactor to serialize only the relevant exception properties (message, stack trace, type name) as a custom wrapper object instead.
- **[breaking]** Abstract and override methods now require an explicit public, protected, or global modifier; omitting an access modifier or using private causes a compilation failure. _(v65-apex-005, Winter '26)_
  - Test: Before upgrading classes past v65, scan for abstract/override methods lacking explicit access modifiers and add public, protected, or global as appropriate.
- **[breaking]** Flows now enforce stricter visibility rules for Apex class constructors used as invocable action parameters. Public no-arg constructors in managed packages become visible only to code within the same package, causing errors when flows reference inaccessible invocableVariable classes. _(v66-flow-005, Spring '26)_
  - Test: Before upgrading flows to v66+, audit any Apex actions that use invocableVariable classes from managed packages and verify the referenced constructors remain accessible from your namespace.
- **[breaking]** REST API invocable action calls now verify that custom Apex input classes have an accessible no-argument constructor; calls fail if the constructor is private or otherwise inaccessible. _(v66-rest-013, Spring '26)_
  - Test: Before upgrading integrations to API 66.0, audit Apex classes used as invocable action parameters and ensure their no-arg constructors are public or global.
- **[breaking]** Custom Apex classes serving as invocable action parameters now require an explicitly visible no-argument constructor when compiled at v66+. If your class defines any parameterized constructor, you must also add an accessible no-arg constructor or invocations via Flow, REST, or Apex will fail at runtime. _(v67-apex-016, Summer '26)_
  - Test: Before upgrading past 65.0, audit all @InvocableVariable classes that define constructors with parameters and add a visible no-argument constructor. Test invocable action calls from flows and REST to confirm instantiation succeeds.
- **[breaking]** Invocable action calls now validate that custom Apex parameter classes have visible no-argument constructors. Previously invalid classes may now cause runtime failures. _(v67-rest-001, Summer '26)_
  - Test: Ensure all custom Apex classes used as invocable action parameters have public or global no-argument constructors before calling via API 66.0+.
- **[breaking]** REST API invocable action calls now validate that custom Apex parameter classes expose a visible no-argument constructor; requests fail if the constructor is private or protected. _(v67-rest-012, Summer '26)_
  - Test: Audit Apex classes used as invocable action inputs and ensure each has a public or global no-arg constructor before upgrading integrations to API 66.0+.
- **[breaking]** AccountCleanInfo and ContactCleanInfo objects, deprecated in v65, are now fully removed. Any code referencing these objects will fail when targeting v67 or higher. _(v67-rest-016, Summer '26)_
  - Test: Search your codebase for references to AccountCleanInfo and ContactCleanInfo; remove or replace them with alternative data-quality solutions before upgrading past v66.
- **[breaking]** Apex DML and SOQL operations now execute with the current user's permissions and sharing rules by default instead of system context when components target API version 67.0 or higher. _(v67-sharing-002, Summer '26)_
  - Test: Audit Apex code for operations that assumed system-mode access. Test with restricted users and add explicit 'without sharing' or System.runAs() where system privileges are required.
- **[breaking]** Classes that omit a sharing declaration now run as 'with sharing' instead of 'without sharing', so record-level access rules that were previously bypassed get enforced. _(v67-sharing-003, Summer '26)_
  - Test: Review classes lacking sharing keywords. Add 'without sharing' where system-level record access is intentional, or verify business logic works correctly under sharing enforcement.
- **[breaking]** Apex database operations (SOQL, SOSL, DML, Database methods) now enforce object-level, field-level, and sharing permissions of the running user by default instead of bypassing them in system mode. _(v67-sharing-006, Summer '26)_
  - Test: Before upgrading classes past 67.0, audit all SOQL/SOSL queries and DML operations that relied on implicit system-mode access. Add explicit 'as system' or WITH SYSTEM_MODE where full data access is intentional, and run integration tests under restricted users to catch permission failures.
- **[breaking]** The WITH SECURITY_ENFORCED clause is no longer supported in SOQL queries for components at API 67.0+. Queries using this clause will fail. _(v67-soql-001, Summer '26)_
  - Test: Replace WITH SECURITY_ENFORCED with stripInaccessible() or WITH USER_MODE before upgrading components past API 66.0.
- **[breaking]** SOQL and SOSL queries using WITH SECURITY_ENFORCED will fail to compile once an Apex class targets API version 67.0 or higher; the clause has been fully removed from the language at that version. _(v67-soql-002, Summer '26)_
  - Test: Before upgrading any Apex class past v66.0, search for WITH SECURITY_ENFORCED and replace each occurrence with WITH USER_MODE to preserve field-level security enforcement.
- **[behavior-change]** ProfileTabVisibility now consistently returns 'Hidden' via the API when tab visibility is hidden, regardless of whether it was set through the UI or API. Earlier versions only returned 'Hidden' if set programmatically. _(v37-packaging-002, Summer '16)_
  - Test: Review any deployment scripts or tools that parse ProfileTabVisibility and expect blank values for UI-set hidden tabs; they will now receive 'Hidden' explicitly.
- **[behavior-change]** The instanceOf operator now correctly evaluates to true when checking if a class extending a type from a managed package is an instance of that base type. Previously this returned false incorrectly. _(v39-apex-008, Spring '17)_
  - Test: Review any code that uses instanceOf checks against managed package types, especially where subclassing is involved. Logic that worked around the previous bug may now behave differently.
- **[behavior-change]** PermissionSet metadata retrieval now returns all associated content (Apex class assignments, object CRUD, field permissions, etc.) instead of only app and system permissions. Packages and retrieval scripts may receive substantially more data than before. _(v40-packaging-006, Summer '17)_
  - Test: Review deployment and CI scripts that parse or diff PermissionSet metadata; expect larger payloads and adjust validation logic accordingly.
- **[behavior-change]** Wildcard retrieval of Workflow metadata no longer returns empty files for entities without workflow rules or actions; previously every standard and custom entity produced a file regardless of content. _(v41-packaging-013, Winter '18)_
  - Test: If your CI/CD or source-tracking relies on the presence of empty Workflow files for all entities, update scripts to handle the reduced file list at v41.0+.
- **[behavior-change]** Dashboard metadata type replaced the dashboardChartTheme and dashboardColorPalette fields with chartTheme and colorPalette respectively starting in v42. The old fields remain only for backward compatibility with earlier API versions. _(v42-packaging-003, Spring '18)_
  - Test: When deploying Dashboard metadata at v42+, use chartTheme and colorPalette instead of the deprecated dashboardChartTheme and dashboardColorPalette fields.
- **[behavior-change]** Platform event publications in Apex tests now trigger subscribed flows and processes when the test class is at v43.0+, enabling automated verification of event-driven automation. Tests at v42.0 and earlier do not fire these subscribers. _(v43-apex-016, Summer '18)_
  - Test: After upgrading test classes past 43.0, verify that any platform-event-publishing tests account for side effects from subscribed flows and processes that will now execute during test runs.
- **[behavior-change]** The ConnectApi.User output class no longer populates the stamps property for performance reasons; code must now query stamps via SOQL instead. _(v44-apex-006, Winter '19)_
  - Test: Replace any reliance on ConnectApi.User.stamps with a direct SOQL query against the appropriate stamps object before upgrading past v44.0.
- **[behavior-change]** WITH SECURITY_ENFORCED is now GA but introduces new restrictions on polymorphic lookup fields: traversing polymorphic relationships and using TYPEOF with ELSE clauses are disallowed (except for Owner, CreatedBy, and LastModifiedBy fields). _(v48-soql-001, Spring '20)_
  - Test: Review SOQL queries using WITH SECURITY_ENFORCED for polymorphic relationship traversals or TYPEOF with ELSE clauses; refactor affected queries to remove these patterns or handle security checking differently.
- **[behavior-change]** Topic images for featured and navigational topics are now stored as asset files instead of documents, which changes the URL format returned by coverImageUrl and featuredImageUrl properties in ConnectApi.TopicImages. _(v50-rest-014, Winter '21)_
  - Test: If your code parses or caches topic image URLs from ConnectApi.TopicImages, verify the new asset-file-based URL format works with your integration after upgrading past v50.0.
- **[behavior-change]** Schema.DescribeFieldResult.getReferenceTo() now returns referenced objects even when the running user lacks access to them, whereas previously inaccessible objects were omitted from the result. _(v51-apex-006, Spring '21)_
  - Test: Review code using getReferenceTo() and add explicit accessibility checks if business logic depended on the old filtering behavior.
- **[behavior-change]** The String.format() method now correctly handles single quotes in the format string pattern. Previously in v50.0 and earlier, single quotes were ignored or mishandled. _(v51-apex-007, Spring '21)_
  - Test: Review any String.format() calls that work around the old single-quote limitation; the workaround may now produce doubled quotes or other unexpected output on v51.0+.
- **[behavior-change]** FieldService namespace scheduling methods become synchronous instead of asynchronous when ESO is enabled and the calling code is at API 56.0 or later. _(v56-apex-007, Winter '23)_
  - Test: Review code calling FieldService scheduling methods; synchronous execution may change error handling patterns and timeout behavior compared to the previous async model.
- **[behavior-change]** Apex invocable actions called via REST API now roll back the entire transaction when an exception occurs, preventing partial data commits. The org-wide Release Update enforcement was dropped in Spring '25, but the behavior now applies automatically to flows at API 64.0+. _(v64-apex-017, Summer '25)_
  - Test: Before upgrading flows to API 64.0+, verify that Apex invocable actions handle exceptions gracefully and that callers expect atomic all-or-nothing behavior. Ensure input/output collections match in size and order to avoid exceptions.
- **[behavior-change]** User-mode DML operations (insert as user, update as user, etc.) now throw DmlException instead of SecurityException when validation fails, such as missing required fields. _(v58-apex-004, Summer '23)_
  - Test: Review catch blocks that handle user-mode DML failures; code catching SecurityException must be updated to catch DmlException instead when upgrading past v58.0.
- **[behavior-change]** Test.startTest() and Test.stopTest() now automatically release all active savepoints in tests running on API version 60.0+, logging a SAVEPOINT_RESET event when this occurs. _(v60-apex-006, Spring '24)_
  - Test: Review tests that create savepoints and rely on them persisting across startTest/stopTest boundaries; they will now be cleared automatically.
- **[behavior-change]** The default quiddity value for events without an assigned quiddity changes from Synchronous Uncategorized (R) to undefined (UD) in v60+ Apex code. _(v60-apex-010, Spring '24)_
  - Test: Review any Apex logic that inspects Request.getQuiddity() and expects the R value as a fallback; update conditionals to handle UD instead.
- **[behavior-change]** Apex REST API now returns JSON by default when the HTTP ACCEPT header is missing or malformed, aligning with other Salesforce APIs. Previously, classes at v59 and earlier would return an error in these cases. _(v60-rest-013, Spring '24)_
  - Test: Review any Apex REST endpoints that rely on error responses for missing/malformed ACCEPT headers, and verify clients sending requests without proper headers can handle JSON responses.
- **[behavior-change]** Private methods in abstract or virtual classes are no longer shadowed by subclass methods with identical signatures once the superclass is at API 61.0+. Previously, subclass methods would override private superclass methods despite the private visibility. _(v61-apex-007, Summer '24)_
  - Test: Review class hierarchies where subclasses define methods matching private method signatures in parent classes. After upgrading the superclass past 61.0, both methods will execute independently rather than the subclass method replacing the parent's private method.
- **[behavior-change]** Custom exception classes that override equals() and hashCode() now behave correctly when used in collections or comparisons, fixing previous inconsistent handling. _(v61-apex-009, Summer '24)_
  - Test: Review any code relying on custom exception identity checks or storing custom exceptions in Sets/Maps; behavior may differ after upgrading to 61.0.
- **[behavior-change]** The DescribeFieldResult.getRelationshipOrder method now returns meaningful values (0 for primary, 1 for secondary) when invoked on standard fields, whereas previously it always returned null. _(v61-apex-010, Summer '24)_
  - Test: Review any code that calls getRelationshipOrder on standard fields and expects null; update logic to handle the new integer return values.
- **[behavior-change]** SOQL queries against Data Cloud DMOs using Database.QueryLocator or FOR loops now return all matching records at API 61.0+, whereas earlier versions truncate results to the first 201 rows. _(v61-soql-001, Summer '24)_
  - Test: Review any Apex at pre-61.0 that queries DMOs via QueryLocator or FOR loops expecting ≤201 rows. After upgrading, larger result sets may affect memory, Data Cloud credit consumption, and downstream logic.
- **[behavior-change]** Autolaunched flows invoked from Apex classes declared with 'with sharing' now respect the caller's sharing rules when running in default context. Previously these flows ignored sharing and could access all records. _(v62-flow-006, Winter '25)_
  - Test: Before upgrading Apex or Flow components to API 62.0+, audit autolaunched flows called from 'with sharing' classes. Verify they still function correctly under restricted data access, or explicitly set flow run context to system mode where broader access is intentional.
- **[behavior-change]** SOQL queries using WITH USER_MODE now execute successfully when running as the Automated Process User, whereas in earlier API versions these queries would fail unless explicitly switched to system mode. _(v66-soql-001, Spring '26)_
  - Test: Review any workarounds or error handling you implemented for USER_MODE queries failing under Automated Process User context; these may no longer be necessary after upgrading to v66.
- **[retirement]** The ChatterMobileSettings and TouchMobileSettings subtypes along with their corresponding chatterMobile and touchMobile fields were removed from MobileSettings metadata type starting in API version 46.0. _(v61-packaging-006, Summer '24)_
  - Test: Remove any references to these deprecated MobileSettings fields from package.xml files and deployment scripts before upgrading API versions past the removal thresholds.
- **[retirement]** AccountInsightsSettings and OpportunityInsightsSettings metadata types, along with the enableAccountInsightsInMobile and enableOpportunityInsightsInMobile fields, are deprecated and effectively retired in v59.0 as the underlying Einstein features have been replaced by Einstein Relationship Insights and Deal Insights. _(v59-packaging-002, Winter '24)_
  - Test: Remove any deployment or retrieval of AccountInsightsSettings and OpportunityInsightsSettings from your package manifests and migrate to the replacement Einstein features before upgrading to API 59.0.
- **[deprecation]** The FlexiPage.pageTemplate field is deprecated starting in API version 39.0; use the template field instead when working with Lightning Page metadata. _(v39-packaging-002, Spring '17)_
  - Test: Update any metadata deployments or tooling that references FlexiPage.pageTemplate to use the template field instead.

  - Test: Update integrations and scripts that read or write FlexiPage.SobjectType to use EntityDefinitionId before the field is eventually removed.
- **[deprecation]** The getAvgValueSize() and getMaxValueSize() methods on Cache.Org, Cache.Partition, and Cache.Session are deprecated starting in v50.0; use getAvgGetSize() and getMaxGetSize() instead. _(v50-apex-012, Winter '21)_
  - Test: Replace calls to getAvgValueSize() with getAvgGetSize() and getMaxValueSize() with getMaxGetSize() before upgrading classes past v49.0.
- **[deprecation]** The targetAppDeveloperName and targetAppNamespacePrefix fields on PromptVersion are deprecated starting in API 51.0. _(v51-packaging-014, Spring '21)_
  - Test: Plan migration away from these fields; they may be removed in a future release. Check In-App Guidance prompts that rely on app-specific targeting.
- **[deprecation]** The two-argument AuthConfiguration constructor that accepts networkId and startUrl parameters is deprecated starting with API version 56.0. _(v56-auth-002, Winter '23)_
  - Test: Identify any code using the AuthConfiguration(networkId, startUrl) constructor and migrate to an alternative constructor or approach before upgrading past 56.0.
- **[deprecation]** The recalculateFormulas() method on SObject is no longer supported starting with v57.0; developers must migrate to the Formula.recalculateFormulas() method instead. _(v57-apex-010, Spring '23)_
  - Test: Before upgrading past 57.0, search for any SObject.recalculateFormulas() calls and replace them with System.Formula.recalculateFormulas().
- **[deprecation]** The enableExperienceFriendlyUrls field on SiteSettings is deprecated starting in v59.0; it remains functional only through v58.0. Developers must switch to the expFriendlyUrlsAsDefault field on the Network metadata type for v59.0 and later. _(v59-packaging-001, Winter '24)_
  - Test: Replace any references to SiteSettings.enableExperienceFriendlyUrls with Network.expFriendlyUrlsAsDefault before targeting API version 59.0 or higher.
- **[deprecation]** The enableXssProtection field on SecuritySettings metadata type is deprecated starting in API version 60.0; CSPTrustedSite should be used instead for XSS protection configuration. _(v60-packaging-006, Spring '24)_
  - Test: Migrate any automation or deployment scripts that set enableXssProtection to use CSPTrustedSite metadata type instead before upgrading to API 60.0+.
- **[deprecation]** The sameCarrier property on InsurancePolicyBulkRenewInputRepresentation and InsurancePolicyRenewInputRepresentation Connect API input classes is deprecated starting with v66.0. _(v66-rest-028, Spring '26)_
  - Test: Review Apex code or integrations that set the sameCarrier property on insurance policy renewal inputs and migrate to the replacement approach before this property is removed in a future release.
- **[additive]** Apex methods can now declare cacheability directly via @AuraEnabled(cacheable=true) annotation, eliminating the need for client-side setStorable() calls on each action invocation. _(v44-apex-002, Winter '19)_
- **[additive]** Batch Apex can now fire platform events on errors in all job phases (start, execute, finish), whereas the beta only supported execute. The event payload now identifies which phase encountered the error. _(v46-apex-004, Summer '19)_
- **[additive]** New WITH SECURITY_ENFORCED clause available in SOQL SELECT statements within Apex to automatically enforce field-level and object-level security, throwing an exception when the user lacks access to referenced fields or objects. _(v45-soql-001, Spring '19)_
- **[additive]** The @namespaceAccessible annotation now works with interfaces, abstract classes, and properties, allowing these constructs to be exposed across namespace boundaries in 2GP packages. Additionally, stricter containment rules require annotated members to reside in annotated outer classes. _(v50-packaging-004, Winter '21)_
- **[additive]** Apex code at v61+ can call SObjectType.getDescribe() on Data Cloud DMOs to retrieve object metadata, but field-level and record-level security checks remain unsupported—only object-level access is enforced. _(v61-apex-005, Summer '24)_
- **[additive]** SOQL relationship queries in Apex can now traverse up to five levels of parent-to-child records (one parent root plus four nested child subqueries), where previously fewer levels were supported. Each subquery counts toward the 300 aggregate query limit. _(v61-soql-002, Summer '24)_
- **[additive]** Data Cloud SOQL gains MIN and MAX aggregate functions, and all aggregate functions (AVG, SUM, COUNT, MIN, MAX) now work against Data Lake Objects in addition to Data Model Objects. _(v65-soql-001, Winter '26)_
- **[additive]** Apex cursors for SOQL results are now GA, introducing standard cursors (for queueable-based large dataset processing as an alternative to batch Apex) and pagination cursors (for UI pagination). Both support bidirectional traversal and come with new Limits methods and AuraEnabled serialization support. _(v66-apex-005, Spring '26)_
- **[additive]** System.purgeOldAsyncJobs() gains a new overload accepting a maximum record count, letting you delete completed async jobs incrementally rather than all at once. _(v66-apex-008, Spring '26)_
- **[additive]** New Apex methods allow programmatic updates and deletions of named credentials, external credentials, and external auth identity providers. Updating endpoint URLs via Apex disables the credential for callouts until an admin re-enables it. _(v66-apex-012, Spring '26)_
- **[additive]** External Services binary file handling expands to 100 MB (up from 16 MB), adds a customFileName parameter for Flows, and introduces a deterministic priority order for resolving filenames on downloaded files. _(v67-rest-007, Summer '26)_

- **[breaking]** SControls metadata type is not supported in scratch orgs, so any project relying on legacy SControls cannot be deployed to or tested in a scratch org environment. _(v41-packaging-006, Winter '18, low confidence)_

- **[breaking]** The UsedLicenses field on UserLicense can no longer be used in WHERE clauses starting in API v64. Queries filtering on this field will fail; you must retrieve all records and filter in application code. _(v64-soql-005, Summer '25, low confidence)_

### ApexTrigger @ 52.0 ×1

Components: `force-app/main/default/triggers/AccountTrigger.trigger-meta.xml`

_Candidates for ApexTrigger between API 52.0 and 67.0 — Almanac did not read this source. Confirm each against the actual code before acting._
_**Full procedure:** after confirming corpus candidates against the source, apply Gate 1 + Gate 2 validation (upgrade-guide.md §4b)._

- **[breaking]** Platform cache methods in Cache.Session and Cache.Org now throw Cache.InvalidParamException when given keys containing non-alphanumeric characters, whereas earlier versions threw a different exception type or none at all for the cacheBuilder variant. _(v53-apex-003, Winter '22)_
  - Test: Audit cache key values and catch blocks before upgrading past 53.0; ensure keys are alphanumeric-only and update exception handling from OrgCacheException to InvalidParamException where applicable.
- **[breaking]** The isAccessible() method on DescribeSObjectResult now correctly returns false when users lack permissions for custom settings and custom metadata types, whereas earlier versions incorrectly returned true. _(v54-apex-004, Spring '22)_
  - Test: Review code that calls isAccessible() on custom settings or custom metadata types; logic relying on the prior permissive behavior may now fail permission checks after upgrading past 54.0.
- **[breaking]** The URL.getSalesforceBaseUrl() method no longer compiles when a class targets API version 59.0 or higher. Developers must migrate to getOrgDomainUrl() or getCurrentRequestUrl() before upgrading. _(v59-apex-008, Winter '24)_
  - Test: Search your codebase for getSalesforceBaseUrl() calls and replace them with getOrgDomainUrl() (for org domain) or getCurrentRequestUrl() (for full request URL) before bumping any class past v58.0.
- **[breaking]** The async DML methods (Database.insertImmediate(), Database.insertAsync(), etc.) now enforce strict type checking and throw a TypeException if you pass standard or custom sObjects instead of external/big objects. Additionally, these operations no longer count against DML statement and row limits. _(v60-apex-009, Spring '24)_
  - Test: Before upgrading past 60.0, search for usages of Database.insertImmediate/insertAsync and verify only external or big objects are passed; add try-catch for TypeException if mixed-object scenarios existed, and review any limit-monitoring code that tracked these operations.
- **[breaking]** Modifying a Set during iteration in a for or foreach loop now throws a System.FinalException, whereas earlier versions silently allowed it with unpredictable outcomes. _(v62-apex-002, Winter '25)_
  - Test: Audit code for patterns that add or remove Set elements mid-iteration; refactor to collect changes in a separate collection and apply them after the loop completes.
- **[breaking]** Apex now consistently throws a DmlException when code attempts to reparent a master-detail child record whose relationship definition disallows reparenting. Previously, the operation could silently succeed depending on the order fields were assigned. _(v63-apex-007, Spring '25)_
  - Test: Before upgrading Apex to v63.0, search for DML updates that reassign master-detail fields and verify the relationship allows reparenting or add try-catch handling for the new DmlException.

- **[behavior-change]** Triggers now consistently execute in a 'without sharing' context regardless of the sharing mode of calling code, standardizing trigger execution behavior. _(v67-sharing-004, Summer '26)_
  - Test: Review triggers that may have inherited sharing context from calling classes. Verify record access logic still works as expected with guaranteed system-mode sharing.
- **[retirement]** AccountInsightsSettings and OpportunityInsightsSettings metadata types, along with the enableAccountInsightsInMobile and enableOpportunityInsightsInMobile fields, are deprecated and effectively retired in v59.0 as the underlying Einstein features have been replaced by Einstein Relationship Insights and Deal Insights. _(v59-packaging-002, Winter '24)_
  - Test: Remove any deployment or retrieval of AccountInsightsSettings and OpportunityInsightsSettings from your package manifests and migrate to the replacement Einstein features before upgrading to API 59.0.
- **[deprecation]** The recalculateFormulas() method on SObject is no longer supported starting with v57.0; developers must migrate to the Formula.recalculateFormulas() method instead. _(v57-apex-010, Spring '23)_
  - Test: Before upgrading past 57.0, search for any SObject.recalculateFormulas() calls and replace them with System.Formula.recalculateFormulas().
- **[deprecation]** The enableExperienceFriendlyUrls field on SiteSettings is deprecated starting in v59.0; it remains functional only through v58.0. Developers must switch to the expFriendlyUrlsAsDefault field on the Network metadata type for v59.0 and later. _(v59-packaging-001, Winter '24)_
  - Test: Replace any references to SiteSettings.enableExperienceFriendlyUrls with Network.expFriendlyUrlsAsDefault before targeting API version 59.0 or higher.
- **[deprecation]** The enableXssProtection field on SecuritySettings metadata type is deprecated starting in API version 60.0; CSPTrustedSite should be used instead for XSS protection configuration. _(v60-packaging-006, Spring '24)_
  - Test: Migrate any automation or deployment scripts that set enableXssProtection to use CSPTrustedSite metadata type instead before upgrading to API 60.0+.
- **[additive]** Apex code at v61+ can call SObjectType.getDescribe() on Data Cloud DMOs to retrieve object metadata, but field-level and record-level security checks remain unsupported—only object-level access is enforced. _(v61-apex-005, Summer '24)_
- **[additive]** SOQL relationship queries in Apex can now traverse up to five levels of parent-to-child records (one parent root plus four nested child subqueries), where previously fewer levels were supported. Each subquery counts toward the 300 aggregate query limit. _(v61-soql-002, Summer '24)_
- **[additive]** Data Cloud SOQL gains MIN and MAX aggregate functions, and all aggregate functions (AVG, SUM, COUNT, MIN, MAX) now work against Data Lake Objects in addition to Data Model Objects. _(v65-soql-001, Winter '26)_

<details><summary>Weak provenance (low extraction confidence — verify against the release notes)</summary>

- **[breaking]** The UsedLicenses field on UserLicense can no longer be used in WHERE clauses starting in API v64. Queries filtering on this field will fail; you must retrieve all records and filter in application code. _(v64-soql-005, Summer '25, low confidence)_
  - Test: Search for SOQL queries against UserLicense that filter on UsedLicenses. Refactor them to fetch all UserLicense records and apply the filter in Apex or your integration layer before upgrading to API 64.0.
- **[additive]** SOQL relationship queries can now traverse up to five levels of parent-to-child nesting (one parent root plus four child levels) when executed through REST or SOAP API calls on standard and custom objects. _(v58-soql-001, Summer '23, low confidence)_
- **[additive]** DigitalExperienceBundle now includes an sfdc_cms__styles folder containing styles.css and print.css for global site styling. Developers can add custom global stylesheets to this folder and reference them in head markup. _(v59-packaging-003, Winter '24, low confidence)_

</details>

Components: `force-app/main/default/aura/legacyPanel/legacyPanel.cmp-meta.xml`

_Candidates for Aura between API 45.0 and 67.0 — Almanac did not read this source. Confirm each against the actual code before acting._

- **[breaking]** Several metadata fields are deleted in API 51.0: AnalyticsSettings fields (canSubscribeDashboardWidgets, enablePowerInsights, enableWaveTemplate, enableSmartDataDiscovery), SiteSettings.enableWebruntimeBYOTemplate, SecuritySettings fields (enableSetPasswordInApi, isTLSv12Required, isTLSv12RequiredCommunities), and SessionSettings.securityCentralKillSession. _(v51-packaging-013, Spring '21)_

### Flow @ 61.0 ×1

Components: `force-app/main/default/flows/Order_Fulfillment.flow-meta.xml`

_Candidates for Flow between API 61.0 and 67.0 — Almanac did not read this source. Confirm each against the actual code before acting._
_**Review-only:** verify these corpus changes manually in a scratch/sandbox org. The characterization-test (Gate 1 + Gate 2) procedure does not apply to Flow — there is no Apex test class to validate against._

- **[breaking]** When an Apex action invoked by a flow throws an exception, the entire transaction now rolls back to preserve data integrity. Apex actions must return outputs that match inputs in count and order, or batch executions will fail. _(v64-flow-007, Summer '25)_
  - Test: Review Apex actions called from flows to ensure output collections align with input collections in size and sequence. Test exception handling paths to confirm rollback behavior is acceptable.
- **[breaking]** Create Records element output references return field IDs instead of strings starting at API 65.0, causing flows that reference these outputs to fail on save if they expect string values. _(v65-flow-004, Winter '26)_
  - Test: Before upgrading flows past API 64.0, audit all Create Records elements and change any downstream references to explicitly use the record's ID field rather than the raw element output.
- **[breaking]** Flows now enforce stricter visibility rules for Apex class constructors used as invocable action parameters. Public no-arg constructors in managed packages become visible only to code within the same package, causing errors when flows reference inaccessible invocableVariable classes. _(v66-flow-005, Spring '26)_
  - Test: Before upgrading flows to v66+, audit any Apex actions that use invocableVariable classes from managed packages and verify the referenced constructors remain accessible from your namespace.
- **[breaking]** Before-save record-triggered flows now properly enforce field writeability, rejecting updates to non-insertable fields that were previously silently accepted. _(v66-flow-006, Spring '26)_
  - Test: Review before-save record-triggered flows for field assignments targeting system-controlled or non-insertable fields; remove or guard those assignments before upgrading to v66+.
- **[behavior-change]** Null text values returned from invocable actions now remain null rather than converting to empty strings. Logic that relied on null-to-empty-string coercion may break. _(v62-flow-005, Winter '25)_
  - Test: Audit flows that check invocable action text outputs for empty string versus null conditions; update decision elements and formulas to handle true nulls.
- **[behavior-change]** Autolaunched flows invoked from Apex classes declared with 'with sharing' now respect the caller's sharing rules when running in default context. Previously these flows ignored sharing and could access all records. _(v62-flow-006, Winter '25)_
  - Test: Before upgrading Apex or Flow components to API 62.0+, audit autolaunched flows called from 'with sharing' classes. Verify they still function correctly under restricted data access, or explicitly set flow run context to system mode where broader access is intentional.
- **[behavior-change]** Reactive Data Tables now clear their contents when a screen action's output collection is not assigned, instead of retaining stale records from the previous action execution. _(v63-flow-007, Spring '25)_
  - Test: Review flows where Data Table components depend on screen action outputs; ensure your autolaunched flows explicitly set output collections even when empty, or update UI logic to handle cleared tables.
- **[behavior-change]** Variables in a subflow no longer inherit values from identically-named variables in the parent flow; each flow's variable scope is now isolated. _(v63-flow-008, Spring '25)_
  - Test: Audit parent-subflow pairs for variables sharing API names; explicitly pass values via input/output parameters if the subflow needs parent data.
- **[behavior-change]** Repeater components now always include an initial empty instance in the AddedItems output collection, even when users make no selections in child components like Lookups. Code that checks collection size to detect user input must now iterate and inspect each item for null values instead. _(v64-flow-008, Summer '25)_
  - Test: Update flow logic that relies on Repeater.AddedItems being empty when no selections are made. Add iteration with null-checks on child component fields, or make child input required to prevent empty instances.
- **[behavior-change]** Flow and Process runtime behavior changes when components target API version 65.0, potentially affecting execution semantics. _(v65-flow-001, Winter '26)_
  - Test: Review the specific runtime changes documented for API 65.0 before upgrading Flow versions; test existing flows in sandbox after version bump.
- **[behavior-change]** The typeName field on FlowDataTypeMapping becomes optional starting in API 65.0, whereas flows at v64.0 or earlier still require it. _(v65-flow-003, Winter '26)_
  - Test: Review any deployment tooling or CI/CD that validates or generates FlowDataTypeMapping entries; ensure it handles typeName as optional when targeting v65+.
- **[behavior-change]** Apex invocable action inputs with ID data type now accept null values at run time instead of failing the flow. Previously, passing a null ID caused the flow to error out. _(v65-flow-005, Winter '26)_
  - Test: Review any error-handling logic that relied on flows failing when null IDs were passed to Apex actions; this scenario now succeeds silently.
- **[behavior-change]** Data tables in flows now auto-refresh when field labels, API names, or user/org language settings change. Earlier versions required manual updates and could throw run-time errors if field API names were modified. _(v65-flow-006, Winter '26)_
  - Test: Test flows using data tables after upgrading to confirm automatic field/language synchronization behaves as expected; remove any workarounds for manual refresh.
- **[behavior-change]** Flows and processes built or updated to API version 66.0 incorporate runtime behavior changes that may alter how existing automations execute. _(v66-flow-001, Spring '26)_
  - Test: Review the detailed 'Flow and Process Run-Time Changes in API Version 66.0' documentation before upgrading Flow metadata to v66, and regression-test critical automations.
- **[additive]** Flows gain native Time data type support, enabling direct manipulation of time-of-day values without extracting them from DateTime fields via formulas. _(v64-flow-005, Summer '25)_
- **[additive]** Scheduled flows can now specify a custom batch size (1–200) in the Start element, allowing developers to partition interviews into smaller chunks to avoid governor limit exhaustion in complex automations. _(v67-flow-002, Summer '26)_
- **[additive]** External Services binary file handling expands to 100 MB (up from 16 MB), adds a customFileName parameter for Flows, and introduces a deterministic priority order for resolving filenames on downloaded files. _(v67-rest-007, Summer '26)_

<details><summary>Weak provenance (low extraction confidence — verify against the release notes)</summary>

- **[behavior-change]** When saving a flow in auto-layout mode, the locationX and locationY fields on FlowNode elements are now reset to 0, reducing XML noise when comparing flow versions. _(v64-flow-004, Summer '25, low confidence)_
  - Test: If your CI/CD or version control processes rely on locationX/locationY values in Flow metadata, update your diff tooling to ignore these fields or expect zero values for auto-layout flows at v64+.

</details>

### LWC @ 55.0 ×1

Components: `force-app/main/default/lwc/orderList/orderList.js-meta.xml`

_Candidates for LWC between API 55.0 and 67.0 — Almanac did not read this source. Confirm each against the actual code before acting._
_**Review-only:** verify these corpus changes manually in a scratch/sandbox org. The characterization-test (Gate 1 + Gate 2) procedure does not apply to LWC — there is no Apex test class to validate against._

- **[breaking]** Non-global SLDS design tokens (those marked internal rather than Global Access) are no longer valid in LWC CSS and trigger a validation error at component save time. _(v56-lwc-005, Winter '23)_
  - Test: Audit LWC stylesheets for non-GA token references before upgrading component API versions past 56.0. Replace internal tokens with their global equivalents or define custom Aura design tokens.
- **[breaking]** HTML template validation now treats syntax errors as blocking failures rather than warnings. Components with malformed HTML (such as extra closing template tags) cannot be deployed until fixed. _(v59-lwc-011, Winter '24)_
  - Test: Before upgrading components to v59+, run a local build or VS Code validation pass to surface any HTML errors that were previously tolerated as warnings, and correct them.
- **[breaking]** LWC now renders empty HTML comments instead of empty text nodes for virtual DOM placeholders in slots, scoped slots, and lwc:if directives, which can break tests or code that traverse DOM using childNodes or nextSibling. _(v60-lwc-002, Spring '24)_
  - Test: Review and update test snapshots and any JavaScript that navigates the DOM via childNodes, nextSibling, or similar APIs, since the node types at placeholder positions have changed from text to comment nodes.
- **[breaking]** Light DOM slots now include extra empty text nodes, causing childNodes, firstChild, and lastChild to return different results than before—code indexing into childNodes may now hit whitespace instead of the expected element. _(v60-lwc-003, Spring '24)_
  - Test: Replace uses of childNodes, firstChild, and lastChild with children, firstElementChild, lastElementChild, lwc:ref, or querySelector before upgrading components to API 60.0.
- **[breaking]** LWC decorators (@api, @track, @wire) are now restricted to classes extending LightningElement; using them in plain classes throws a syntax error at version 60.0+. _(v60-lwc-004, Spring '24)_
  - Test: Before upgrading components to API 60.0, search for @api, @track, or @wire in non-LightningElement classes and refactor by either removing the decorators or converting those classes to extend LightningElement.
- **[breaking]** LWC enforces stricter validation of imports and exports from the lwc package at deploy time. Bare imports, any exports from lwc, and imports of private/internal APIs now block deployment. _(v62-lwc-006, Winter '25)_
  - Test: Before upgrading components to v62.0, search for bare imports like `import 'lwc'` and any export statements referencing lwc. Replace bare imports with named imports such as `import { LightningElement } from 'lwc'` and remove all exports from lwc.
- **[behavior-change]** LWC drops Babel transpilation for object rest/spread syntax in favor of native JavaScript behavior, which can change observable side-effect counts in getters due to a Babel bug that previously caused double invocation. _(v60-lwc-005, Spring '24)_
  - Test: Review any components using object destructuring with rest/spread that have getters with side effects; verify that logic does not depend on the getter being called multiple times during a single destructuring operation.
- **[behavior-change]** LWC class attribute binding now interprets arrays and objects semantically rather than stringifying them; booleans, numbers, and functions are stripped instead of coerced to strings. _(v62-lwc-003, Winter '25)_
  - Test: Review components that pass non-string values to class attributes. Code relying on stringified booleans/numbers (e.g., class="true") or comma-separated array output will behave differently after upgrading to v62.
- **[behavior-change]** The this.hostElement property now returns the component's host HTMLElement instead of undefined, enabling direct access to host properties in renderedCallback and other lifecycle hooks. _(v62-lwc-004, Winter '25)_
  - Test: Search LWC code for references to this.hostElement that rely on it being initially undefined. Rename any custom hostElement properties to avoid collision, or explicitly initialize them to undefined before assignment.
- **[behavior-change]** The this.style property on LWC components now returns the host element's CSSStyleDeclaration instead of undefined, enabling direct runtime style manipulation but breaking code that relied on this.style being initially falsy. _(v62-lwc-005, Winter '25)_
  - Test: Search for usages of this.style in light DOM components. If any code depended on this.style being undefined or used it as a custom property, rename to this.customStyle or explicitly initialize to undefined before assignment.
- **[retirement]** AccountInsightsSettings and OpportunityInsightsSettings metadata types, along with the enableAccountInsightsInMobile and enableOpportunityInsightsInMobile fields, are deprecated and effectively retired in v59.0 as the underlying Einstein features have been replaced by Einstein Relationship Insights and Deal Insights. _(v59-packaging-002, Winter '24)_
  - Test: Remove any deployment or retrieval of AccountInsightsSettings and OpportunityInsightsSettings from your package manifests and migrate to the replacement Einstein features before upgrading to API 59.0.
- **[deprecation]** The enableExperienceFriendlyUrls field on SiteSettings is deprecated starting in v59.0; it remains functional only through v58.0. Developers must switch to the expFriendlyUrlsAsDefault field on the Network metadata type for v59.0 and later. _(v59-packaging-001, Winter '24)_
  - Test: Replace any references to SiteSettings.enableExperienceFriendlyUrls with Network.expFriendlyUrlsAsDefault before targeting API version 59.0 or higher.
- **[deprecation]** The enableXssProtection field on SecuritySettings metadata type is deprecated starting in API version 60.0; CSPTrustedSite should be used instead for XSS protection configuration. _(v60-packaging-006, Spring '24)_
  - Test: Migrate any automation or deployment scripts that set enableXssProtection to use CSPTrustedSite metadata type instead before upgrading to API 60.0+.
- **[additive]** LWC gains the ability to dynamically import and instantiate components at runtime, enabling lazy loading and constructor resolution at execution time. Requires LWS enablement. _(v59-lwc-001, Winter '24)_
- **[additive]** LWC now supports component-level API versioning via the apiVersion element in .js-meta.xml, allowing developers to pin components to specific framework behavior. Components at 58.0 or lower all receive Summer '23 behavior; upgrading to 59.0 opts into new versioned behaviors like lowercase CSS scope tokens and stricter HTML parsing errors. _(v59-lwc-002, Winter '24)_

<details><summary>Weak provenance (low extraction confidence — verify against the release notes)</summary>

- **[behavior-change]** New orgs now run Lightning web components under Lightning Web Security (LWS) instead of Lightning Locker by default, which may cause runtime differences for LWCs that rely on Locker-specific behaviors or workarounds. _(v56-lwc-006, Winter '23, low confidence)_
  - Test: Before deploying LWCs to a new org, test them in a sandbox with LWS enabled. Look for DOM access violations, third-party library incompatibilities, and cross-namespace communication issues.
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Web Security adds new API distortions blocking Function constructor, eval, and HTMLObjectElement.data setter, while removing distortions that previously blocked iframe/object contentDocument/contentWindow access and certain window property getters. _(v56-lwc-007, Winter '23, low confidence)_
  - Test: Audit LWC code for eval() or new Function() usage which will now fail. Review any workarounds for iframe content access since those APIs are now available. Run ESLint with the updated LWS rules to detect affected patterns.

  - Test: Replace any usage of shadowSupportMode = 'any' with shadowSupportMode = 'native' in your LWC component classes.

- **[additive]** LWC flow screen components can now programmatically surface validation errors via new setCustomValidity() and reportValidity() methods, enabling richer error handling within Flow Builder screens. _(v63-lwc-010, Spring '25, low confidence)_
- **[additive]** LWC templates can now embed complex JavaScript expressions directly in HTML markup, reducing boilerplate in component JavaScript files. This opt-in capability activates when a component targets API 66.0 or higher. _(v66-lwc-002, Spring '26, low confidence)_

## Org-wide changes in span (apply regardless of component version)

- **[breaking]** The relationship name for retrieving Notes and Attachments via SOQL or Visualforce changed from NotesAndAttachments to CombinedAttachments. For Case, the name changed from Attachments to CombinedAttachments. _(v29-vf-005, Winter '14)_
- **[breaking]** The Limits class methods getInteractionQueries() and getLimitInteractionQueries() have been removed from the platform after being part of a Visual Workflow pilot. _(v30-apex-006, Spring '14)_
- **[breaking]** All governor limits on Apex describe calls (sObjects, fields, field sets, child relationships, picklists, record types) have been eliminated. The 100-object and 100-statement caps no longer apply. _(v31-apex-005, Summer '14)_
- **[breaking]** Connected apps that previously bypassed user profile checks now enforce the 'API Enabled' permission, so users without that permission lose access to affected apps including Salesforce1 mobile, Salesforce for Outlook, and partner integrations. _(v31-auth-003, Summer '14)_
- **[breaking]** Flows now count against standard Apex governor limits for DML statements and SOQL queries. Create/update/delete elements consume DML limits, and lookup elements consume query limits. _(v31-flow-003, Summer '14)_
- **[breaking]** Connected apps that previously bypassed user profile settings now require users to have the 'API Enabled' profile permission. Apps like Salesforce1, Salesforce for Outlook, and Connect for Office will stop working for users lacking this permission. _(v32-auth-001, Winter '15)_
- **[breaking]** The escapeHtml3, escapeHtml4, and escapeEcmaScript String methods now escape additional characters beyond their previous behavior, potentially affecting output that relied on the old escaping rules. _(v33-apex-006, Spring '15)_
- **[breaking]** Lightning component markup now enforces case sensitivity, meaning attribute names, component references, and event names must match their declarations exactly in terms of upper and lowercase characters. _(v33-aura-002, Spring '15)_
- **[breaking]** Lightning component markup now enforces case sensitivity throughout, including attribute references and expressions. Previously only JavaScript and CSS references were case-sensitive. _(v33-aura-003, Spring '15)_
- **[breaking]** API Client Whitelisting blocks all API client applications (Data Loader, Salesforce1, Force.com Migration Tool, etc.) by default unless each client is configured as an approved connected app or the user has the 'Use Any API Client' permission. _(v33-auth-011, Spring '15)_
- **[breaking]** Address and geolocation compound fields are now blocked in BLANKVALUE, CASE, NULLVALUE, PRIORVALUE, and comparison/equality operators within formulas. Existing formulas using these combinations must be corrected before they can be saved again. _(v33-other-004, Spring '15)_
- **[breaking]** The Approval object no longer permits create, update, or upsert operations via API; integrations that programmatically create or modify approval records will fail. _(v33-rest-003, Spring '15)_
- **[breaking]** The ui:input component no longer accepts custom body content; any component extending ui:input that previously injected child elements into the body will break. _(v34-aura-001, Summer '15)_
- **[breaking]** Design files for Lightning App Builder components no longer accept the type field and now only permit int, string, or boolean attribute types. Components using other types or defining types in the design file will fail validation. _(v34-lwc-001, Summer '15)_
- **[breaking]** The XOrgHub and XOrgHubSharedObject metadata types have been removed as the Cross-Organization Data Sharing pilot is no longer available. _(v34-packaging-006, Summer '15)_
- **[breaking]** Custom fields on the User object are no longer retrievable via Tooling API. This corrects unintended exposure in prior releases. _(v34-rest-006, Summer '15)_
- **[breaking]** Apex classes declared with 'with sharing' now respect org-wide sharing rules on the User object, losing their previous unfiltered access when User sharing is set to private. _(v34-sharing-002, Summer '15)_
- **[breaking]** HTML Area home page components now strip JavaScript, CSS, iframes, and other advanced markup both on save and at runtime. Any existing unsupported code is permanently lost when the component is edited. _(v34-vf-005, Summer '15)_
- **[breaking]** Calling PageReference.getContent() or getContentAsPDF() in Apex now counts against callout limits and follows callout restrictions, such as being prohibited in triggers and requiring async handling in certain contexts. _(v38-vf-004, Winter '17)_
- **[breaking]** The ui:outputRichText component now blocks several HTML tags (<object>, <iframe>, <embed>, <form>, <button>, <input>), strips unescaped comments, rejects href values without http/https prefixes, and drops the CSS expression() directive in IE. _(v35-aura-001, Winter '16)_
- **[breaking]** Lightning components require My Domain to be configured in the org. Organizations using Lightning components without My Domain will see those customizations disabled when Winter '16 activates. _(v35-auth-009, Winter '16)_
- **[breaking]** The 'contains' operator for multi-select picklist fields has been removed from Flow conditions because it was never supported at runtime and caused automatic failures. _(v35-flow-002, Winter '16)_
- **[breaking]** Lightning components used in tabs, Lightning pages, or standalone apps stop working in Winter '16 unless My Domain is enabled for the org. Organizations without a custom domain will have these customizations disabled automatically. _(v35-lwc-001, Winter '16)_
- **[breaking]** Canvas apps now render inside two nested iframe elements instead of one, which breaks any JavaScript using parent.postMessage() or other frame-hierarchy-dependent messaging to communicate with Salesforce. _(v35-other-001, Winter '16)_
- **[breaking]** The undocumented Sfdc JavaScript global object is no longer injected into Lightning containers. Components that relied on this internal utility will break, except for the officially supported Sfdc.canvas API which remains available. _(v36-aura-004, Spring '16)_
- **[breaking]** TLS 1.0 is being disabled for HTTPS connections including Force.com Migration Tool, requiring clients to support TLS 1.2. Integrations using older encryption protocols will fail. _(v36-auth-001, Spring '16)_
- **[breaking]** TLS 1.0 will be disabled for all Salesforce connections starting Q1 2016, requiring TLS 1.2 for all inbound and outbound API traffic including Data Loader batch operations. _(v36-auth-002, Spring '16)_
- **[breaking]** jQuery is no longer automatically injected into custom Lightning components. Components that relied on the implicit jQuery global must now explicitly load it as a static resource. _(v36-lwc-001, Spring '16)_
- **[breaking]** Custom Lightning components in Community Builder no longer receive jQuery automatically; components relying on jQuery will break unless you add a manual script reference in the community's head markup. _(v36-lwc-003, Spring '16)_
- **[breaking]** Lightning access attribute violations that previously only logged warnings now throw actual errors and prevent code execution when this critical update is activated. Components referencing resources outside their allowed access scope will fail rather than just warn. _(v37-aura-001, Summer '16)_
- **[breaking]** LockerService enforces strict JavaScript isolation for Lightning components: ES5 strict mode becomes mandatory, components can only access their own DOM elements, global objects are replaced with secure wrappers, and only published framework APIs remain accessible. _(v37-aura-002, Summer '16)_
- **[breaking]** The force:showToast event now requires the message attribute, so existing code firing this event without explicitly setting message will fail. _(v37-aura-008, Summer '16)_
- **[breaking]** Session IDs returned during OAuth 1.0 token exchanges via the UI are now short-lived and restricted to frontdoor.jsp usage only. Previously these session IDs could be used for API calls and had their validity extended. _(v37-auth-003, Summer '16)_
- **[breaking]** LockerService security enforcement becomes mandatory for Lightning components in Communities, blocking inline scripts in page head markup and applying the same security restrictions as the general LockerService critical update. _(v37-lwc-001, Summer '16)_
- **[breaking]** LockerService introduces strict security isolation for Lightning components, blocking access to non-public framework internals and restricting components to supported APIs only. _(v37-lwc-002, Summer '16)_
- **[breaking]** The PUT method on Wave Analytics XMD endpoints has been removed, affecting dataset version metadata updates for main, system, and user XMD resources. _(v37-rest-003, Summer '16)_
- **[breaking]** The SObject Suggested Articles for Case REST resource replaces the categoryid parameter with a new categories parameter that uses a JSON object syntax for specifying data category group/name pairs. _(v37-rest-011, Summer '16)_
- **[breaking]** When converting a lead and assigning the resulting account/contact/opportunity to a different user, the new record is now owned by that target user immediately rather than temporarily belonging to the converting user first. _(v37-sharing-001, Summer '16)_
- **[breaking]** Lightning component access checks are now strictly enforced org-wide. Code referencing resources lacking appropriate access system attributes will fail to execute or return undefined instead of succeeding silently. _(v38-aura-003, Winter '17)_
- **[breaking]** New orgs no longer include the built-in Default Certificate. Code using PageReference.getContent() or getContentAsPDF(), delegated auth, AJAX proxy, or SAML SSO with the default cert must instead reference a self-managed (self-signed or CA-signed) certificate. _(v38-auth-003, Winter '17)_
- **[breaking]** Tooling API access to SecurityHealthCheck and SecurityHealthCheckRisks objects now requires 'View Setup and Configuration' permission, tightening previous access rules. _(v38-rest-006, Winter '17)_
- **[breaking]** Test classes with multiple @testSetup methods now fail to compile. Earlier versions allowed this due to a bug that has been corrected. _(v39-apex-007, Spring '17)_
- **[breaking]** Lightning components now fail to load entirely when referencing events they lack permission to access, whereas previously only client-side checks ran and produced partially working components. _(v39-aura-003, Spring '17)_
- **[breaking]** LockerService now blocks unsafe-inline and unsafe-eval in CSP for script-src, meaning any Lightning component code using eval() or inline JavaScript execution will fail. _(v39-lwc-003, Spring '17)_
- **[breaking]** The originalItemId property on ConnectApi.FeedItemInput is removed; code using it must migrate to capabilities.feedEntityShare.feedEntityId instead. _(v39-rest-004, Spring '17)_
- **[breaking]** The FlexiPage REST API resource was deprecated in v39.0 and simultaneously removed from all prior API versions, breaking any integrations that called this endpoint regardless of which API version they targeted. _(v39-rest-007, Spring '17)_
- **[breaking]** The FlexiPage REST API resource was deprecated at v39.0 and retroactively removed from all earlier API versions, breaking any integration that relied on it regardless of which API version the caller requests. _(v39-rest-010, Spring '17)_
- **[breaking]** The originalFeedItemId property on FeedItemInput is removed; integrations must now use capabilities.feedEntityShare.feedEntityId to share feed entities. _(v39-rest-011, Spring '17)_
- **[breaking]** Enabling Lightning Knowledge permanently removes the 'ArticleType' field from SOQL queries and API access, breaking any custom Apex or integrations that reference this field. _(v39-soql-001, Spring '17)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce reordered URL parameters in Visualforce page URLs, causing action overrides to fail if the retURL parameter value is not properly encoded. _(v39-vf-008, Spring '17)_
- **[breaking]** JavaScript execution within HYPERLINK formula function URLs is blocked platform-wide to close a cross-site scripting vulnerability. Formula fields using javascript: URLs will stop functioning. _(v41-sharing-001, Winter '18)_
- **[breaking]** Lightning components can no longer invoke non-global Apex controller methods from managed packages. Cross-namespace calls now require the Apex method to be marked global, not just public. _(v40-apex-005, Summer '17)_
- **[breaking]** The Databinding.ObjectMapper class and its transform methods have been deleted after deprecation in the prior release, so any Apex code still referencing them will fail to compile or execute. _(v40-apex-013, Summer '17)_
- **[breaking]** Apex controller methods in managed packages that lack the global access modifier become inaccessible to Lightning components outside the package namespace once this critical update activates. _(v40-apex-016, Summer '17)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce will reject TLS 1.0 connections to Communities starting March 2018, requiring all browser access, inbound API calls, and outbound integrations to use TLS 1.1 or higher. _(v40-auth-002, Summer '17)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce now reserves the path prefixes /id/, /idp/, and /saml/ for authentication endpoints. Attempts to save site or community paths using these prefixes will fail with an error. _(v40-auth-005, Summer '17)_
- **[breaking]** Stricter Content Security Policy enforcement removes unsafe-inline and unsafe-eval from script-src, breaking Lightning components that rely on inline scripts or eval-based patterns. _(v40-lwc-002, Summer '17)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce DX beta renames the project configuration file from sfdx-workspace.json to sfdx-project.json, changes CLI command names (e.g., force:workspace:create becomes force:project:create), removes several CLI parameters and commands, and switches JSON property naming to lower camel case. _(v40-packaging-004, Summer '17)_
- **[breaking]** Lightning components outside a managed package namespace can no longer invoke Apex controller methods that lack the global modifier. Previously accessible public methods now throw errors when called across namespace boundaries. _(v40-packaging-005, Summer '17)_
- **[breaking]** The POST method on the Tooling API's runTestsSynchronous endpoint now requires the calling user to have View Setup permission, which was not previously enforced. _(v40-rest-009, Summer '17)_
- **[breaking]** Streaming API now requires CometD client library version 3.0.9 or newer; older CometD versions may exhibit undefined behavior or connection failures. _(v40-rest-015, Summer '17)_
- **[breaking]** The Lightning API has been renamed to User Interface API and its base URL path changed from /lapi to /ui-api, requiring updates to any integration code calling these endpoints. _(v40-rest-018, Summer '17)_
- **[breaking]** The HYPERLINK formula function no longer permits JavaScript in the URL argument, blocking execution to prevent XSS vulnerabilities. _(v40-sharing-001, Summer '17)_
- **[breaking]** The setPassword() SOAP call can no longer be used for users to change their own passwords; code must switch to the new changeOwnPassword() call instead. _(v40-soap-002, Summer '17)_
- **[breaking]** Enabling Lightning Knowledge removes access to the 'ArticleType' field in SOQL queries and API calls, breaking any custom code that references this field. _(v40-soql-002, Summer '17)_
- **[breaking]** Aura components outside a managed package namespace lose access to Apex controller methods not marked as global. Only global methods remain callable across namespace boundaries, enforcing the access controls package authors intended. _(v48-aura-002, Spring '20)_
