Public methods become inaccessible to external consumers, enforcing the access modifier contract the package author intended. _(v50-aura-003, Winter '21; supersedes v47-aura-003)_
- **[breaking]** Aura components outside a managed package namespace can no longer invoke Apex controller methods unless those methods are marked global. Methods marked public become inaccessible across namespace boundaries, causing server action failures for code that relied on this loophole. _(v51-aura-004, Spring '21)_
- **[breaking]** Aura components outside a managed package namespace can no longer invoke Apex controller methods unless those methods are declared global. Public methods in managed packages are now restricted to components within the same namespace. _(v52-aura-002, Summer '21)_
- **[breaking]** Label expressions written as strings in JavaScript (e.g., "{!$Label.c.someLabel}") no longer auto-resolve to label text. Previously undocumented evaluation paths have been removed as a security hardening measure. _(v41-aura-006, Winter '18)_
- **[breaking]** Named credentials now require HTTPS URLs unless the identity type is Anonymous. Existing named credentials using HTTP with non-Anonymous identity types will fail validation. _(v41-auth-004, Winter '18)_
- **[breaking]** Process Builder formulas now enforce that field references must use the same object as the process trigger. Previously invalid cross-object references were silently corrected at runtime, but now they cause errors. _(v41-flow-001, Winter '18)_
- **[breaking]** Two critical updates enforce stricter CSP for Lightning components by removing unsafe-inline and unsafe-eval from script-src, breaking any components that rely on inline scripts or eval(). _(v41-lwc-001, Winter '18)_
- **[breaking]** Einstein Vision API v2.0 now mandates the type parameter when creating datasets; omitting it causes request failures. _(v41-rest-008, Winter '18)_
- **[breaking]** User Interface API graduates to GA at version 41.0, and requests using earlier Developer Preview API versions now fail with HTTP 404. _(v41-rest-012, Winter '18)_

- **[breaking]** The Salesforce CLI bulk upsert command now requires the external ID parameter (-i | --externalid) whereas it was previously optional. _(v42-bulk-001, Spring '18)_
- **[breaking]** Bulk-invoked autolaunched flow interviews now execute all interviews instead of only the first one. Previously, when multiple interviews were triggered in a single bulk operation, all but the initial interview were silently dropped. _(v42-flow-002, Spring '18)_
- **[breaking]** Bulk-invoked autolaunched flow interviews now all execute instead of only the first one running and the rest being silently dropped. This can cause transactions to hit governor limits (e.g., duplicate update limit of 12) that were previously avoided. _(v42-flow-003, Spring '18)_
- **[breaking]** Lightning component controllers without explicit sharing keywords previously defaulted to with sharing; this critical update changes them to without sharing, matching standard Apex behavior but potentially exposing records the user shouldn't access. _(v42-sharing-001, Spring '18)_
- **[breaking]** The UserPermissionsMobileUser field on User has been deleted from the API, causing SOQL queries, reports, or list views referencing it to fail or return unexpected results. _(v48-rest-008, Spring '20)_
- **[breaking]** Lightning container components now enforce that the component's namespace must match the static resource's namespace, and raw iframe elements are blocked unless they include a session-unique confirmation token query parameter. _(v43-aura-006, Summer '18)_
- **[breaking]** Community ID tokens no longer include a trailing slash in the issuer URL when the community lacks a root path prefix, aligning with OpenID Connect Discovery requirements. _(v43-auth-001, Summer '18)_

- **[breaking]** Bulk API now enforces batch size limits on query results when the job's contentType is XML, potentially causing previously oversized batches to fail. _(v43-bulk-002, Summer '18)_
- **[breaking]** The AuraLocalizationService date formatting methods no longer support the uppercase W token for week-of-year. Use lowercase w instead. _(v44-aura-001, Winter '19)_

- **[breaking]** The updated_at claim in UserInfo, identity URL responses, and ID tokens changes from an ISO 8601 string with offset (e.g., 2017-07-28T19:17:41.000+0000) to a JSON number per OpenID Connect Core 1.0. The address claim in ID tokens also switches from a stringified map to a proper nested JSON object. _(v44-auth-006, Winter '19)_

- **[breaking]** Salesforce transitions from JDK8 to ICU locale formatting for dates, times, and numbers. Markup expressions like {!v.apexObject.counter} will fail if the backing Apex property uses a private getter, aligning component behavior with standard Apex access rules. _(v49-lwc-011, Summer '20)_

ExternalSharing is now enabled by default, and ListCustomSettingCreation must be configured via SchemaSettings metadata instead. _(v49-packaging-008, Summer '20)_

- **[breaking]** Guest users now have enforced private org-wide defaults and restricted sharing mechanisms. Apex managed sharing, manual sharing, public groups, and queues can no longer grant record access to guest users—only guest user sharing rules work. _(v49-sharing-001, Summer '20)_

- **[breaking]** The release update disabling $Api.Session_ID resolution in flow interviews is now enforced. Flows that display this variable on screens will no longer show the browser session ID. _(v59-flow-011, Winter '24)_
- **[breaking]** LWC CSS scope tokens switch from readable component-name format (c-cmp_cmp) to obfuscated hash strings (lwc-hashstring). Any code querying or relying on these internal token values will break. _(v59-lwc-010, Winter '24)_
- **[breaking]** Internet Explorer 11 and other legacy browsers can no longer render Lightning Experience or custom Lightning components after Winter '24. Any polyfills or browser-detection code supporting IE11 is now dead code. _(v59-lwc-012, Winter '24)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce enforces enhanced domains org-wide, changing all application and login URLs to include your My Domain name. This affects hardcoded URLs in Apex, Visualforce, API integrations, Experience Cloud sites, and Salesforce Sites. _(v59-other-001, Winter '24)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce no longer persists implicit child share records linking accounts to their opportunity children. SOQL queries and Apex tests that previously retrieved these share records now return empty results. _(v60-sharing-002, Spring '24)_
- **[breaking]** The EmailSimple invocable action now validates organization-wide email address profile settings before sending. Calls from Flow, Apex, or REST API fail with an error if the sender address lacks the required profile configuration. _(v61-flow-004, Summer '24)_
- **[breaking]** Flow execution now requires explicit permission grants via profiles or permission sets. Users without the Run Flows permission or specific flow access can no longer execute flows, and the FlowSites org permission is deprecated. _(v61-flow-005, Summer '24)_
- **[breaking]** Flow execution becomes permission-gated: users must have explicit profile or permission set grants to run flows. The FlowSites org permission that previously allowed universal flow access is deprecated. _(v62-flow-007, Winter '25; supersedes v59-flow-008)_
- **[breaking]** The EmailSimple invocable action now enforces organization-wide email address profile settings. Invocations via Flow, Apex, or REST API will fail if the caller lacks the required profile setting on the org-wide email address. _(v62-flow-013, Winter '25)_
- **[breaking]** Flow execution will require explicit profile or permission set grants; the FlowSites org permission that allowed all users to run any flow is deprecated and will stop working. _(v63-flow-010, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** After enforcement, users can only execute flows if explicitly granted access via profile or permission set. The FlowSites org permission that previously allowed all users to run any flow is deprecated. _(v64-flow-010, Summer '25)_
- **[breaking]** Flows now require explicit profile or permission set grants for users to execute them. The FlowSites org permission that previously allowed any user to run any flow is deprecated and no longer effective. _(v65-flow-002, Winter '26)_
- **[breaking]** The JsonAccess annotation is now validated by the Visualforce JavaScript Remoting API, causing failures for Apex classes that attempt cross-namespace serialization without proper annotation. _(v60-apex-001, Spring '24)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce now validates REST response header names against RFC 7230 when using RestResponse.addHeader(). Headers with non-compliant characters (like forward slashes) throw InvalidHeaderException at runtime. _(v60-apex-007, Spring '24)_
- **[breaking]** Android push notifications for mobile connected apps now require Firebase Admin SDK private key and project ID instead of the previous configuration method, due to changes in Google's push notification handling. _(v60-auth-019, Spring '24)_
- **[breaking]** Autolaunched flows invoked from Apex classes declared with 'with sharing' will enforce sharing rules when running in the default context, rather than bypassing them. _(v60-flow-002, Spring '24)_
- **[breaking]** Flow execution now requires explicit profile or permission set grants. Previously some flows could be executed by any user without permission checks; after enforcement, only users with the Run Flows permission or specific flow access can execute flows. _(v60-flow-005, Spring '24)_
- **[breaking]** Flows will fail at runtime if they invoke legacy Apex actions (classes implementing Process.Plugin) marked as public rather than global. This enforcement ensures managed package access modifiers are respected. _(v60-flow-008, Spring '24)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce replaces JDK locale formats with ICU locale formats org-wide, altering how dates, times, currencies, numbers, addresses, and names render across the platform. Code or integrations parsing or generating formatted locale strings may produce different results. _(v60-other-001, Spring '24)_
- **[breaking]** AppExchange lead Description field now delivers data as JSON instead of plain text, changing the structure ISV partners must parse to extract customer contact preferences and traffic source details. _(v60-other-002, Spring '24)_
- **[breaking]** Legacy *.force.com site URL redirects will stop working in 2024, breaking any hardcoded references to those domains in Aura, LWR, or Visualforce sites. _(v60-other-003, Spring '24)_
- **[breaking]** RestResponse.addHeader() now validates header names against RFC 7230 regardless of the Apex class API version, rejecting headers with invalid characters that were previously accepted. _(v60-rest-002, Spring '24; supersedes v60-rest-004)_
- **[breaking]** REST response headers set via RestResponse.addHeader() are now validated against RFC 7230 regardless of the Apex class API version. Invalid header names will cause failures. _(v60-rest-003, Spring '24; supersedes v60-rest-005)_
- **[breaking]** When an Apex invocable action called via REST API throws an exception, the entire transaction will be rolled back to preserve data integrity, rather than leaving partial changes committed. _(v60-rest-006, Spring '24)_
- **[breaking]** API calls that deserialize XML into Apex classes now require explicit @JsonAccess annotation permission. Without it, requests fail with a 400 XML_PARSER_ERROR response. _(v60-rest-008, Spring '24)_
- **[breaking]** Implicit child share records for opportunities are no longer persisted in the database. Instead, the system evaluates access rights at query time when users attempt to access child opportunity records through account sharing. _(v60-sharing-001, Spring '24)_
- **[breaking]** Autolaunched flows invoked from Apex classes declared with 'with sharing' now inherit those sharing rules instead of running in system context without sharing. Queries may return fewer records and DML may fail due to restricted access. _(v60-sharing-004, Spring '24)_
- **[breaking]** Visualforce JavaScript Remoting now validates the @JsonAccess annotation on Apex classes, blocking unauthorized cross-namespace serialization and deserialization that previously succeeded silently. _(v60-vf-001, Spring '24)_
- **[breaking]** Legacy *.force.com site URL redirects will stop working in September 2024, breaking any hardcoded references to the old domain in code, metadata, or external integrations. _(v61-other-002, Summer '24)_
- **[breaking]** The Commerce product-import endpoint at /commerce/management/webstores/{webstoreId}/product-import is being removed in API version 63.0. Integrations must migrate to the replacement endpoint /commerce/management/import/product/jobs. _(v62-rest-012, Winter '25; supersedes v61-rest-012, v60-rest-012)_
- **[breaking]** Orgs still on the legacy single-configuration SAML framework will lose SSO functionality entirely when Summer '26 enforcement kicks in; migration to the multiple-configuration framework is now mandatory. _(v67-auth-007, Summer '26; supersedes v65-auth-014, v64-auth-007, v63-auth-011, v61-auth-007, v60-auth-005)_
- **[breaking]** Named credentials for Event Relay now reject AWS region values that are not entirely uppercase, causing creation failures for previously accepted mixed-case or lowercase regions like 'us-west-2'. _(v61-auth-003, Summer '24)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce now enforces email verification for all users across all orgs and Experience Cloud sites. Emails sent from unverified addresses are rejected outright, which can break automated email workflows or integrations relying on user accounts with unverified email addresses. _(v61-auth-008, Summer '24)_
- **[breaking]** Concurrent OAuth token requests using the same refresh token now fail instead of being processed in parallel. Only one refresh token request is handled at a time; additional simultaneous requests return a 'Token request is already being processed' error. _(v61-auth-012, Summer '24)_
- **[breaking]** OAuth refresh token rotation begins working correctly on first-party infrastructure instances where it was previously silently broken. Integrations that enabled the setting but never handled rotating tokens will break when Salesforce starts invalidating old tokens as designed. _(v61-auth-014, Summer '24)_
- **[breaking]** Flows will fail at runtime if they invoke a legacy Apex action (Process.Plugin implementation) marked as public rather than global, enforcing access modifier visibility rules that were previously ignored. _(v61-flow-007, Summer '24)_
- **[breaking]** The $Api.Session_ID global variable no longer resolves at flow runtime, returning null instead of the browser session ID. This prevents flows from accessing session tokens that could bypass security controls. _(v61-flow-008, Summer '24)_
- **[breaking]** Flows connected to Conversation Intelligence rules must switch from individual signal-type parameters to a single Apex-defined intelligenceSignals input variable. Existing flows break at enforcement if not updated. _(v61-flow-012, Summer '24)_
- **[breaking]** API calls using instance-specific URLs (e.g., na1.salesforce.com, ap2.salesforce.com) will fail after October 12, 2024. All integrations must switch to My Domain login URLs, which automatically route to the correct instance even after org migrations or instance refreshes. _(v61-rest-002, Summer '24)_
- **[breaking]** The CustomObjectUserLicenseMetrics object has been permanently deleted and is no longer queryable. Any code referencing this object will fail. _(v61-rest-008, Summer '24)_
- **[breaking]** The List Views share-recipients endpoint now requires shareType=RoleAndSubordinatesInternal; the previous value RoleAndInternalSubordinates is no longer accepted and requests using it will fail. _(v61-rest-013, Summer '24)_
- **[breaking]** The /wave/data-conversions REST endpoint and its associated request/response bodies have been removed from the CRM Analytics API. _(v61-rest-014, Summer '24)_
- **[breaking]** Autolaunched flows invoked from Apex classes marked 'with sharing' now inherit and enforce the calling user's sharing rules when running in default context, whereas previously they ran in system context without sharing. _(v61-sharing-002, Summer '24)_
- **[breaking]** Marketing Cloud Engagement now enforces a 180-day retention limit on send and engagement data retrieved via SOAP API, tracking extracts, Email Studio, or Analytics Builder. Data older than 180 days is purged. _(v61-soap-001, Summer '24)_
- **[breaking]** Flows linked to Conversation Intelligence rules must switch from legacy input parameters to a new Apex-defined intelligenceSignals variable for receiving detected signals. After enforcement, flows using the old parameter structure will stop receiving signal data. _(v62-flow-014, Winter '25)_
- **[breaking]** Unmanaged Visualforce pages previously served from salesforce.com are now served exclusively from force.com or site domains. Hard-coded URLs, bookmarks, and external integrations pointing to the old domain will break. _(v62-vf-001, Winter '25; supersedes v61-vf-001)_
- **[breaking]** Flows invoking Apex actions that accept built-in Apex classes with permission requirements will now enforce those permissions and execute within the current component context rather than inheriting the previous context. _(v63-flow-004, Spring '25; supersedes v62-flow-011, v61-flow-011)_
- **[breaking]** Flows tied to Conversation Intelligence rules must now receive intelligence signals through a new Apex-defined input parameter called intelligenceSignals rather than the previous method. _(v63-flow-011, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** Apex classes used as invocable action parameters must have a visible no-argument constructor. Previously implicit default constructors sufficed, but after enforcement any class lacking an explicit public/global parameterless constructor will fail at runtime when used with invocable actions. _(v64-apex-005, Summer '25)_
- **[breaking]** Shared domain certificates for Salesforce CDN are being retired. When enforced, any CDN traffic using shared certificates will fall back to non-HTTPS, breaking secure content delivery. _(v64-other-007, Summer '25)_
- **[breaking]** Apex classes used as invocable action parameters must have an accessible no-argument constructor. Classes lacking this constructor will fail when invoked through flows or other invocable mechanisms. _(v65-apex-002, Winter '26)_
- **[breaking]** Two ConnectApi methods for retrieving CMS delivery channels have been removed: getAllDeliveryChannels in ManagedContent and getManagedContentChannel in ManagedContentDelivery. Code calling these methods will fail at runtime. _(v62-apex-007, Winter '25)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce is overhauling its SAML framework, which may break existing SSO and single-logout integrations including IdP-initiated login, SP-initiated login via connected apps, and org-to-org SAML configurations. _(v62-auth-012, Winter '25)_
- **[breaking]** Flows can no longer resolve the $Api.Session_ID variable at runtime. Screen flows that previously displayed or used the browser session ID will no longer have access to it, breaking any logic that depended on capturing the session ID. _(v62-flow-001, Winter '25)_
- **[breaking]** Flows triggered by bots now run in user context rather than system context, meaning the bot's profile and permission sets determine data access. Flows that previously accessed or modified records beyond the bot user's permissions will fail. _(v62-flow-002, Winter '25)_
- **[breaking]** Flows now enforce access modifiers on legacy Apex actions (classes implementing Process.Plugin). Public legacy Apex actions from managed packages will cause flow execution failures, and only global legacy Apex actions remain accessible cross-namespace. _(v62-flow-009, Winter '25)_
- **[breaking]** The $Api.Session_ID global variable no longer resolves at flow runtime, returning null instead of the browser session ID. This re-enforcement targets orgs where the original Winter '24 enforcement was inadvertently reverted. _(v62-flow-010, Winter '25)_
- **[breaking]** JDK locale formats are being retired and replaced by ICU locale formats for all date, time, currency, address, name, and number formatting across the platform. This affects any code that parses or formats locale-sensitive strings. _(v62-other-001, Winter '25)_
- **[breaking]** The forecastContextFieldName field on AdvAccountForecastSet and canGovCloudUseAdoptionApps field on UserEngagementSettings have been removed from the Metadata API as of v62.0, requiring migration to replacement fields. _(v62-packaging-003, Winter '25)_
- **[breaking]** API calls using instanced URLs (e.g., na1.salesforce.com, ap2.salesforce.com) will stop routing correctly after org migrations or instance refreshes. Starting June 14, 2025, traffic using stale instanced URLs fails entirely. _(v62-rest-002, Winter '25)_
- **[breaking]** The TargetRecordId field on ShippingConfigurationSet can no longer be updated via API; the Update property is now false. _(v62-rest-010, Winter '25)_
- **[breaking]** Starting Spring '25, visit record access will be restricted to the record owner only. Organizations must implement platform-based sharing rules before this enforcement to maintain access for non-owners. _(v62-sharing-002, Winter '25)_
- **[breaking]** Thirteen deprecated Apex classes were removed from the FinServ managed package to resolve ICU Locale Format warnings. Custom permission sets or profiles referencing these classes will fail. _(v63-apex-012, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** The HealthCloudGA managed package dropped deprecated Apex classes and a Visualforce page to comply with ICU locale formats, so any code referencing these removed components will fail. _(v63-apex-013, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** The Triple_Des encryption type for SAML-enabled connected apps is no longer valid. Deployments or configurations using this value will fail. _(v63-auth-001, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** GET requests passing OAuth access tokens via the URL query string are now blocked on the services/oauth2/singleaccess endpoint, requiring tokens to be sent in headers instead. _(v63-auth-002, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce is upgrading its internal SAML framework, which can break existing SSO and single-logout integrations that rely on SAML—including third-party IdP logins, connected-app-based SP flows, and org-to-org federation. _(v63-auth-010, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** The /id/keys endpoint no longer returns public keys for OAuth 2.0 asset token signing certificates. Integrations that fetch public keys via this endpoint must switch to Auth.JWTUtil Apex methods or migrate to a different authorization flow. _(v63-auth-013, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** External client apps using OAuth must now specify an OAuth scope; apps without a scope cannot be saved via Metadata API or App Manager once validation is enforced. _(v63-auth-014, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** Lightning web components now require an explicit apiVersion key in their .js-meta.xml configuration file. Components previously saved without this key will have one auto-added upon retrieval from Salesforce. _(v63-lwc-003, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** LWC's TypeScript tooling now enforces stricter type checking on @wire decorator configuration and properties, and the experimentalDecorators compiler option must be disabled or removed. _(v63-lwc-005, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** LWC now strips leading/trailing whitespace from class and style attribute values and removes empty class/style attributes entirely from the rendered DOM, breaking JavaScript selectors that matched on exact strings containing whitespace. _(v63-lwc-006, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** Financial Account Party records now use the prefix FAP instead of FAR in their record names, which will break any SOQL queries, Apex code, or report filters that reference the old FAR prefix pattern. _(v63-other-012, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** LWR sites upgraded to enhanced LWR sites switch from ExperienceBundle metadata type to DigitalExperienceBundle and DigitalExperienceConfig types, fundamentally changing how the site is deployed and managed. _(v63-packaging-007, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** Nine Apex classes and one Visualforce page were deleted from the HealthCloudGA managed package to comply with ICU locale format requirements. Custom permission sets or profiles referencing these components will break after upgrade. _(v63-packaging-009, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** The AccountContactRelationHistory associated object was documented in Winter '25 but never actually existed; that erroneous documentation has now been removed. _(v63-rest-011, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** The synchronous product import endpoint at /commerce/management/webstores/{webstoreId}/product-import no longer exists in API v63.0; integrations must switch to the asynchronous /commerce/management/import/product/jobs resource. _(v63-rest-017, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** The Custom Domain Connect REST API renamed the CustomUrlList property to CustomUrls in the Custom Domain Custom URL Collection response body, which will break clients parsing the old property name. _(v63-rest-019, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** The PutCartsItems API now enforces data type validation on userValues when updating attributes, throwing an exception if there is a type mismatch such as passing a string to a numeric attribute. _(v63-rest-021, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce is retiring instance-based URL routing for API calls. Any integration hardcoding instance names like na44.salesforce.com in SOAP, REST, or other API endpoints will fail after enforcement dates and must switch to My Domain URLs. _(v63-soap-001, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** The DisclosureDefinitionId field on the Disclosure object has been removed and replaced with DisclosureDefinition due to a field type change from ForeignKey to EnumOrId. _(v63-soql-001, Spring '25)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce is upgrading its internal SAML framework, which may break existing SAML-based SSO and single logout integrations. This affects orgs using SAML for login via external IdPs, connected apps acting as SAML IdPs, inter-org SSO, and single logout flows. _(v64-auth-008, Summer '25)_
- **[breaking]** The 'api' and 'botAction' enum values were removed from the invocationActionType field on BotVersion metadata subtypes starting in API 63.0, breaking deployments that reference these values. _(v64-packaging-008, Summer '25)_
- **[breaking]** The JVM system property that mapped Shift_JIS to Windows-31J is removed, causing Shift_JIS encoding operations to follow strict IANA definitions and potentially produce different byte sequences for characters that were previously Windows-31J aliases. _(v64-apex-009, Summer '25)_
- **[breaking]** Invocable action parameters using Apex classes will require a visible no-argument constructor. Public constructors in managed packages become inaccessible to code outside that package, causing invocable actions referencing them to fail. _(v64-apex-016, Summer '25)_
- **[breaking]** Subscriber-side control over JWT-based access tokens is removed; if a developer enabled JWT tokens in app settings, all installed versions now automatically issue JWT tokens. This breaks integrations using SOAP API, Pub/Sub API, Streaming API, or Salesforce DX since those do not support JWT-based access tokens. _(v64-auth-010, Summer '25)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce will block end users from authorizing or using connected apps that are not installed in the org. Only users with the new 'Approve Uninstalled Connected Apps' permission (or 'Use Any API Client' if API Access Control is enabled) can bypass this restriction. _(v64-auth-011, Summer '25)_
- **[breaking]** OAuth connected apps used with Bring Your Own Channel must have the JWT-based access token setting disabled, otherwise bearer tokens will stop working for Interaction Service API calls. _(v64-auth-013, Summer '25)_
- **[breaking]** Apex classes invoked as Flow invocable actions must now have a public no-argument constructor. Classes relying on constructors with parameters will fail when called from Flows. _(v64-flow-001, Summer '25)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce now enforces stricter access checks when Aura and LWC components reference other components or modules, causing previously working cross-component imports to fail with 'No COMPONENT or MODULE named X found' errors if proper exposure is missing. _(v64-lwc-003, Summer '25)_
- **[breaking]** The platformResourceLoader module no longer permits dynamic imports via import() syntax; only static import declarations are accepted. Components using dynamic imports will fail with a blocking error. _(v64-lwc-009, Summer '25)_
- **[breaking]** The Omnistudio component CPQ-AssetToOrderRequestPayload has been renamed to CPQAssetToOrderRequestPayload (hyphen removed). Deployments or code referencing the old name will fail. _(v64-packaging-010, Summer '25)_
- **[breaking]** When an Apex action in a Flow throws an unhandled exception during a REST API call, the entire transaction now rolls back instead of partially committing. Previously, some DML might persist despite the exception. _(v64-rest-002, Summer '25)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce will stop routing API traffic that uses hardcoded instance URLs (e.g., na1.salesforce.com). All API integrations must switch to the org's My Domain login URL before enforcement. _(v64-rest-003, Summer '25)_
- **[breaking]** Data Cloud Connect REST API responses for Activation Target Output and Activation Output have removed several properties and replaced them with new ones. Properties like dataSpace, activationTargetObjectPath, activationTargetSubject, and curatedEntity-related fields are no longer available and must be accessed via their replacement properties. _(v64-rest-012, Summer '25)_
- **[breaking]** The JVM property that mapped Shift_JIS to Windows-31J is now removed across all orgs, so Apex EncodingUtil, Visualforce CSV exports, and External Services callouts will encode Japanese text according to strict IANA Shift_JIS definitions instead of the Windows-31J superset. _(v65-apex-007, Winter '26)_
- **[breaking]** Invocable action parameters now require their Apex classes to have a visible no-argument constructor. Managed package classes with public no-arg constructors become invisible to code outside the package, causing runtime errors if referenced. _(v65-apex-013, Winter '26)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce is retiring the legacy single-configuration SAML framework; orgs still on it must migrate to the multi-configuration framework or lose SSO functionality entirely. _(v65-auth-003, Winter '26)_
- **[breaking]** OAuth 2.0 client credentials flow now rejects token requests containing only unsupported scopes (web, refresh_token, full) instead of sometimes returning a usable opaque access token. Calls with no valid scopes return an invalid_grant error. _(v65-auth-013, Winter '26)_
- **[breaking]** OmniOut capability is being removed from the Omnistudio Standard Runtime, which will break any implementations relying on OmniOut to render Omnistudio components outside of Salesforce. _(v65-lwc-002, Winter '26)_
- **[breaking]** The enableVoiceInGovCloudOptIn field on ServiceCloudVoiceSettings was removed in API 60.0 and is no longer available. _(v65-packaging-003, Winter '26)_
- **[breaking]** The sfiAdsDataGrid Lightning Web Component in the Media Cloud managed package now requires additional custom labels to be deployed. Upgrading to Winter '26 without deploying these labels will break the component's internationalization support. _(v65-packaging-005, Winter '26)_
- **[breaking]** API requests using hard-coded instance URLs (e.g., na1.salesforce.com) instead of your org's My Domain login URL will be blocked. All integrations must route through the org's My Domain URL. _(v65-rest-006, Winter '26)_
- **[breaking]** ConversationChannelDefinition and CustomMsgChannel objects have new event-driven settings fields replacing old ones. The deprecated fields will be deleted in API 66.0, breaking any integration still referencing them. _(v65-rest-023, Winter '26)_
- **[breaking]** External community users can no longer inherit record access through the old 'Roles and Subordinates' sharing group once digital experiences are active. Code referencing that group name must be updated to use 'Roles and Internal Subordinates' before dynamic conversion ends. _(v65-sharing-001, Winter '26)_
- **[breaking]** The SOAP API login() method is now off by default in newly provisioned orgs and completely unavailable when calling API version 65.0 or higher, regardless of org age. _(v65-soap-002, Winter '26)_
- **[breaking]** API requests using incorrect instanced URLs will be rejected. All traffic must use the org's My Domain login URL or requests will fail. _(v66-rest-005, Spring '26; supersedes v65-rest-004)_
- **[breaking]** Apex classes serving as invocable action parameters must now expose a visible no-argument constructor—public for unpackaged code, global for managed packages called externally. Managed-package classes with merely public constructors become invisible to callers outside the package. _(v66-apex-003, Spring '26)_
- **[breaking]** New connected app creation is now disabled by default across all orgs, meaning automated provisioning or setup scripts that create connected apps will fail unless an admin explicitly enables this capability first. _(v66-auth-001, Spring '26)_
- **[breaking]** mTLS certificates from public CAs in Chrome's trusted root list can no longer serve dual purposes; organizations must migrate to separate PKI hierarchies for server vs. client authentication before Chrome enforces the policy. _(v66-auth-003, Spring '26)_
- **[breaking]** Outbound messages will no longer transmit session IDs. The IncludeSessionId API flag becomes non-functional and the sessionID payload element will be empty. _(v66-auth-010, Spring '26)_
- **[breaking]** AppExchange partner connected apps and external client apps used by more than two production orgs must now enable PKCE and refresh token rotation. Non-compliant apps risk delisting or suspension. _(v66-auth-012, Spring '26)_
- **[breaking]** Partner-distributed Connected Apps and External Client Apps used in more than two production orgs must enable refresh token IP allowlisting and enforce a 30-day idle refresh token expiration, then self-attest to lock these settings permanently. _(v66-auth-013, Spring '26)_
- **[breaking]** Einstein Activity Capture integrations using Microsoft 365 must migrate from Exchange Web Services authentication to Microsoft Graph before October 2026, when Microsoft discontinues EWS entirely. _(v66-auth-016, Spring '26)_
- **[breaking]** New connected app creation is now blocked by default in all orgs; developers must contact Salesforce Support to enable it or migrate to external client apps for new integrations. _(v66-auth-018, Spring '26)_
- **[breaking]** SAML SSO configurations using Triple DES encryption will cease to function entirely in Summer '26. Any integration relying on Triple DES for SAML assertion encryption—whether Salesforce acts as IdP or SP—must migrate to AES-128 or AES-256 before the release. _(v66-auth-023, Spring '26)_
- **[breaking]** Named credentials bundled in managed packages become immutable by default—subscribers can no longer modify them post-install, and any programmatic endpoint change via Apex or Metadata API automatically disables callouts until an admin re-enables them. _(v66-auth-028, Spring '26)_
- **[breaking]** Temporary redirects from legacy Salesforce hostnames to enhanced domains are removed; any integrations or bookmarks still using old hostnames will fail outright instead of being redirected. _(v66-other-006, Spring '26)_
- **[breaking]** Tableau Semantics numeric functions (ASIN, ACOS, LOG, LN, COT, POWER) now throw query errors on invalid input instead of returning null, and regex functions migrate from ICU to RE2 engine—breaking backreferences, lookahead/lookbehind, and possessive quantifiers while also changing empty-string match behavior. _(v66-other-007, Spring '26)_
- **[breaking]** Automatic redirects from legacy force.com site URLs cease entirely in this release. Any integration, external link, or internal reference still pointing to the old URL format will fail rather than redirect. _(v66-other-009, Spring '26)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce now enforces per-zip and 24-hour rate limits on deploying and retrieving AIAuthoringBundle, AnalyticsDashboard, AnalyticsWorkspace, and AnalyticsVisualization metadata types, which may cause previously successful CI/CD pipelines to fail. _(v66-packaging-003, Spring '26)_
- **[breaking]** The enableDevOpsCenter field has been deleted from DevHubSettings metadata. Deployments or scripts referencing this field will fail. _(v66-packaging-006, Spring '26)_
- **[breaking]** The Connect API Performance Beta setting has been removed. Code that relied on this beta performance optimization may experience different behavior or errors. _(v66-rest-001, Spring '26, low confidence)_
- **[breaking]** Legacy and instanced host names in API calls will no longer redirect; requests to these endpoints will fail outright, requiring updates to hardcoded URLs. _(v66-rest-004, Spring '26)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce will block API requests using hard-coded instanced URLs that don't match the org's actual instance; all API traffic must use the org's My Domain login URL instead. _(v66-rest-011, Spring '26)_
- **[breaking]** Reading the RedirectWhitelistUrl object now requires the Customize Application permission, whereas previously that permission was only needed for editing. Integrations or tools that query this object without the permission will start failing. _(v66-rest-016, Spring '26; supersedes v66-rest-021)_
- **[breaking]** Event-driven settings fields in ConversationChannelDefinition and CustomMsgChannel metadata objects are removed in API 66.0; integrations must migrate to the replacement fields introduced in API 65.0. _(v66-rest-033, Spring '26)_
- **[breaking]** Sharing recalculations after group or role membership changes will run asynchronously rather than immediately, potentially breaking Apex or Flows that assume share records exist right after the membership update. _(v66-sharing-002, Spring '26)_
- **[breaking]** Sharing recalculations following group or role membership changes now execute asynchronously for performance reasons. Apex and Flows that expect share records to exist immediately after modifying groups or roles will fail once enforcement begins. _(v66-sharing-003, Spring '26)_
- **[breaking]** Apex classes used as parameters in invocable actions must now have a no-argument constructor. Classes lacking one will fail when this release update is enforced. _(v67-apex-001, Summer '26)_
- **[breaking]** Managed packages will no longer be able to retrieve a session ID via UserInfo.getSessionId() and use it to run anonymous Apex in subscriber orgs. Any package relying on this pattern for dynamic code execution will break. _(v67-apex-004, Summer '26)_
- **[breaking]** Managed packages can no longer call executeAnonymous via session IDs obtained from UserInfo.getSessionId(). Packages with namespaces created in Summer '26 or later are blocked immediately; existing packages will be blocked org-wide when enforcement begins in Summer '27. _(v67-apex-013, Summer '26)_
- **[breaking]** Aura action responses for custom objects will stop including internal system fields that lack public API support, causing components that reference those fields to break with missing data or JS errors. _(v67-aura-003, Summer '26)_
- **[breaking]** Publicly trusted certificates used for mTLS client authentication must be migrated to dedicated PKI hierarchies separate from TLS server certificates, due to Google Chrome Root Program Policy v1.7 prohibiting dual-use certificates from Chrome-trusted CAs. _(v67-auth-006, Summer '26)_
- **[breaking]** AgentExchange partner apps using Connected Apps or External Client Apps must now enable PKCE and Refresh Token Rotation. Non-compliant apps risk de-listing or suspension of Salesforce interoperability. _(v67-auth-012, Summer '26)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce retires the legacy single-configuration SAML SSO framework. Orgs still on this framework must migrate to the multiple-configuration SAML framework or SSO will cease to function entirely. _(v67-auth-015, Summer '26)_
- **[breaking]** Triple DES encryption for SAML SSO has been removed entirely. Orgs still configured with Triple DES will experience SSO login failures for all affected users. _(v67-auth-016, Summer '26)_
- **[breaking]** External auth identity provider callback URLs now incorporate the org's My Domain instead of the generic login.salesforce.com hostname, requiring updates to allowlists and redirect URI configurations in external identity providers. _(v67-auth-020, Summer '26)_
- **[breaking]** API calls using legacy instanced URLs instead of the org's My Domain login URL will be rejected. Traffic must route through the correct My Domain endpoint. _(v67-rest-005, Summer '26)_
- **[breaking]** Salesforce will reject API requests using hard-coded instance URLs (e.g., na1.salesforce.com) and require the org's My Domain login URL instead. This release update was postponed from Spring '26 to Winter '27. _(v67-rest-010, Summer '26)_
- **[breaking]** Sharing recalculations triggered by group or role membership changes now execute asynchronously for performance reasons, which can break Apex and Flows that expect share records to exist immediately after the membership update. _(v67-sharing-005, Summer '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** The per-transaction code statement limit is removed and replaced with CPU time limits: 10 seconds for synchronous Apex and 60 seconds for asynchronous Apex. Exceeding CPU time throws an unhandleable LimitException. _(v29-apex-004, Winter '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** Scheduled Apex jobs created before Summer '13 are migrated to a new scheduling infrastructure, causing the CronTrigger.PreviousFireTime field to reset to null until the job runs again. _(v29-apex-005, Winter '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Messaging.reserveMassEmailCapacity and Messaging.reserveSingleEmailCapacity methods now throw System.HandledException instead of LimitException when the org's daily email quota would be exceeded. _(v29-apex-011, Winter '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** DML operations on User records now return different StatusCode values in their exceptions, which may break code that catches and inspects specific status codes. _(v29-apex-012, Winter '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce as a SAML Identity Provider now signs each assertion individually using the same certificate that signs the overall SAML response, whereas previously assertions relied solely on the parent response signature. _(v29-auth-001, Winter '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce apps are now delivered as connected apps bundled into managed packages that install automatically when any user triggers OAuth approval or a refresh token flow for any app in the package. _(v29-auth-002, Winter '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** SAML service providers can no longer be created from the Identity Provider page; they must now be configured as connected apps with SAML enabled via Setup > Create > Apps. _(v29-auth-003, Winter '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** Canvas apps no longer require users to have the 'API Enabled' permission to run. Previously blocked users can now execute installed canvas apps without this permission being granted. _(v29-auth-007, Winter '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** Force.com Sites sandbox URLs now use a hyphen instead of a period between the sandbox name and subdomain, changing the format to [sandboxName]-[subdomain].[instance].force.com. _(v29-other-001, Winter '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Metadata API deployment workflow changed from polling AsyncResult to using checkDeployStatus() with a new DeployResult object that provides detailed real-time status, error messages, and test progress. _(v29-soap-005, Winter '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** A bug fix now preserves the SOQL WHERE clause when calling save() on a StandardSetController that was initialized with a queryLocator. Previously the WHERE condition was silently dropped. _(v29-vf-014, Winter '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** The deprecated Limits.getScriptStatements() method no longer returns actual statement counts; it now returns an approximation derived from CPU time consumption relative to the CPU timeout limit. _(v30-apex-010, Spring '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** OAuth token responses now include the token_type field set to "Bearer", which may affect integrations that parse the response structure strictly. _(v30-auth-001, Spring '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** Several session security settings are now enabled by default for all organizations and can no longer be disabled from the Session Settings page: HTTPS required, SMS identity confirmation, clickjack protection, and CSRF protection on non-setup pages. _(v30-auth-002, Spring '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** Sandbox refreshes now rewrite all user email addresses to an @example.com domain, which the Salesforce MTA silently discards. Code or integrations that rely on sandbox-originated emails reaching real inboxes will stop working. _(v30-other-004, Spring '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** The UserRecordAccess object can now be queried as a foreign key lookup on records, enabling inline access checks like `SELECT Id, UserRecordAccess.HasReadAccess FROM Account` without filtering by UserId or RecordId. _(v30-soap-002, Spring '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** Geolocation compound fields with partial null values (one of latitude/longitude null but not both) now return null in SOQL SELECT and are excluded from DISTANCE() and ORDER BY calculations, whereas querying individual component fields still returns the actual stored values. _(v30-soql-001, Spring '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** Connected Apps experience modified API access controls, potentially affecting how OAuth-based integrations authenticate and what data they can reach. _(v31-auth-001, Summer '14, low confidence)_
- **[behavior-change]** Cross-domain session exchanges now use POST requests instead of GET, which may affect custom integrations that intercept or rely on the previous GET-based exchange mechanism. _(v31-auth-002, Summer '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** An OAuth access token can now retrieve identity URLs for multiple users within the same org, provided the token was obtained with 'full' or 'api' scope and belongs to a user with 'API Enabled' permission. _(v31-auth-007, Summer '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** Sandbox creation and refresh now automatically copies connected apps installed via packages, but org-created connected apps still require manual recreation after sandbox copy or refresh. _(v31-auth-010, Summer '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** Trigger-ready flows now support Apex Plug-in elements but no longer permit choice or dynamic choice resources; flows containing these resources lose their trigger-ready status. _(v31-flow-001, Summer '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Force.com Migration Tool now honors the rollbackOnError setting in build.xml instead of always defaulting to true, meaning deployments to non-production orgs can now proceed partially if you explicitly set it to false. _(v31-packaging-001, Summer '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** When a Chatter REST API request includes both URL query parameters and a JSON request body, resource-specific query parameters are silently discarded and only the body is processed. _(v31-rest-007, Summer '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** Tooling API's ContainerAsyncRequest object replaces the CompilerErrors field with a new DeployDetails field that provides richer error information including line numbers and component names. _(v31-rest-008, Summer '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** AccountTerritoryAssignmentRuleItem records can now be created or deleted via the API when the parent rule's BooleanFilter is null, removing a previous restriction that affected all API versions. _(v31-soap-002, Summer '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** SOQL queries against ProcessInstance, ProcessInstanceNode, ProcessInstanceStep, and ProcessInstanceWorkitem return incomplete data for historical approval records: fields like CompletedDate, LastActorId, and elapsed time values may be null depending on when the approval was completed relative to the Summer '14 rollout. _(v31-soql-001, Summer '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** Visualforce now generates and manages session IDs differently to handle cross-server transitions more reliably. Custom integrations that parse or depend on specific session ID values may break. _(v31-vf-009, Summer '14)_
- **[behavior-change]** A critical update fixes how screen fields in loops obtain their initial value: after activation, each loop iteration uses the configured default rather than the value entered in a prior iteration. _(v32-flow-001, Winter '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** Flow screens in loops now reset to their defined default values on each iteration instead of retaining the previously entered value from earlier visits to that screen. _(v32-flow-002, Winter '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** Flow creators now receive a separate fault notification email for every unhandled interview error, rather than only the first occurrence when multiple faults share similar messages. _(v32-flow-003, Winter '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** The triggerUserEmail API field now respects per-user notification preferences when the org setting is enabled, meaning API-created task assignments may no longer send emails to users who have opted out, even when triggerUserEmail=true. _(v32-rest-001, Winter '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** The DandBCompany object transitions from read-only to fully CRUD-enabled, allowing create, update, and delete operations. Organizations with Data.com automated Clean enabled may see manual changes overwritten during sync cycles. _(v32-rest-012, Winter '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** When unlisted groups are enabled, Apex and Visualforce code running in system mode bypasses unlisted group visibility controls, potentially exposing these groups to non-members through custom pages or AppExchange apps. _(v32-sharing-002, Winter '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** Apex collections without guaranteed ordering (Sets and Map key iteration) now follow a consistent, predictable iteration sequence. Code relying on arbitrary iteration behavior may see different results. _(v33-apex-001, Spring '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** Batch job submission now routes jobs through a flex queue with a new 'Holding' status before they reach 'Queued'. This affects SOQL queries against AsyncApexJob that filter on Status values. _(v33-apex-008, Spring '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** The escapeHtml3 and escapeHtml4 methods now escape single quotes, and escapeEcmaScript now escapes angle brackets (< and >), which may alter output strings that previously passed these characters through unmodified. _(v33-apex-013, Spring '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** Bug fixes to code coverage calculation may cause reported percentages to differ from previous runs even without code changes. Manually deleted rows in ApexCodeCoverageAggregate are now recreated when tests execute, and other calculation bugs were corrected. _(v33-apex-014, Spring '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** Activating this critical update makes Map and Set iteration order deterministic and repeatable across executions, but the new fixed order may differ from the previous arbitrary order. _(v33-apex-015, Spring '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** The OAuth 2.0 username-password flow now returns a unified error response of 'invalid_grant — authentication failure' for all credential failures, replacing the previous specific error codes that distinguished between bad passwords, expired tokens, and invalid users. _(v33-auth-010, Spring '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** The critical update enforcing governor limits on all executed flows has its activation date changed, affecting when flows become subject to standard execution limits. _(v33-flow-001, Spring '15, low confidence)_
- **[behavior-change]** SharingRules metadata type restructured to use child subtypes (SharingCriteriaRule, SharingOwnerRule, SharingTerritoryRule) with wildcard retrieval support, while the legacy per-object sharing rule types (AccountSharingRules, CampaignSharingRules, etc.) are removed. _(v33-packaging-005, Spring '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** Chatter REST API response bodies now use different enum string values for the method property on Action Link Definition (e.g., 'Delete' becomes 'HttpDelete') and the status property on Platform Action (e.g., 'Failed' becomes 'FailedStatus'). The Platform Action type value 'AnchorAction' is renamed to 'ProductivityAction'. _(v33-rest-008, Spring '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** SOSL search infrastructure switches from bigram to morphological tokenization, significantly altering how East Asian (CJKT) text is matched. Queries that previously matched substrings within compound words now require exact morphological boundaries. _(v33-soql-002, Spring '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** PageReference getContent() and getContentAsPDF() methods are now treated as callouts, meaning they count against callout limits and cannot be invoked in contexts where callouts are prohibited. _(v34-apex-003, Summer '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** Case emails are now visible to external community users by default when they have case access. Developers can control this visibility by writing an Apex trigger on EmailMessage to set the IsExternallyVisible field to false. _(v34-apex-006, Summer '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** Apex code coverage now counts each line of a multiline statement separately rather than treating the entire statement as one line, which can raise or lower reported coverage percentages depending on which lines execute. _(v34-apex-013, Summer '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** Map and Set iteration now yields a consistent, repeatable element order across executions, whereas previously the order was arbitrary and could vary between runs. _(v34-apex-014, Summer '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** The SymbolTable in Tooling API now returns all relevant modifiers including implicit ones (e.g., global for webservice methods, private by default). The visibility field that incorrectly combined PROTECTED with PRIVATE has been removed. _(v34-apex-015, Summer '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce HTTPS callouts from Apex, workflow outbound messaging, and delegated authentication now attempt TLS 1.2, TLS 1.1, and SNI during negotiation. Endpoints that cannot handle these newer protocols may fail to connect even though TLS 1.0 remains supported. _(v34-apex-016, Summer '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** PageReference.getContent() and getContentAsPDF() now count as callouts, affecting transaction limits and requiring callout permissions; they also change how the calling page's transaction state is handled. _(v34-apex-017, Summer '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** The platform now validates more dependency references in Lightning components at save time, including explicit <aura:dependency> tags, inheritance hierarchies, and custom field references. Previously allowed saves may now fail with compilation errors if they break referential integrity. _(v34-aura-005, Summer '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** Change Sets now use the FlowDefinition metadata type instead of the legacy Flow component for deploying flows, requiring updates to any scripts or tooling that reference the old component name. _(v34-packaging-001, Summer '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** The runAllTests boolean option in DeployOptions has been removed and replaced by the testLevel field, which provides finer control over which tests execute during deployment. _(v34-packaging-005, Summer '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** When the critical update is enabled, PageReference.getContent() and PageReference.getContentAsPDF() are treated as callouts. This means they count against callout limits and follow callout transaction semantics. _(v34-vf-013, Summer '15)_
- **[behavior-change]** The PageReference getContent() and getContentAsPDF() methods will be treated as callouts once this critical update is enforced, meaning they count against callout limits and cannot be invoked after DML in the same transaction. _(v37-vf-009, Summer '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** The critical update treating PageReference.getContent() and getContentAsPDF() as callouts has been delayed from Winter '16 to Spring '16, giving more time to refactor code that calls these methods from contexts prohibiting callouts. _(v35-apex-019, Winter '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Lightning framework now sends multiple XHR requests concurrently instead of serializing them one at a time, which may affect code that assumed sequential request ordering. _(v35-aura-002, Winter '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** The JavaScript methods for managing field-level errors on Aura input components have been replaced; cmp.addErrors, cmp.getErrors, cmp.clearErrors, cmp.setValid, and cmp.isValid are superseded by direct attribute access via cmp.set/get on v.errors. _(v35-aura-003, Winter '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Aura framework now logs console warnings when code accesses components, attributes, or events that lack the required access system attribute. These warnings signal upcoming stricter enforcement that will block such access entirely in a future release. _(v35-aura-005, Winter '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** Session IDs obtained via $Api.Session_ID or GETSESSIONID() in Lightning Experience carry restricted privileges similar to the Lightning session itself, preventing their use for API calls. _(v35-auth-002, Winter '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** The OAuth UserInfo endpoint now functions correctly within Communities contexts, whereas previously it returned a No_Site_Endpoint error after successful OAuth authentication. _(v35-auth-003, Winter '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** OAuth authorization flows cannot be completed while an admin is logged in as another user. Any integration code that relied on approving OAuth grants during a Login-As session will now be blocked. _(v35-auth-004, Winter '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce now uses Twitter's oauth/authenticate endpoint instead of oauth/authorize, eliminating repeated authorization prompts but restricting the returned access token from accessing Twitter direct messages. _(v35-auth-005, Winter '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** Auth provider SSO errors now render error codes and descriptions directly on the page, not just in the URL. Developers can throw custom exceptions from createUser/updateUser methods in Auth.RegistrationHandler to display tailored error messages to users. _(v35-auth-006, Winter '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** Flows now bulkify their SOQL queries internally, reducing the likelihood of hitting governor limits when processing multiple records in a single transaction. _(v35-flow-001, Winter '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** Custom metadata records can now be marked as protected within managed packages, restricting read access so that only Apex code within the same package (or the package defining the type) can query them. _(v35-packaging-001, Winter '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** Request and response bodies for the Reports and Dashboards REST API were modified, which may affect existing integrations parsing these responses. _(v35-rest-003, Winter '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** The User object fields AboutMe, FullPhotoURL, and SmallPhotoURL no longer depend on Chatter being enabled, allowing photo operations without Chatter across all API versions. _(v35-rest-006, Winter '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** Tooling API queries that retrieve Metadata or FullName fields are now limited to returning a single record per request. _(v35-rest-012, Winter '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** SOQL queries on Boolean fields now distinguish between null and false values, so null checks no longer inadvertently return records with checkbox fields set to false. _(v35-soql-001, Winter '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** Social Customer Service moderation now uses new ReviewedStatus picklist values ('Needed' and 'Reviewed'). Orgs with custom Apex classes that don't extend the default must manually update their code to set the reviewedStatus field and adjust list filters. _(v36-apex-002, Spring '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** Test.startTest() and Test.stopTest() now consistently reset all governor limits including SOQL query counts within the enclosed block, fixing prior inconsistent behavior where some limits like SOQL queries did not always reset. _(v36-apex-008, Spring '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** The @future method workaround for MIXED_DML_OPERATION errors now functions correctly within Apex test contexts. Previously, using @future to separate setup and non-setup sObject DML still threw errors during test execution; this bug has been resolved. _(v36-apex-009, Spring '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** The PageReference getContent() and getContentAsPDF() methods now count as callouts, meaning they are subject to callout limits and cannot be invoked after DML in the same transaction context. _(v36-apex-020, Spring '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Lightning Component framework will strictly enforce access system attribute checks starting Summer '16. Components currently triggering browser console warnings for accessing resources without proper access attributes will fail at runtime once enforcement begins. _(v36-aura-001, Spring '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning components can now pass List and Map objects as parameters to server-side Apex controller methods without triggering UnsupportedOperationException errors that occurred in earlier releases. _(v36-aura-005, Spring '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** Analytics API and SOAP API calls now fail with an error when attempting to access resources protected by a high-assurance session policy from a standard-assurance session. _(v36-auth-005, Spring '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce introduces org-specific API client certificates as a replacement for the older proxy.salesforce.com certificate, affecting workflow outbound messages, AJAX proxy, certain Apex PageReference methods, and delegated authentication callouts to endpoints using Microsoft Trusted Root Certificate Program. _(v36-auth-007, Spring '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** Force.com Migration Tool v36.0 automatically enables TLS 1.1 and 1.2 when running on Java 7+, and Salesforce has announced plans to discontinue TLS 1.0 support entirely. _(v36-packaging-002, Spring '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** User.UITheme, User.UIThemeDisplayed, UserInfo.getUiTheme(), and UserInfo.getUiThemeDisplayed() now return two new values: Theme4d for Lightning Experience and Theme4t for Salesforce1 mobile, in addition to the existing theme identifiers. _(v36-vf-001, Spring '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** Static resources will be served from the Visualforce domain instead of the core Salesforce domain, which may break hardcoded URL references or cross-origin requests that assume the old domain. _(v36-vf-002, Spring '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** DML operations such as insert, update, and delete cannot be performed within Apex code executed by Transaction Security policies. _(v37-apex-001, Summer '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** Programmatic approval submissions now validate that the submitter is in the allowed submitters list, matching the behavior of manual submissions. Code, flows, or processes that submit records for approval may route to a different approval process or fail if the submitter lacks permission. _(v37-apex-003, Summer '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** The TxnSecurity.Event data map gains ActionName and UserName for Entity events but loses Browser, Platform, TimeStamp, URI, and UserAgent across all event types, breaking code that reads those removed keys. _(v37-apex-008, Summer '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** ApexTestResult objects are now fully writable via Tooling API, allowing programmatic creation, update, and deletion of test result records along with all their fields. _(v37-apex-010, Summer '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** Abortable server actions are now aborted when their originating component becomes invalid (cmp.isValid() == false), replacing the previous behavior where an abortable action was aborted when another abortable action was queued. _(v37-aura-005, Summer '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** The force:showToast event gains new attributes enabling multiple actions per toast and stacking behavior, but force:hideToast no longer functions with the enhanced toast system. _(v37-aura-006, Summer '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** Percent field handling in Flow sObject variables is corrected: values passed between sObject percent fields no longer get unexpectedly transformed, but formula references now divide by 100. Existing workarounds that multiplied values to compensate for the old bug must be removed. _(v37-flow-001, Summer '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** The SignupRequest SOAP API object's Edition field no longer accepts 'Group Edition' and renames existing values; code that programmatically provisions trial orgs must update hardcoded edition strings. _(v37-soap-005, Summer '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** External objects now have an Allow Search toggle controlling SOSL and global search inclusion. Existing external objects get search enabled by default upon Summer '16 rollout, but new external objects default to search disabled. _(v37-soql-002, Summer '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce Connect OData adapters now preserve hyphens in SOSL and Salesforce search query strings sent to external systems, instead of stripping all ASCII punctuation beforehand. _(v37-soql-003, Summer '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** SOQL queries on the PlatformAction object now accept a LIMIT clause in Apex, whereas previously they were rejected. This is a bug fix enabling previously blocked query patterns. _(v37-soql-004, Summer '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** The threshold for non-selective SOQL queries in triggers doubled from 100,000 to 200,000 rows, meaning triggers that previously failed with a selectivity error on large objects may now succeed. _(v37-soql-005, Summer '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** The PageReference getContent() and getContentAsPDF() methods now behave as callouts, meaning they count against callout limits and cannot be used in contexts where callouts are prohibited. Auto-activation was postponed to Winter '17. _(v37-vf-001, Summer '16)_
- **[behavior-change]** Transaction Security policies now enforce resource metering that can block access if policy evaluation consumes too many resources. Static local variables in policy Apex code are no longer supported. _(v38-apex-002, Winter '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** The LockerService security architecture critical update, originally scheduled for automatic activation in Winter '17, has been delayed until Summer '17, giving developers more time to ensure their Lightning components are compatible. _(v38-aura-004, Winter '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** Events fired from components created via $A.createComponent() now bubble through the containment hierarchy identically to events from markup-declared components, fixing a prior inconsistency. _(v38-aura-007, Winter '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** The force:inputField and force:outputField components now enforce access checks, meaning they will respect field-level security when access checks are enabled in the org. _(v38-aura-011, Winter '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** LockerService enforcement for Lightning components can now be toggled by all orgs via the Critical Update settings, and a new checkbox controls whether managed package components are subject to LockerService restrictions separately from org-created components. _(v38-lwc-002, Winter '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** The CustomApplication metadata object now requires regeneration of WSDLs created before Winter '17 due to the addition of the uiType field. _(v38-packaging-001, Winter '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** The ApexTestRunResult object gains three new fields (MethodsCompleted, MethodsEnqueued, MethodsFailed) that provide real-time progress tracking during test runs, which may affect integrations polling for test status. _(v38-rest-007, Winter '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** SOQL queries against custom metadata type relationship fields now enforce object-level permissions, returning only records referencing accessible objects, whereas Metadata API and Setup queries return all records regardless of permissions. _(v38-soql-001, Winter '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** SOQL queries traversing foreign key relationships now return actual name field values even when the querying user lacks access to the referenced object, whereas previously these returned null. _(v38-soql-002, Winter '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** SOSL WITH SNIPPET now works on additional objects (Case, CaseComment, FeedItem, FeedComment, Idea, IdeaComment) and the HTML tag wrapping matched terms changed from <em> to <mark>. _(v38-soql-003, Winter '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** SOQL queries on custom metadata types that include long text area fields now count against Apex governor limits, whereas previously they may have been exempt from certain limit calculations. _(v39-apex-010, Spring '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** Trace flags on the same entity can no longer have overlapping active time windows, even when one window is fully nested inside another. Previously nested windows were permitted. _(v39-apex-011, Spring '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** Custom authentication providers now require the AuthProviderPluginClass abstract class instead of the AuthProviderPlugin interface for new implementations or to access new capabilities like custom error handling and refresh token support via named credentials. _(v39-auth-002, Spring '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** Activating the LockerService critical update disables the ui:inputRichText and forceChatter:feed components in Lightning Experience, Salesforce1, and standalone apps. Developers must migrate to the LockerService-compliant lightning:inputRichText component. _(v39-lwc-001, Spring '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** LockerService enforces namespace isolation and restricts Lightning components to supported APIs only, blocking access to internal framework methods and DOM outside the component's namespace. _(v39-lwc-002, Spring '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Open CTI onNavigationChange method exhibits different behavior when invoked within Lightning console apps compared to standard Lightning apps. _(v39-other-001, Spring '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** Picklist value labels and API names are now independent; changing a label no longer alters the API name used by Apex, integrations, and data operations. _(v39-packaging-001, Spring '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** Push upgrades that add or modify RemoteSiteSetting records now deploy them as inactive, requiring subscriber admins to manually activate. Previously these were auto-activated, so packages relying on immediate remote site availability after push upgrade will break. _(v39-packaging-004, Spring '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** The ltng:allowGuestAccess interface enables Lightning Out apps to be served to unauthenticated users, but bypasses object-level and field-level security checks configured on the guest user profile—developers must manually enforce CRUD and FLS in Apex controllers or risk exposing org data publicly. _(v39-sharing-001, Spring '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** Modifying any Apex class now invalidates the entire platform cache, clearing cached data across all partitions. _(v40-apex-002, Summer '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** When processes, workflow rules, or Apex triggers update a record that also triggered an email notification (task assignment, case owner change, user welcome, etc.), Salesforce previously suppressed those emails. Activating this Critical Update restores the emails, which may cause duplicates if you added workaround notifications. _(v40-apex-004, Summer '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** Editing, deploying, or upgrading an Apex class now invalidates Platform Cache entries, potentially causing cache misses where previously cached data would have been returned. _(v40-apex-007, Summer '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** Automated field updates from processes, workflow rules, and Apex triggers no longer suppress system-generated email notifications (such as task assignment emails) once this critical update is enabled. _(v40-apex-017, Summer '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** Calling cmp.get() on an invalid Aura component now returns null instead of throwing an InvalidComponent error, and cmp.set() on an invalid component silently does nothing. _(v40-aura-006, Summer '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** Connected apps using SAML with OAuth single sign-on now support IP relaxation, matching the existing OAuth-only behavior. Additionally, refresh token exchanges can bypass IP restrictions, allowing users to continue sessions from outside restricted networks after initial authentication. _(v40-auth-006, Summer '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** LockerService no longer blocks the instanceof operator in JavaScript except for array checks, where Array.isArray() must still be used because Proxy objects do not support instanceof with native arrays. _(v40-lwc-003, Summer '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Open CTI saveLog method no longer auto-refreshes records after creation or update; callers must now explicitly invoke refreshView within the callback to see updated data. _(v40-rest-021, Summer '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** External object records returned by SOSL or global searches will receive temporary Salesforce IDs instead of permanent ones, breaking any code that stores or relies on these IDs persisting across queries. _(v40-soql-001, Summer '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** SOQL queries against Knowledge Article Version (KAV) objects no longer require explicit language and publishStatus filters; omitted filters now default to the current user's language and 'online' status. _(v40-soql-003, Summer '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** External object records returned by SOSL and Salesforce searches will receive temporary Salesforce IDs instead of permanent ones, meaning the same external data row may have different record IDs across queries. _(v40-soql-005, Summer '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** JavaScript remoting calls to Apex remote actions now roll back all DML when the method throws an exception, whereas previously the transaction committed despite the error. _(v40-vf-003, Summer '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Design System CSS class naming switched from double-dash BEM notation (.slds-block--modifier) to single-underscore notation (.slds-block_modifier); the old syntax remains supported for 18 months before removal. _(v40-vf-006, Summer '17)_
- **[behavior-change]** When enabled, field updates made by processes, workflow rules, or Apex triggers no longer suppress automatic email notifications (such as task assignment or case owner change emails) that were triggered by the same transaction. _(v50-flow-007, Winter '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** A planned change to recompile all Apex code during deployments was removed from this release and not rolled out to all orgs. _(v41-apex-001, Winter '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Synchronous Apex test execution via the Tooling API (including Developer Console single-class runs and /runTestsSynchronous/) no longer triggers case assignment rules, fixing a prior bug where assignment rules fired unexpectedly during tests. _(v41-apex-003, Winter '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** The default TTL for Cache.Org.put() methods that omit an explicit lifetime parameter increases from 12 hours to 24 hours, correcting a documentation mismatch. _(v41-apex-005, Winter '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** The lightning:container component's CSP attribute values changed from 'minimum/Lightning/custom' (default Lightning) to 'low/high/custom' (default low), altering how iframed third-party content is sandboxed. _(v41-aura-007, Winter '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** The email_verified claim returned by the UserInfo endpoint and identity URL now indicates whether the user actually clicked a verification link in a confirmation email, rather than just reflecting whether the org has email verification turned on. _(v41-auth-001, Winter '18; supersedes v41-auth-006)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce's default Facebook authentication provider now retrieves additional user profile fields (email, first name, last name, locale, profile link) instead of just the user ID and full name. Custom Facebook auth providers must update their userinfo endpoint URL to include these fields. _(v41-auth-005, Winter '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Orgs without My Domain enabled can now save Lightning pages containing custom components via Tooling API and Metadata API, and can install or upgrade packages with such pages. Previously these operations were blocked. _(v41-packaging-002, Winter '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Change set deployments and managed package upgrades now preserve existing platform cache allocations in the target org instead of resetting them to zero. _(v41-packaging-008, Winter '18; supersedes v41-packaging-010)_
- **[behavior-change]** Platform cache partition allocations now persist their configured values during change set deployments, metadata deploys, and managed package upgrades instead of being reset to zero. _(v41-packaging-009, Winter '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** ISVs can now remove S-Controls from managed-released packages in new versions, and subscribers gain the ability to delete them from their org. _(v41-packaging-011, Winter '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** The CLIENT_IP field in Event Monitoring log files changed from an IP data type to a String, and Salesforce internal IPs now appear as the literal value 'Salesforce.com IP' rather than actual addresses. _(v41-rest-003, Winter '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Tooling API now permits CRUD operations on most objects in active (production) orgs, matching behavior previously available only in sandboxes and scratch orgs. ApexClass, ApexComponent, ApexPage, and ApexTrigger remain blocked in active orgs for performance reasons. _(v41-soap-004, Winter '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** SOQL queries filtering by record type now return results only for objects where the querying user has Read permission. _(v41-soql-001, Winter '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** SOQL queries against the RecordType object now enforce object-level Read permission; users without Read access on the parent object no longer see its record types in query results. _(v41-soql-003, Winter '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Quick actions backed by Visualforce pages or Lightning components no longer execute multiple times when users click them rapidly; debounce logic now prevents duplicate invocations. _(v41-vf-001, Winter '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Social Customer Service Apex methods now locate parent cases by matching on Persona instead of replyToId, and findParentCase internally delegates to findParentCaseFromPersona. _(v42-apex-002, Spring '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** The cmp.find() method now correctly locates components created at runtime via $A.createComponent(), fixing a bug that previously prevented this lookup from working. _(v42-aura-004, Spring '18)_
