- **[behavior-change]** JWT tokens returned by the Einstein Platform Services token endpoint and web page are now longer than before, which may affect code that validates or stores these tokens with length constraints. _(v42-auth-001, Spring '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Social sign-on auth provider URLs now route through subdomain and community-specific domains instead of login.salesforce.com, and the orgID parameter has been removed. Existing integrations using the old callback URLs must update their third-party app configurations to avoid redirect URI mismatch errors. _(v42-auth-006, Spring '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Einstein Platform Services JWT tokens have increased in length, which may break integrations with hardcoded buffer sizes or storage constraints for token values. _(v42-auth-008, Spring '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Autolaunched flows invoked in bulk contexts now execute every interview instead of silently discarding all but the first, which may surface latent errors or trigger limits in flows that previously ran only once per bulk operation. _(v42-flow-006, Spring '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Global value sets in managed package upgrades now preserve subscriber-org customizations (labels, API names, active/inactive status, defaults) the same way standard value sets do, except that global value set labels still update when the package includes new label values. _(v42-packaging-005, Spring '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Streaming API clients now receive explicit 401 error notifications on the /meta/connect or /meta/handshake channels when their OAuth token or session becomes invalid, enabling programmatic detection and reauthentication. _(v42-rest-014, Spring '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Apex controllers annotated with @AuraEnabled that omit explicit sharing keywords will run in without sharing mode once this update is active, potentially granting broader data access than the previous implicit with sharing behavior. _(v42-sharing-002, Spring '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** EmailServicesFunction picklist fields (AddressInactiveAction, AttachmentOption, AuthenticationFailureAction, AuthorizationFailureAction, FunctionInactiveAction, OverLimitAction) now return string values instead of numeric values, which may break integrations parsing these fields as integers. _(v42-soap-001, Spring '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** The FOR REFERENCE and FOR VIEW clauses in SOQL queries now track user actions more comprehensively for time-based workflows, potentially affecting audit trails and workflow triggers tied to record views or references. _(v42-soql-001, Spring '18, low confidence)_
- **[behavior-change]** Global value sets in managed packages now behave like standard value sets: upgrades no longer modify labels, API names, active/inactive states, or add new values in subscriber orgs. _(v46-packaging-002, Summer '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** Production orgs now recompile all Apex code during metadata deploys, package installs, and upgrades rather than lazily recompiling on first execution. This shifts compilation time into the deployment window. _(v43-apex-008, Summer '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Experience URLs switch from /one/one.app to /lightning format. Custom Lightning components that parse URLs using window.location or aura:locationChange may break if they expect the old path structure. Query string parameters are also rewritten with a prefix. _(v43-aura-001, Summer '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** The interface for Lightning components usable as flow local actions was renamed from flowruntime:availableForFlowLocalActions to lightning:availableForFlowActions, and the callback-based control flow was replaced with Promise-based resolution. _(v43-aura-004, Summer '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Locker Service now permits eval() even with Strict CSP enabled, but it always executes in global scope rather than local scope, so code relying on local variable access within eval() must be refactored to use Function() with explicit parameter passing. _(v43-aura-007, Summer '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Server-side Apex controllers returning Blob types to Lightning components now yield the string 'Blob(sizeOfBlobInBytes)' instead of throwing a generic error. To obtain actual blob data on the client, serialize the content as a JSON-friendly type such as String or Integer. _(v43-aura-008, Summer '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** When passing $Flow.ActiveStages or $Flow.CurrentStage to Lightning component attributes, the stage label is now returned instead of the fully qualified stage name. _(v43-flow-001, Summer '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Scheduled process actions and waiting flow interviews now batch only when they share the same execution time, process/flow version ID, and triggering user ID. Previously batches could mix different versions and users, leading to unexpected governor limit failures or mixed DML errors. _(v43-flow-002, Summer '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** When activated, this Critical Update makes Flow and Process Builder execute bulkifiable queries together in batches rather than one-by-one, reducing SOQL query consumption against governor limits. _(v43-flow-003, Summer '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** When activated, a process failure during batch create/update operations no longer rolls back the entire transaction. Instead, only records whose processes failed are rolled back, while successful records are saved after up to three retry attempts. _(v43-flow-004, Summer '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Flow interviews running in Lightning runtime now terminate when the user's session ends, matching the existing Classic runtime behavior. Any actions queued but not yet committed (pending record operations, emails) are lost if a session timeout occurs mid-interview. _(v43-flow-005, Summer '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Flow interview startup errors now appear in a dedicated FLOW_START_INTERVIEWS_ERROR debug log event rather than being bundled into FLOW_START_INTERVIEWS_END. _(v43-flow-007, Summer '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** When enabled, a process that fails no longer causes all other processes in the same transaction to fail. Instead, only the records associated with the failed process are rolled back while other records succeed. _(v43-flow-008, Summer '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Flow and process queries that can be bulkified are now executed in batches rather than individually, helping orgs avoid SOQL governor limits during high-volume transactions. _(v43-flow-009, Summer '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Debug log line formats changed: SYSTEM_CONSTRUCTOR_ENTRY events now logged correctly (not as CONSTRUCTOR_ENTRY), typeRefs appended to trigger/controller/class log entries, namespaces added to variable and method events, and method signatures now include parentheses. _(v43-other-003, Summer '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Package uninstallation now validates that at least one active business or person account record type remains, blocking uninstalls that would remove all active account record types. Previously this check only ran when directly removing a record type from the Record Type settings. _(v43-packaging-007, Summer '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Einstein Vision delete dataset endpoint now returns HTTP 200 with a JSON body containing a deletion ID instead of HTTP 204 with no content. Dataset deletion is now asynchronous and no longer cascades to associated models. _(v43-rest-006, Summer '18; supersedes v43-rest-008)_
- **[behavior-change]** Einstein Vision API no longer cascades model deletions when you delete a dataset. Models must now be explicitly removed via a dedicated DELETE endpoint. _(v43-rest-007, Summer '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** Deleting an Einstein Language dataset no longer cascades to its associated models; you must now call the DELETE /v2/language/models/<MODEL_ID> endpoint explicitly to remove each model. _(v43-rest-009, Summer '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** The ApexExecutionOverlayAction object now allows specifying the target class or trigger by name instead of ID. The ExecutableEntityId field is no longer unconditionally required—you can provide ExecutableEntityName instead, with ID taking precedence if both are supplied. _(v43-rest-010, Summer '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** NavigationMenuItem now defaults Status to DRAFT in API v43+ (previously LIVE in v42 and earlier), and queries without a Status filter now return all items instead of only LIVE ones. _(v43-rest-011, Summer '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** SOQL COUNT() queries now consume only one row toward governor limits instead of counting each returned row, reducing limit pressure for aggregate queries. _(v43-soql-001, Summer '18)_
- **[behavior-change]** System.UserInfo.getSessionId() now returns a valid session ID when invoked from asynchronous Apex (Batch, Future, Queueable, Scheduled) executed by an active user, whereas it previously returned null in all async contexts. _(v44-apex-003, Winter '19; supersedes v44-apex-004)_
- **[behavior-change]** Internal users can now authenticate to Communities via external OpenID Connect providers (e.g., Facebook), requiring the Apex RegistrationHandler to distinguish internal from external user creation. _(v44-auth-001, Winter '19; supersedes v44-auth-004)_
- **[behavior-change]** Stricter CSP enforcement moved from a critical update to a toggleable org setting, blocking inline JavaScript in script tags and event handlers when enabled. _(v44-lwc-002, Winter '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** A new org-level security setting prevents Lightning component code from modifying built-in JavaScript prototypes (Object, Array, DOM APIs, etc.), which breaks components that extend or polyfill native prototypes. _(v44-lwc-003, Winter '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** Flow metadata file names no longer include version numbers when using API 44.0. The fullName field behavior changed and a new status field was added, making flowDefinitions unnecessary for deployment. _(v44-packaging-004, Winter '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** Unlocked package upgrades now hard-delete a much larger set of metadata types (including LightningComponentBundle, NamedCredential, PermissionSetGroup, QuickAction, RemoteSiteSetting, and many others) from the subscriber org when those components are removed from the package source. _(v44-packaging-009, Winter '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** The EventLogFile object now filters out unrelated error events from the UI_EVENT_SOURCE field in Lightning Error event type logs, which may affect monitoring or analytics code that relied on the previous unfiltered data. _(v44-rest-003, Winter '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** The /limits/ endpoint now calculates storage using binary units (1 KB = 1024 bytes) instead of decimal units (1 KB = 1000 bytes), aligning with the Salesforce UI but returning different numeric values than before. _(v44-rest-004, Winter '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Open CTI onNavigationChange() callback now fires when a console tab refreshes, such as after saving a newly created case, eliminating the need for users to switch tabs to trigger the event. _(v44-rest-007, Winter '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** My Domain URLs now omit instance names by default, changing the hostname used by Visualforce pages, Community Builder, Site.com, and content file URLs. Integrations or code that parses or hardcodes instance-specific hostnames will break. _(v44-vf-001, Winter '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** Apex method parameters in Lightning components now undergo stricter validation and deserialization. Data passed to Apex controllers is more rigorously type-checked before method invocation. _(v45-apex-001, Spring '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** A critical update improving how Salesforce caches org schema information fixes bugs where actual behavior diverged from documented object and field handling, particularly around version-specific scenarios. _(v45-apex-002, Spring '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** String.format() now accepts List<Object> instead of List<String>, automatically converting non-string types via their toString() methods. Existing code passing List<String> remains compatible, but behavior differs when non-string objects are passed. _(v45-apex-005, Spring '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** Data passed from Aura JavaScript controllers to Apex methods now undergoes stricter type validation and improved deserialization for Integer, Long, Double, Date, Time, List, SObject, and Object parameters. Previously silent mismatches now throw detailed errors. _(v45-aura-002, Spring '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** The navigateToURL event now handles URL fragments consistently between Lightning Experience and Communities, aligning Community navigation behavior with Lightning Experience. _(v45-aura-006, Spring '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** The platform now blocks deletion of custom fields referenced by Aura components, preventing a previously silent metadata operation that caused runtime failures. _(v45-aura-007, Spring '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** Process and Flow formulas now correctly return null when evaluating expressions involving null record variables or null lookup relationship fields, rather than potentially returning unexpected non-null defaults. _(v45-flow-002, Spring '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Locker now sanitizes SVG files by stripping embedded JavaScript, which may break components that relied on scripted SVG content for legitimate functionality. _(v45-lwc-005, Spring '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Web Components introduce Shadow DOM encapsulation, which hides component internals from traditional DOM queries and breaks existing Selenium-style UI tests that rely on global DOM traversal. _(v45-lwc-008, Spring '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** The force:navigateToURL event no longer opens a new tab when navigating to hash-only URLs like '#123'. Developers should migrate to the standard__webPage PageReference type for external URL navigation. _(v45-lwc-009, Spring '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** High-volume platform events become GA and are now the default type for newly created event definitions. Standard-volume events defined in API 44.0 and earlier remain supported, but new standard-volume definitions are blocked. _(v45-other-002, Spring '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** Organizations provisioned from Spring '19 onward now count email alerts, simple email actions, Send Email flow actions, and REST API calls against the 5,000 daily external email cap. Older orgs remain limited only for Apex and non-REST API sends. _(v45-rest-003, Spring '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** Change Data Capture now emits events when custom field type conversions modify data, such as when incompatible type changes null out field values. Previously these data modifications were silently ignored by CDC. _(v45-rest-007, Spring '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** Change Data Capture now emits events when picklist field values are renamed or replaced across records, whereas previously these bulk picklist value changes were silently ignored. _(v45-rest-008, Spring '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** A new org-wide setting lets admins disable the default sharing behavior that gives case contacts (and their role hierarchy) automatic access to cases. When disabled, developers must implement manual shares or Apex managed sharing to grant case access to community users. _(v45-sharing-002, Spring '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce replaces JDK8-based date/time locale formatting with ICU-standard formats org-wide. This affects how dates and times render across the platform and can break integrations or code that parses formatted date strings. _(v48-other-005, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce replaces JDK8-based date/time locale formats with ICU-standard formats across the platform. API version 45.0 and later surfaces these new formats, and org-wide enforcement occurred January 2022. _(v49-other-003, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Flow and Process Builder formulas that reference null record variables or null lookup relationship fields now consistently return null instead of sometimes throwing unhandled exceptions. _(v50-flow-006, Winter '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce switches date and time formatting from Oracle JDK8 patterns to ICU locale standards, affecting how dates/times render across the platform and in API responses at v45.0+. _(v50-other-002, Winter '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** Custom Aura components in Experience Cloud sites that rely on URL query parameters now receive empty strings instead of literal expression text when expected URL values are missing. This retroactive enablement may affect components that previously saw raw expressions like {!recordId} when parameters were absent. _(v55-aura-002, Summer '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** A critical update improves how org schema information is cached and fixes issues with how object and field metadata is handled across different API versions. Originally scheduled for Summer '19, auto-activation has been pushed to Winter '19. _(v46-apex-005, Summer '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** The navigateToURL event in Lightning communities now handles URL fragments (hash values) the same way Lightning Experience does, opening them in the same tab rather than inconsistent behavior. _(v46-aura-001, Summer '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** Aura components now undergo stricter validation when saved or when managed packages are upgraded, surfacing errors that previously only appeared at runtime. _(v46-aura-002, Summer '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** The lightning:datatable URL column type now opens links in a new browser tab by default instead of the current window. _(v46-aura-003, Summer '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** SAML Assertion Consumer Service URLs generated for new SSO configurations in My Domain-enabled orgs no longer include the so=orgID query parameter suffix, which may affect IdP configurations expecting the old format. _(v46-auth-007, Summer '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** The default connected app used by force:auth:sfdxurl:store was updated, which can cause CI pipelines to fail with expired token errors when using previously generated SFDX auth URLs. _(v46-auth-010, Summer '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** Flow Assignment elements now undergo stricter validation during save, deploy, and install operations. Misconfigured values that previously passed silently will now throw errors, and error message strings have changed. _(v46-flow-003, Summer '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** In lightning-datatable, URL-type columns now open links in a new browser tab by default instead of the same window, and date-type columns derive their 12/24-hour time format from user locale rather than a fixed setting. _(v46-lwc-006, Summer '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** EventSubscription and EventDelivery metadata types are now auto-generated when activating platform-event-triggered processes, so these files should be removed from package manifests and deployments. _(v46-packaging-001, Summer '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** Namespaced unlocked packages now expose Apex debug logs and source code for Apex classes, triggers, and Visualforce components to subscriber org admins, and components can be removed directly from an installed package in Setup without creating a new package version. _(v46-packaging-007, Summer '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** Einstein Vision API now enforces a 2 GB ceiling on image datasets; POST calls creating a dataset or PUT calls adding images will fail with an error if the operation would push the dataset over this limit. _(v46-rest-008, Summer '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** Einstein Language API calls that create or append to text datasets now fail with an error if the operation would push the dataset beyond the 2 GB limit, whereas previously this may have been handled differently. _(v46-rest-009, Summer '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** Apex controllers marked @AuraEnabled that lack an explicit sharing declaration will be treated as 'without sharing' rather than inheriting sharing from the caller. Originally slated for auto-activation in Summer '19, enforcement is now delayed to Winter '20. _(v46-sharing-004, Summer '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** New Schema Settings options allow admins to hide custom settings and custom metadata fields from the Enterprise WSDL and block SOAP API access entirely, requiring Customize Application permission instead. _(v46-soap-002, Summer '19)_
- **[behavior-change]** Account Team Member objects now fire Apex triggers, validation rules, and workflow rules when records are created, edited, or deleted in Lightning Experience. Classic continues to bypass these automations. _(v47-apex-003, Winter '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Legacy transaction security policies using TxnSecurity.PolicyCondition no longer fail when the execution user is inactive; the automated process user now runs them instead. _(v47-apex-008, Winter '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Apex governor limits in Lightning components are now enforced individually per controller action rather than across all batched actions in a single request, affecting how limit consumption is tracked and reported in EventLogFile. _(v47-apex-009, Winter '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** A critical update modifies how Salesforce internally caches org schema metadata for standard and custom objects/fields, fixing bugs where actual behavior deviated from documented behavior and resolving intermittent issues with version-specific object/field handling. _(v47-apex-010, Winter '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** The lightning:datatable URL type now opens links in the same frame (_self) by default instead of a new tab, and no longer shows a tooltip unless explicitly configured. _(v47-aura-004, Winter '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** A new option lets admins strip encrypted consumer secrets from Metadata API and SOAP API responses when retrieving or deploying authentication provider configurations, which can break CI/CD pipelines that rely on round-tripping those secrets. _(v47-auth-002, Winter '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Custom authorization errors thrown by Apex registration handlers or third-party identity providers no longer appear visibly on the Problem Logging In page; they are now embedded only in the page URL as query parameters. _(v47-auth-003, Winter '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Users with the API Only User permission will be blocked from accessing Lightning Out, enforcing the same API-only restriction that already applies elsewhere in Salesforce. _(v47-auth-005, Winter '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** When activated, Flows will check that the running user has access to any Apex classes the Flow invokes, blocking execution if access is missing. Originally slated for Winter '20 auto-activation, enforcement is now delayed until Spring '21. _(v47-flow-002, Winter '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** LWC design property default values for Boolean and Integer types now correctly coerce to their declared types instead of being passed as strings. _(v47-lwc-001, Winter '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** The lightning-datatable url type now opens links in the same browser tab by default instead of a new tab, requiring explicit target: '_blank' configuration to restore previous behavior. _(v47-lwc-009, Winter '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Real-Time Event Monitoring moves from beta to GA with altered streaming architecture; existing beta subscribers must unsubscribe before the Winter '20 upgrade and resubscribe afterward or streams will break. _(v47-rest-008, Winter '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Einstein Language training endpoints now enforce a 3-million-word ceiling on text datasets; exceeding this limit causes POST /v2/language/train and /retrain to return an error. _(v47-rest-010, Winter '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** The EffectivePageTime field in LightningUriEvent and LightningUriEventStream now returns 0 instead of the actual value when it exceeds 60 seconds, filtering out outlier measurements. _(v47-rest-014, Winter '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** SOQL queries against KnowledgeArticleVersion without a publication_status filter now return draft, archived, and published articles, whereas previously only published articles were returned by default. _(v47-soql-001, Winter '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** When the new org permission is enabled, Apex code running outside System context loses implicit read access to custom settings unless the running user's profile or permission set explicitly grants Custom Setting Definitions access. _(v48-sharing-004, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Bulk REST API calls to invocable actions switch to partial-save semantics: individual action failures no longer roll back the entire transaction. Only the failing actions roll back while successful ones commit after up to three retry attempts. _(v50-rest-008, Winter '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** Bulk REST API calls to invocable actions now use partial-save semantics: a single failed action no longer rolls back the entire transaction. Instead, Salesforce retries successful actions up to three times and only rolls back the specific actions that fail. _(v51-flow-003, Spring '21; supersedes v47-flow-001)_
- **[behavior-change]** When an order product modification triggers a recalculation on the parent Order record, Salesforce now correctly fires custom logic (Apex triggers, validation rules, workflows, flows) on that parent. Previously this cascade was silently skipped. _(v60-apex-022, Spring '24; supersedes v56-apex-012, v55-apex-010)_
- **[behavior-change]** When an order product modification triggers a recalculation on its parent order, Apex triggers, validation rules, workflows, and flows on the Order object now fire correctly. Previously these were silently skipped. _(v61-apex-015, Summer '24; supersedes v59-apex-013)_
- **[behavior-change]** Notification emails (task assignment, case owner change, user welcome, etc.) are no longer suppressed when a process, workflow rule, or Apex trigger subsequently updates the same record. _(v48-apex-004, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** A critical update improves how Salesforce caches org schema internally, fixing bugs where version-specific object and field describe results could return stale or incorrect data, and eliminating rare cases where undocumented object types appeared in Apex describe methods. _(v48-apex-007, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Apex controllers with @AuraEnabled methods that omit explicit sharing declarations will default to 'with sharing' enforcement, applying the current user's sharing rules to all SOQL queries and DML operations. _(v48-apex-009, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** A new API Access Control setting can restrict external (community/portal) users so they may only call Salesforce APIs through connected apps that are explicitly installed in the org, blocking direct API access otherwise. _(v48-auth-002, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Orgs can now restrict external users' API access so they may only call Salesforce APIs through connected apps explicitly installed in the org. When enabled, external users without an approved connected app lose API access entirely. _(v48-auth-004, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** The default Facebook authentication provider for Social Sign-On now calls Facebook Graph API v5.0, which expires access tokens after 90 days of inactivity and removes the link and locale fields from the response. _(v48-auth-006, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Named credentials can now be accessed via the Salesforce API by any user holding the View Setup and Configuration permission, whereas previously different or more restrictive access rules may have applied. _(v48-auth-007, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Process Builder now correctly evaluates original field values that started as null when checking criteria across multiple evaluation passes, which can alter whether process actions fire for processes using ISCHANGED() or the 'only when specified changes are made' option. _(v48-flow-003, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** When activated, flows will enforce that the running user has explicit access to any Apex classes the flow invokes, rather than allowing invocation regardless of user permissions. _(v48-flow-004, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Flows and processes using partial-save actions no longer roll back the entire batch when one record fails; only the failing records are rolled back while successful changes persist. _(v48-flow-006, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** FlowExecutionErrorEvent platform event now guarantees values in EventType, FlowApiName, InterviewGuid, and InterviewStartDate fields that were previously nullable, and adds four new fields for richer error context. _(v48-flow-008, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Flow and process formulas now correctly return null when a record variable is null or when traversing a null lookup relationship, rather than failing or returning unexpected values. _(v48-flow-009, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** All class fields in Lightning web components are now automatically reactive without needing the @track decorator. The framework observes value assignments to any field and triggers rerenders when template-bound fields change. _(v48-lwc-002, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Data Service wire adapters may now return data objects that fail JavaScript strict equality checks even when the adapter configuration is unchanged, breaking code that relies on === comparisons for change detection. _(v48-lwc-003, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Locker now strips executable script content from HTML inserted via document.execCommand('insertHTML'), which may break components relying on that method to inject scripts dynamically. _(v48-lwc-007, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Jest snapshots for LWC tests now use stable placeholder values for dynamic attributes like id, for, href, and ARIA references instead of actual rendered values, which may cause existing snapshot tests to fail until regenerated. _(v48-lwc-008, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** The experimental session setting that froze JavaScript prototypes to prevent prototype pollution has been removed from Session Settings. Orgs that had enabled this security hardening measure will no longer have prototype freezing active. _(v48-lwc-009, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** The lightning-input number type now formats according to Salesforce locale during entry (not just on blur), removes increment/decrement buttons, prevents scroll-to-change behavior, fires change events when input becomes invalid, and preserves invalid input for correction instead of clearing it. _(v48-lwc-013, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** The lightning/uiListApi module now returns only fields explicitly requested via displayColumns, fields/optionalFields parameters, and standard system fields—previously it also included unrequested fields, so components relying on those extra fields will break. _(v48-lwc-014, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Visibility field for custom settings is now restricted to developer and scratch orgs only. Protected custom settings must be created in these org types and deployed via managed packages to keep their data hidden from subscriber orgs while remaining accessible to the package's Apex code. _(v48-packaging-002, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Symbol tables generated for managed packages now omit non-global implementation details, exposing only members explicitly marked global. Internal references previously misidentified as external are also corrected. _(v48-packaging-003, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** New orgs created from Spring '20 onward have the external sharing model enabled by default with all objects set to Private external access. Managed packages that assume non-Private external access levels may malfunction in these orgs. _(v48-packaging-005, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Installing an unlocked package containing a flow now overwrites any existing flow in the target org that shares the same API name, and removing a flow from an unlocked package no longer deletes it from subscriber orgs—manual deletion is required. _(v48-packaging-006, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Territory2 metadata type now requires unlocked packages to have no namespace across all API versions, aligning its behavior with Territory2Type which already had this requirement. _(v48-packaging-007, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Territory2Model no longer supports namespaces in unlocked packages across all API versions, fixing an inconsistency where territory models could previously be deployed with a namespace. _(v48-packaging-008, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Bulk REST API calls to invocable actions now use partial-save semantics: a single failure no longer rolls back the entire transaction. Instead, Salesforce retries successful actions up to three times and only rolls back the specific actions that fail. _(v48-rest-013, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** In orgs with Shield Platform Encryption, Change Data Capture events now flow through even when event encryption is disabled, arriving in plaintext on the event bus. Previously these events were blocked entirely until encryption was configured. _(v48-rest-016, Spring '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** A Release Update improves how Salesforce internally caches org schema metadata, fixing bugs where describe results could expose undocumented object types or incorrectly reuse version-specific schema details across API versions. _(v49-apex-006, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Querying TaskWhoIDs, AcceptedEventInviteeIds, DeclinedEventInviteeIds, UndecidedEventInviteeIds, or EventWhoIDs from within an Apex trigger now returns the contact and lead IDs associated with those activities. _(v49-apex-008, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** lightning:datatable columns with text data type now render boolean values as 'true'/'false' strings and currency values as raw numbers instead of empty cells, and clip-text mode no longer preserves multi-line truncation or extra whitespace. _(v49-aura-004, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Sforce-Locator response header in Bulk API 2.0 query jobs now returns a pseudo-random string instead of a numeric value, breaking any client code that attempts to predict or calculate locator values rather than reading them from the response. _(v49-bulk-001, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** The recalculateForecast invocable action now recalculates all account forecasts rather than being limited to a single account forecast, which may affect Flows relying on the previous single-account behavior. _(v49-flow-001, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Process Builder processes that check for field changes or use ISCHANGED() will evaluate against the original record values when a field started as null, potentially altering which criteria nodes fire. _(v49-flow-003, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Message Service moves from beta to GA with a breaking change to the subscribe() method: the default scope shifts from APPLICATION to active-area-only, meaning cross-page message delivery now requires an explicit scope parameter. _(v49-lwc-002, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** LWC components placed in custom tabs now rerender instead of being fully destroyed and recreated when query parameters change, aligning with standard LWC reactivity behavior. _(v49-lwc-007, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning components that reference Salesforce-provided components requiring specific permissions will fail with access errors if the user lacks the required permission, once the release update is enforced. _(v49-lwc-010, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** lightning-datatable now renders boolean values as 'true'/'false' strings and currency values as unformatted numbers when using text column type, instead of showing empty cells as before. _(v49-lwc-012, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Lightning Message Service subscribe() method no longer requires the subscriberOptions parameter. Without it, channel communication now defaults to scoped messaging within the active navigation context rather than application-wide. _(v49-lwc-013, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Installing or upgrading unlocked packages now deletes Flows that were removed from earlier package versions, whereas previously these orphaned Flows persisted in the target org. _(v49-packaging-003, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Attempting to enable event encryption via the PlatformEncryptionSettings Metadata API now fails with an error if no Event Bus tenant secret exists, rather than silently blocking CDC and platform events at runtime. _(v49-packaging-009, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** The FilterScope enumeration now distinguishes between opportunity team assignments (new SalesTeam value) and general team record assignments (Team value), splitting what was previously a single Team scope. _(v49-packaging-010, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce CLI now sends all JSON output to stdout by default when using --json, rather than splitting errors to stderr. Scripts that parse errors from stderr will break. _(v49-packaging-012, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Email Address Internationalization (EAI) enables Unicode characters in the local part of email addresses throughout Salesforce, requiring integrations to handle UTF-8 encoded email addresses and use the latest API version. _(v49-rest-004, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Connect REST API changes its default file rendition from Adobe Flash to a non-Flash format starting Summer '20, and will completely stop generating Flash renditions in Winter '21. _(v49-rest-005, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Bulk REST API calls to invocable actions switch to partial-save semantics: a single failed action no longer rolls back the entire transaction. Instead, Salesforce retries successful actions up to three times and only rolls back the specific failures. _(v49-rest-007, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** The /limits REST endpoint now returns 'DailyBulkApiBatches' instead of 'DailyBulkApiRequests' as the label for the daily Bulk API usage metric. _(v49-rest-017, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Composite REST requests now default collateSubrequests to true, meaning subrequests execute together on a single database transaction for improved performance rather than executing independently. _(v49-rest-018, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** The User Interface API child-relationships endpoint now returns actual values for lastModifiedById, lastModifiedDate, systemModStamp, and weakEtag properties that previously always returned null. _(v49-rest-020, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Metadata API now validates that an Event Bus tenant secret exists before allowing enableEventBusEncryption to be set, returning an error if the prerequisite is missing. _(v49-soap-002, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** Querying AsyncApexJob or FlexQueueItem via SOAP API requires the user to hold View Setup and Configuration permission once this release update is enforced. Anonymous Apex that enqueues async jobs (Batch, @future, Queueable, Scheduled) must also run as a user with that permission. _(v49-soap-003, Summer '20)_
- **[behavior-change]** When an order product insert or update modifies the parent Order record, Salesforce now fires validation rules, Apex triggers, workflow rules, and flows on both the Order and OrderProduct objects. Previously these customizations were skipped in this cascade scenario. _(v50-apex-001, Winter '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** Publishing platform events with Publish Immediately behavior no longer blocks subsequent Apex callouts in the same transaction. These events now count against a separate 150-call limit tracked via new Limits methods rather than the DML statement limit. _(v50-apex-011, Winter '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** The lightning:datatable component now renders empty content for text-type columns when an object value is passed instead of a string, which may cause existing data to disappear if code was inadvertently passing objects. _(v50-aura-005, Winter '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** Firefox's new SameSite=Lax cookie default breaks cross-domain integrations that rely on cookies without explicit SameSite attributes. Custom integrations using iframes or cross-domain communication must update cookies to set SameSite=None; Secure explicitly. _(v50-auth-002, Winter '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** Process Builder processes using multiple criteria with record updates will evaluate the original field value when that field initially contained null, potentially altering which criteria branches execute. _(v50-flow-004, Winter '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** Static resources in Lightning components will be served from the visualforce domain rather than the lightning domain, blocking scripts in those resources from accessing lightning domain documents via same-origin policy. _(v50-lwc-005, Winter '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** The lightning-datatable component no longer renders any content for text-type columns when an object value is passed instead of a string. _(v50-lwc-008, Winter '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Create Transcript REST API endpoint relocates the participant ID from the URI path into the request body for security reasons. The legacy URI format remains functional in Winter '21 but will be removed in a future release. _(v50-rest-001, Winter '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** The DownloadSize field on AppAnalyticsQueryRequest changed from int to long data type because values can exceed integer limits. Integrations parsing this field as int may encounter overflow errors. _(v50-rest-015, Winter '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** SObject Collections errors now pinpoint which specific object in the batch caused the problem, and when allOrNone is false the API processes valid records instead of failing the entire request on parse errors. _(v50-rest-016, Winter '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** The enableSecureGuestAccess field on SharingSettings now always returns true and any value you set is ignored—guest user security settings are permanently enforced. _(v50-sharing-007, Winter '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** Instance names are being stripped from Visualforce URLs via a release update, meaning any integrations or code that parses or constructs URLs using the instance prefix will break when enforcement arrives. _(v50-vf-003, Winter '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** Autolaunched flows with Pause elements will retain their original execution context and user permissions when resuming after a time-based event, instead of switching to system context without sharing. This prevents unintended privilege escalation where paused flows could modify records the running user lacks access to. _(v56-flow-003, Winter '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Autolaunched flows with Pause elements now resume in their original execution context rather than defaulting to system context without sharing. Additionally, flows on API 57.0+ verify the user still has permission to run the flow before resuming a paused interview. _(v58-flow-003, Summer '23; supersedes v57-flow-005)_
- **[behavior-change]** Anonymous Apex blocks that invoke named credential callouts now require the Customize Application permission on the executing user, where previously no such permission was needed. _(v51-auth-001, Spring '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** Modifying the URL, Authentication Provider, or Outbound Network Connection fields on a named credential or external data source with named principal identity now requires reauthentication against the endpoint for OAuth and password authentication protocols. _(v51-auth-003, Spring '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** ISV partners using the Subscriber Support Console to log into customer orgs must now authenticate their License Management Org session with MFA, or the login attempt is blocked. _(v51-auth-006, Spring '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** Flow and Process Builder CPU time consumption is now measured and enforced accurately. Previously, CPU usage was sometimes miscounted or attributed to subsequent automation like Apex triggers. After enablement, flows fail immediately when the element causing the CPU limit breach executes. _(v51-flow-006, Spring '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** The lightning-icon component now loads SVG icons lazily, which can cause DOM markup to be unavailable during initial render cycles. Code that queries icon internals immediately after rendering may fail. _(v51-lwc-008, Spring '21; supersedes v51-aura-005)_
- **[behavior-change]** New LWR sites automatically enable ExperienceBundle metadata type, eliminating the prior manual Setup checkbox step for these sites. _(v51-packaging-007, Spring '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** Standard-volume platform events now publish asynchronously instead of synchronously, meaning publish results return before delivery is confirmed and dependent logic may need adjustment. _(v51-rest-001, Spring '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** Standard-volume platform events now publish asynchronously rather than synchronously. A successful SaveResult no longer guarantees immediate delivery—it only confirms the event was queued for later publishing, matching high-volume event semantics. _(v51-rest-011, Spring '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** Commerce Payments introduces revised formulas for PaymentAuthorization fields: TotalAuthReversalAmount now sums all processed authorization reversals, and Balance now calculates as authorized amount minus captured amount minus reversal amount (can be negative). _(v51-rest-012, Spring '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce now correctly tracks CPU time for flows and processes, applying enforcement to all flows regardless of their configured API version once the release update is active. Flows that previously appeared within limits may now fail if they truly exceed CPU thresholds. _(v54-flow-005, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Stricter validation on Visualforce Remoting API calls (introduced Spring '21) requires explicit Apex class access grants; Field Service Dispatcher Console users need FSL.ctrl001_Gantt added to their profile's Apex Class Access or remote calls fail. _(v54-vf-003, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce will mandate MFA for all UI-based logins starting February 2022. Integrations using direct user credentials without MFA, or SSO flows lacking a second factor, must be updated to comply with the new terms of service. _(v52-auth-001, Summer '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** License Management Orgs used for first- and second-generation managed packages will require MFA authentication before accessing the Subscriber Support Console, blocking login attempts without MFA verification. _(v52-auth-003, Summer '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** The OAuth 2.0 JWT bearer flow now returns both standard and custom scopes in access tokens for preauthorized connected apps, whereas previously only standard scopes or scopes from prior tokens were included. _(v52-auth-005, Summer '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** Embedded Login gains an optional setting that restricts OAuth redirect URLs to same-host/domain targets or explicitly allow-listed domains, rejecting unknown redirect destinations passed in the state parameter. _(v52-auth-008, Summer '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** The defaultValue field on FlowScreenField now works with choice-based field types (RadioButtons, DropdownBox, MultiSelectCheckboxes, MultiSelectPicklist), enabling default selections for choice resources in flow screens. _(v52-flow-001, Summer '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** Flow and Process Builder CPU time consumption is now measured and attributed correctly. Previously, CPU time could be miscounted or blamed on downstream Apex triggers; now the actual consuming element fails immediately when the limit is crossed. _(v52-flow-004, Summer '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** Process Builder processes that check for changed fields or use ISCHANGED() will evaluate against the original field value when that value started as null, potentially altering which criteria branches execute. _(v52-flow-006, Summer '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** SLDS design tokens now reference the operating system's native sans-serif font instead of Salesforce Sans, which may alter text rendering and layout in custom Lightning components. _(v52-lwc-005, Summer '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** SLDS design tokens now reference values from the new Salesforce Color System, which may alter the rendered appearance of components relying on those tokens. _(v52-lwc-006, Summer '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** The lightning-formatted-text, lightning-formatted-url, and lightning-pill components now automatically prepend the host domain's protocol (e.g., https://) to URLs lacking an explicit protocol, changing how relative URLs render as links. _(v52-lwc-007, Summer '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Einstein NER endpoint now derives the time zone for DATETIME normalization from the language parameter when timezone is omitted, instead of using a fixed default. _(v52-rest-002, Summer '21)_
- **[behavior-change]** The valueOf() method on enums now throws an exception when the input string does not match any enum constant, replacing the previous runtime error behavior. _(v53-apex-001, Winter '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** A new org setting allows workflow rules, processes, and Apex triggers to send email notifications for field updates on the same record that triggered the automation, overriding the previous suppression behavior. _(v53-apex-005, Winter '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** The initSelfRegistration Apex method now derives the user's language from the LanguageLocaleKey field on the User object rather than from request parameters, cookies, or browser settings, potentially changing which language verification emails and SMS messages are sent in. _(v53-apex-006, Winter '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce now contractually mandates MFA for all UI-based logins. Organizations must enable MFA either natively in Salesforce or via their SSO provider before the enforcement date. _(v53-auth-001, Winter '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Custom JIT provisioning handlers implementing SamlJitHandler now receive decrypted SAML assertions via the Sfdc.SamlAssertion key, enabling access to attributes that were previously inaccessible when the IdP sent encrypted assertions. _(v53-auth-004, Winter '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Platform event subscribers (flows and processes) now receive at most 200 records per batch instead of the previous 2,000 limit, which may increase the number of batches your automation processes. _(v53-flow-001, Winter '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Scheduled paths in record-triggered flows now execute under asynchronous Apex governor limits instead of synchronous limits, allowing more headroom for complex operations within each path execution. _(v53-flow-002, Winter '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Flows from managed packages now hide error details when they fail, including failures in Pause elements and referenced subflows. This affects debugging visibility when troubleshooting managed package flow errors. _(v53-flow-003, Winter '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Experience HTML structure, CSS, and DOM internals may change between releases without notice, potentially breaking Selenium or similar automated UI tests that depend on specific element selectors or DOM paths. _(v53-lwc-005, Winter '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Deploying opportunity stages mapped to the new Most Likely forecast category via Metadata API, sandbox refresh, or packages will fail unless the target org has already enabled Most Likely as a Forecast Category picklist value. _(v53-packaging-005, Winter '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Status field picklist value for batch job cancellation changed spelling from 'Cancelled' to 'Canceled' across BatchJob, BatchJobPart, and BatchJobStatusChangedEvent objects. _(v53-rest-012, Winter '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Product records gain org-wide sharing defaults, changing from implicit Public Read/Write to configurable access levels. When set to Private, Apex triggers, flows, and validation rules that assume full product access may fail. _(v53-sharing-002, Winter '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Original Territory Management sharing records are permanently deleted, which removes any record access granted through that legacy sharing mechanism and affects report output that previously included those rows. _(v53-sharing-004, Winter '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Admins can now block SOAP API login() calls that use generic endpoints (login.salesforce.com / test.salesforce.com), forcing integrations to authenticate via the org's My Domain URL instead. _(v53-soap-003, Winter '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Users logging in via SSO Authentication Providers no longer face a second MFA challenge in Salesforce, even if they have the MFA user permission enabled. This fixes a bug where some SSO users were prompted for MFA twice. _(v54-auth-006, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** CPU time consumption by flows and processes is now accurately measured and enforced. Transactions that exceed CPU limits will fail at the specific element or action that crosses the threshold, rather than being underreported. _(v54-flow-008, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Users logging in via SSO Auth Providers now correctly skip the Salesforce MFA challenge when they have the MFA for UI Logins permission, ending the double-MFA prompt bug. Orgs that escaped Spring '22 enforcement are now enforced. _(v55-auth-005, Summer '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** The platform now allows queueable jobs to run with shorter intervals between executions than before. Code that assumed a minimum delay between chained queueables may now experience faster-than-expected sequential execution. _(v54-apex-003, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce now contractually mandates MFA for all user logins, whether direct or via SSO. Integrations using interactive user sessions must accommodate MFA verification methods. _(v54-auth-001, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** ISV partners accessing subscriber orgs via the Subscriber Support Console must now authenticate to their License Management Org using MFA. Additionally, subscribers can opt to require a second MFA challenge before granting LMO user access. _(v54-auth-002, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** JWT bearer flow access tokens now inherit high assurance session requirements from user profiles, so integrations connecting as users with elevated session policies may need to satisfy those requirements. _(v54-auth-005, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Flows invoked through REST API can now run in the context of the invoking user rather than system context when the FlowSettings field enableFlowViaRestUsesUserCtxt is enabled. _(v54-flow-001, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** The flowLayout=twoColumn URL parameter and the Two Columns layout property for screen flows will be ignored starting Winter '23. Flows using this layout will render as single-column unless migrated to Section components. _(v54-flow-002, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Custom Aura components embedded in screen flows now display an error window with stack trace details for init handler failures and fire onstatuschange events even when errors occur, whereas previously the screen silently went blank and blocked status events. _(v54-flow-004, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Web Security (LWS) reaches GA as an opt-in replacement for Lightning Locker, applying a different sandboxing model that blocks or modifies some APIs while relaxing other restrictions. Enabling it changes the runtime security enforcement for all LWC in the org. _(v54-lwc-002, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce begins rolling enablement of Lightning Web Security to replace Lightning Locker in production orgs that contain exclusively LWC. Components previously sandboxed by Locker will run under the new LWS runtime instead. _(v54-lwc-003, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** LWC now emits console warnings for malformed HTML such as missing or extra closing tags. These warnings become blocking errors in Winter '23, preventing affected components from loading. _(v54-lwc-004, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Design System styling hooks namespace changes from --sds to --slds, requiring updates to any CSS custom properties using the old prefix. _(v54-lwc-008, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Creating a 2GP package version now requires explicitly setting an ancestor. New keywords HIGHEST and NONE plus the --skipancestorcheck CLI flag provide control over ancestor selection. _(v54-packaging-003, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Batch processing of ServiceAppointmentShare records during service appointment status changes is now capped at 50,000 records per transaction, causing errors and rollback when exceeded. _(v54-rest-004, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Quip Admin and Automation APIs now enforce per-company rate limits of 600 requests per minute by default, with new response headers (X-Company-RateLimit-Limit, X-Company-RateLimit-Remaining, X-Company-RateLimit-Reset, X-Company-Retry-After) to enable client-side backoff logic. _(v54-rest-006, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Product records gain org-wide sharing defaults, which can restrict access from Public Read/Write to Private. Apex triggers, flows, and validation rules that interact with Product2 may fail if they assume full access. _(v54-sharing-002, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** The FIELDS() function in SOQL queries executed from Apex now works reliably in all scenarios where it previously threw errors under certain conditions. _(v54-soql-001, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** When multiple navigation API calls fire in rapid succession from Visualforce or Lightning components, only the first call executes. Previously all calls attempted to run, causing race conditions. _(v54-vf-002, Spring '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Aura components no longer fail to save due to general JavaScript validation errors; these checks now only run via ESLint as optional informational linting rather than blocking deployment. _(v55-aura-001, Summer '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** The idTokenIssuer field on AuthProvider metadata is now configurable for Microsoft authentication providers, whereas previously it was limited to OpenID Connect providers only. _(v55-auth-002, Summer '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Bulk API and Bulk API 2.0 jobs now apply whichever Apex governor limits are higher between synchronous and asynchronous thresholds, except for CPU time which uses a dedicated bulk-specific limit separate from standard Apex transactions. _(v55-bulk-001, Summer '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Process Builder criteria using ISCHANGED() or the 'execute only when specified changes occur' option now correctly evaluate original field values even when those were null, potentially changing which criteria branches fire. _(v55-flow-004, Summer '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Synthetic shadow DOM corrections align with native shadow behavior: assignedSlot now returns the actual slot element for slotted content in mixed shadow environments, and elementsFromPoint returns all elements including those in shadow trees rather than only visible ones. _(v55-lwc-002, Summer '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Web Security now intercepts additional browser APIs including CacheStorage, History state methods, Node DOM manipulation, Notification, Range operations, SVG animation attributes, postMessage, and XSLTProcessor transforms. Components using these APIs may encounter modified behavior or blocked operations. _(v55-lwc-003, Summer '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** The lightning-formatted-rich-text and lightning-input-rich-text components now transform <b> and <i> HTML tags into <strong> and <em> respectively, removing support for the original bold and italic tags. _(v55-lwc-006, Summer '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** The @salesforce/community scoped module now returns 18-character record IDs instead of the previous 15-character format, aligning with standard Salesforce API conventions. _(v55-lwc-009, Summer '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Metadata API deployments now require every component to have a unique name; duplicate names cause deployment failures. _(v55-packaging-001, Summer '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** ManagedContentDeliveryDocument was refactored into a subclass of AbstractManagedContentDeliveryDocument, moving properties like contentKey, contentType, language, managedContentId, publishedDate, title, unauthenticatedUrl, and urlName to the parent class. _(v55-rest-005, Summer '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Quip Automation API now enforces a 4,000-item cap per folder and auto-converts standard folders to workspace folders when membership exceeds 500, affecting integrations that bulk-add items or members. _(v55-rest-012, Summer '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** Platform-wide redirect security validation is tightened, potentially blocking previously allowed URL redirects in custom Apex, Visualforce, Flows, and Experience Cloud sites. _(v55-sharing-002, Summer '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** SOAP API now handles malformed endpoint URIs differently: unparseable version segments default to v21.0 instead of v7.0, and invalid WSDL type segments with extra characters now throw InvalidApiUrlException rather than silently defaulting. _(v55-soap-002, Summer '22)_
- **[behavior-change]** ICU locale formats replace JDK locale formats across the platform, altering how dates, times, currencies, addresses, names, and numbers render in Apex formatting methods, SOQL, Visualforce, and integrations. _(v63-other-010, Spring '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** The lightning:formattedDateTime, lightning:formattedTime, and lightning:input components now interpret all ISO8601 time strings as UTC rather than local time, which may shift displayed times. _(v56-aura-001, Winter '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Fresh Salesforce orgs now ship with Lightning Web Security enabled by default for LWC instead of Lightning Locker, changing the sandbox isolation model that custom components run under. _(v56-lwc-001, Winter '23; supersedes v56-lwc-015)_
- **[behavior-change]** The LWC framework now emits console warnings for additional categories of invalid HTML syntax that were previously ignored. These warnings are expected to become hard errors in a future release, which would prevent affected components from loading. _(v56-lwc-004, Winter '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** The lightning-formatted-date-time, lightning-formatted-time, and lightning-input components now interpret all ISO8601 time strings as UTC, which may shift displayed times for values previously parsed with local timezone assumptions. _(v56-lwc-010, Winter '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** OmniStudio FlexCards cannot be deployed to LWR Experience sites when Standard OmniStudio Runtime is enabled; you must disable standard runtime and use the generated LWC component instead. _(v56-lwc-018, Winter '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Enhanced domains and partitioned domains increase hostname variability across Salesforce orgs, so packages with hard-coded Salesforce URLs (for content, Visualforce, etc.) may break when installed in orgs with different domain configurations. _(v56-packaging-001, Winter '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Enabling high-volume prediction writeback permanently changes how Einstein Discovery prediction history is accessed: retention drops from unlimited to 30 days, SOQL queries no longer work for retrieving predictions, and data must be fetched via the Einstein Discovery REST API instead. _(v56-rest-001, Winter '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Query cursor limits are lifted: orgs can now hold more than 10 concurrent result sets per user, and cursors remain valid for 2 days instead of expiring after 15 minutes of inactivity. Query locator string prefixes changed from 01g to 0r8. _(v56-rest-003, Winter '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** EventRelayConfig moves from beta to GA with breaking changes: Tooling API request body structure is altered, EventRelayFeedback drops NumEventsDropped/NumEventsRelayed/Replay fields and adds ErrorCode/LastRelayedEventTime fields. _(v56-rest-008, Winter '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Records field on ApiEventStream for Bulk API queries now returns null instead of actual record data to avoid bandwidth issues. Integrations that parsed this field for Bulk API audit logging will receive empty values. _(v56-rest-010, Winter '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Connect REST APIs now enforce stricter permission and org-level access checks on the context user, which may cause previously successful calls to return different HTTP status codes or error messages. _(v56-rest-011, Winter '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Duration field on EngagementInteraction is now read-only and auto-calculated from start/end times; code that previously wrote to this field will fail. _(v56-rest-017, Winter '23; supersedes v56-rest-018)_
- **[behavior-change]** Metadata API retrieve and deploy operations no longer return the encrypted consumer secret field for authentication provider records, breaking any tooling that parsed or stored these secrets from metadata responses. _(v56-rest-020, Winter '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Enhanced Personal Information Management replaces the older Hide Personal Information setting and blocks external users (portal, community, guest) from viewing other users' PII fields. Scoping rules now filter records only in SOQL, reports, and list views—no longer in searches, lookups, activity timeline, or SOSL. _(v56-sharing-001, Winter '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Scoping rules no longer apply automatically to SOSL queries, search results, lookups, or the activity timeline. They now only affect SOQL (when explicitly invoked via USING SCOPE), reports, and list views. _(v56-soql-001, Winter '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Static element rendering optimizations introduced in Spring '23 cause extra whitespace characters to appear in class and style attribute values in the DOM, which can break exact-match attribute selectors. _(v61-lwc-007, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** When invoking Apex actions via REST API, any unhandled exception now causes a full transaction rollback, preventing partial data commits. Previously, data changes could persist even when the action threw an exception. _(v61-rest-018, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Admins can now configure an org-wide default delay (1–600 seconds) for queueable jobs enqueued without an explicit delay parameter, which may cause existing jobs to run slower than before if this setting is enabled. _(v57-apex-004, Spring '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Apex static variables set by platform event–triggered flows now reset between groups of flow interviews executing for different users within the same transaction, preventing values from persisting across the full transaction scope. _(v57-apex-007, Spring '23; supersedes v57-apex-011)_
- **[behavior-change]** All Aura-based Experience Cloud sites are forcibly migrated from analytics.js to gtag.js. Sites using custom analytics.js integrations or UA-ID tracking IDs require manual updates to G-IDs to continue collecting data after enforcement. _(v57-aura-001, Spring '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce begins automatically enabling MFA for direct username/password logins across all orgs in phases throughout 2023, with eventual permanent enforcement planned. _(v57-auth-001, Spring '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** AuthProvider metadata now always exports consumerSecret as a placeholder value for all change sets and packages, including those created before November 2022, regardless of sendSecretInApis setting; imported values are treated as plaintext. _(v57-auth-002, Spring '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce automatically enables the MFA requirement for direct UI logins in production orgs via a phased Release Update, forcing all users to authenticate with a second factor after entering credentials. _(v57-auth-008, Spring '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** A new org setting allows administrators to validate certificate revocation status (via OCSP or CRL) during certificate-based authentication, blocking logins when certificates are revoked or cannot be validated. _(v57-auth-009, Spring '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Web Security replaces Lightning Locker as the security architecture for LWC (GA) and Aura (beta). New orgs and scratch orgs have LWS enabled by default, affecting how component JavaScript executes and interacts across namespace boundaries. _(v57-lwc-001, Spring '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Orgs lacking custom LWC or Aura components now default to Lightning Web Security instead of Lightning Locker. When you subsequently deploy or install Lightning components, they run under LWS rules rather than Locker. _(v57-lwc-002, Spring '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Framework optimizations for static element handling can inject extra whitespace into class and style attribute values in the rendered DOM, potentially breaking exact-match attribute selectors. _(v57-lwc-004, Spring '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Light DOM LWC components embedded in Aura containers (outside Experience Cloud, CMS content editor, and Sales Enablement) now require scoped styles; unscoped styles no longer work in these contexts. _(v57-lwc-006, Spring '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** CSS pseudo-element selectors with leading whitespace (like `, ::before`) now scope correctly in synthetic shadow DOM, preventing styles from leaking to descendant elements the component doesn't own. _(v57-lwc-008, Spring '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning apps now receive unique CSRF tokens scoped to each app rather than sharing tokens across apps, and invalid or expired token handling is stricter. _(v57-lwc-010, Spring '23; supersedes v57-lwc-014)_
- **[behavior-change]** The executionProcessApiName field on BatchProcessJobDefinition metadata now supports TierProcessing loyalty program process API names, expanding valid values for this field in deployments. _(v57-packaging-005, Spring '23, low confidence)_
- **[behavior-change]** Authentication provider consumer secrets are now stripped and replaced with placeholders during change set or package deployment, requiring manual re-entry post-deployment. This applies to all packages including those created before November 2022. _(v57-packaging-007, Spring '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** The num_reads metric in AppExchange App Analytics package usage summaries no longer counts SOQL and SOSL queries — it now reflects only actual record reads, resulting in lower reported values. _(v57-rest-002, Spring '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** The GeoCountry object's Name field is now createable, updateable, and nillable, allowing API integrations to set or clear this field where previously it was read-only. _(v57-rest-004, Spring '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** The TaxTreatment object's ProductCode field now supports idLookup, enabling its use as an external ID in upsert operations. _(v57-rest-005, Spring '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** The /limits endpoint no longer breaks down usage by connected app for DailyBulkApiBatches, DailyGenericStreamingApiEvents, and DailyStreamingApiEvents; it now returns only aggregate Max and Remaining values. _(v57-rest-007, Spring '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** REST APIs using Conditional Request Headers now return HTTP 428 (Precondition Required) when a request lacks required conditional headers, instead of a different error or proceeding unconditionally. _(v57-rest-008, Spring '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** The UI API content-documents endpoints now return a generic Record type instead of Content Document and Content Version types, and only required plus explicitly requested fields are returned rather than all object fields. _(v57-rest-009, Spring '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** A new org preference prevents Experience Cloud, portal, and community users from running anonymous Apex, even if they hold Author Apex or other elevated permissions. Enabled by default in new orgs; existing orgs must opt in. _(v57-sharing-002, Spring '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** DataWeave in Apex now requires explicit encoding when coercing binary data (Blobs) to strings, and performs feature-support validation at script creation rather than execution time. _(v58-apex-003, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Tests marked with @IsTest(OnInstall=true) no longer accumulate code coverage metrics when executed during package installation or upgrade. Coverage is only calculated during the package build process itself. _(v58-apex-005, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** AppExchange App Analytics no longer captures CRUD operations performed during Apex unit test execution against packaged custom objects, affecting ISV partners who relied on this telemetry for usage analysis. _(v58-apex-007, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** The maximum number of Aura actions permitted in a single boxcar request has been reduced, potentially causing failures for pages that batch many server calls together. _(v58-aura-001, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Experience Cloud Aura sites now leverage the same CDN-based caching infrastructure as Lightning Experience, which may surface previously hidden timing or caching bugs in custom Aura components. _(v58-aura-003, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce is progressively auto-enabling MFA for direct username/password logins across orgs. This phase continues the rollout started in Spring '23, moving toward mandatory enforcement where MFA becomes a permanent login requirement. _(v58-auth-001, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Headless Registration API ignores the Auth-Verification-Type header in the initial POST to /services/auth/headless/init/registration; only the verificationmethod body parameter is read. Integrations relying on the header to select email vs SMS OTP delivery must move that value into the request body. _(v58-auth-006, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Users holding the API Only User permission can no longer leverage frontdoor.jsp session bridging to reach the Salesforce UI, except for password management screens. _(v58-auth-008, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Guest users executing flows no longer need explicit Apex class access for invocable Apex actions within those flows, as the enforcement rule requiring such access is now disabled. _(v58-flow-006, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** The lightning-input base component's internal DOM structure will change in Winter '24, which may break code that relies on querying or styling internal elements. _(v58-lwc-001, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Web Security now governs Aura components in addition to LWC. When enabled, both component types run under LWS instead of Lightning Locker, which can change runtime sandbox isolation behavior and API access patterns. _(v58-lwc-003, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Web Security adds new distortions for several web APIs including CustomElementRegistry methods, Document event handlers, and various HTMLElement prototypes. Components relying on undistorted behavior of these APIs may behave differently. _(v58-lwc-004, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** The lightning-input base component's internal DOM structure will be reorganized in Winter '24 as part of the move toward native shadow DOM support, breaking any tests or CSS that depend on the current internal element hierarchy. _(v58-lwc-012, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning apps now receive unique per-app CSRF tokens instead of a shared token, and token validation becomes stricter for invalid or expired tokens. Custom code that stores, passes, or validates CSRF tokens across app boundaries may break. _(v58-lwc-013, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** The lightning/uiGraphQLApi graphql wire adapter no longer requires metaschema directives (@category) for referential integrity. Existing code using these directives should remove them as the usage is deprecated. _(v58-lwc-015, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** LWR sites now perform single-page navigation using Lightning Navigation instead of full page reloads, and external links default to opening in a new tab rather than the current tab. _(v58-lwc-017, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** The ProgramId, TemplateName, and TemplateVersion fields on the LoyaltyProgramWidget object are now read-only; integrations that previously updated these fields will fail. _(v58-rest-016, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** REST API calls to Apex invocable actions now roll back all DML if the action throws an exception, preserving transactional integrity where partial commits previously occurred. _(v58-rest-017, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Implicit child share records linking accounts to their opportunity children are no longer persisted; the system now evaluates access dynamically at query time. SOQL queries and Apex tests that previously retrieved these implicit share records will return empty results. _(v58-sharing-001, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** Flow Orchestration objects now respect standard sharing rules. The Manage Flow permission alone no longer grants access; users need the Manage Orchestration Runs and Work Items permission plus sharing access. _(v58-sharing-002, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** SOQL queries on FeedItem without an explicit ORDER BY clause may now return results in a different sequence than before, potentially breaking code that assumed a particular ordering. _(v58-soql-003, Summer '23)_
- **[behavior-change]** The AuthConfigProviders object now permits creating records with AuthConfigId and AuthProviderId values, enabling programmatic configuration of authentication providers on login pages. _(v59-rest-004, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** The EmailSimple invocable action will start honoring organization-wide email address profile settings. Calls from Flow, Apex, or REST API that lack proper email profile configuration will begin throwing errors. _(v60-flow-004, Spring '24; supersedes v59-flow-006)_
- **[behavior-change]** When deserializing Apex objects, the runtime now honors the API version of the class that originally serialized the data, rather than the current class version. This ensures consistent behavior between serialization and deserialization across version boundaries. _(v59-apex-006, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Apex method generateThreadingMessageId(caseId) now returns a Message-ID using a simplified format that differs structurally from the previous EntityId-based format, potentially breaking code that parses or validates the old format. _(v59-apex-014, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Flows initiated by Einstein Bots will run in user context using the bot's profile and permission sets, rather than system context with full data access. _(v59-apex-015, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** The lightning:navigation component no longer auto-closes modals when navigate() is called with the replace parameter at its default false value; instead, modals now stack. To restore the previous auto-close behavior, explicitly pass replace as true. _(v59-aura-001, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** The force:navigateToURL and force:navigateToSObject events no longer auto-close modals by default. Setting isredirect=false or replace=false now stacks modals instead of closing them, requiring explicit isredirect=true or replace=true to restore the previous auto-close behavior. _(v59-aura-002, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce continues phased auto-enablement of MFA for direct UI logins. When enabled, users must provide a second factor after username/password entry.
