The OAuth 2.0 username-password flow and SOAP API login are explicitly discouraged for security reasons. _(v59-auth-004, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Managing named credentials and external credentials now requires the new 'Manage Named Credentials' permission instead of the broader 'Customize Applications' permission. _(v59-auth-010, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce now applies HTTP caching with up to 10-minute TTL for LWC and Aura component resources, meaning code deployments may not appear in the browser immediately without a hard refresh or debug mode enabled. _(v59-lwc-003, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Base Lightning components now render with updated color values for improved WCAG non-text contrast compliance. Custom components using hardcoded colors may look inconsistent unless migrated to global color styling hooks (--slds-g-*). _(v59-lwc-004, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Web Security adds new distortions that block or alter behavior for several DOM and event APIs including getInnerHTML, setHTML, window.find, and various event handlers like storage and rejectionhandled events. _(v59-lwc-008, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** JavaScript loaded from static resources in LWR Experience Cloud sites now executes under Lightning Web Security restrictions, which may break code relying on DOM access patterns or APIs that LWS blocks. _(v59-lwc-013, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** LWC components registered via CustomElementConstructor with native shadow DOM now preserve slotted content in top-level elements during rendering, whereas previously that content was removed. _(v59-lwc-014, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** A new org setting lets Lightning apps embedded in third-party contexts (Lightning Out, Outlook integration) authenticate via session token instead of cookies, bypassing browser third-party cookie restrictions. _(v59-lwc-015, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Each Lightning app now receives its own unique CSRF token, and the platform rejects tokens used outside their originating app context. Invalid or expired tokens are also handled more strictly. _(v59-lwc-016, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** The lightning-input base component's internal DOM structure is being modified in preparation for native shadow DOM, which may break code that queries or traverses its internal elements. _(v59-lwc-017, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Using NavigationMixin.Navigate from a modal no longer auto-closes the modal. With replace defaulting to false, modals now stack instead of closing, requiring explicit replace:true to restore the prior auto-close behavior. _(v59-lwc-018, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Static resources loaded via lightning/platformResourceLoader now execute inside the LWS sandbox in LWR sites, isolating global mutations within the component's namespace. Previously, custom loadScript implementations were needed to achieve sandbox isolation. _(v59-lwc-022, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** The REST Limits endpoint no longer returns MonthlyPlatformEventsUsageEntitlement for orgs without the high-volume platform events add-on, potentially breaking integrations that parse or depend on this field. _(v59-rest-003, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** GraphQL API displayValue field for Integer and Double types now returns null instead of formatted strings, aligning with UI API behavior. _(v59-rest-005, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce stops persisting implicit child share records between accounts and opportunities. Instead, opportunity access is evaluated at query time, which means SOQL queries and Apex tests that select from OpportunityShare expecting implicit child shares will return empty results. _(v59-sharing-001, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Cross-org redirections from your Salesforce org to other Salesforce orgs are blocked unless destination URLs are explicitly added to a Trusted URLs allowlist. Integrations or code redirecting users to external orgs will fail after enforcement. _(v59-sharing-002, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Query All Files permission now extends to ContentDocumentLink queries, allowing users with this permission plus View All Data to retrieve file share records across the entire org, including those in non-member libraries and unlisted groups. _(v59-soql-001, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** The sforce.one navigateToURL function no longer auto-closes modals by default; instead modals stack when isredirect is false, leaving the original modal open but inactive beneath new navigation targets. _(v59-vf-002, Winter '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** The lightning-input base component's internal DOM structure has been modified as part of Salesforce's transition toward native shadow DOM support. Tests or CSS selectors that depend on the component's internal element hierarchy will break. _(v60-lwc-012, Spring '24; supersedes v59-lwc-006)_
- **[behavior-change]** Type.forName() now consistently returns null when given an invalid namespace or when incorrectly using an outer class name as the namespace parameter, whereas previously the results were unpredictable. _(v60-apex-008, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Database.insertImmediate() and Database.insertAsync() methods now perform additional validation when called on non-external objects, potentially causing previously accepted calls to fail. _(v60-apex-014, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Type.forName() now returns null instead of throwing an exception when an invalid namespace is provided, changing error-handling behavior for code that relied on exceptions. _(v60-apex-015, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** MFA becomes the default login requirement for production orgs, meaning integrations or automated processes relying on direct UI login without MFA will be blocked after a 30-day grace period. _(v60-auth-001, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Headless identity APIs (registration, passwordless login, forgot password) now require email templates to be explicitly allowlisted via the new NetworkEmailTmplAllowlist metadata type; non-allowlisted templates in the emailtemplate parameter are rejected. _(v60-auth-007, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** The final phase of MFA auto-enablement activates for all remaining orgs in Spring '24, requiring users to authenticate with a second factor for all direct UI logins. Integrations using UI-based authentication flows may be affected if they rely on username/password-only login. _(v60-auth-016, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** When an API integration user exceeds 3,600 logins per hour and triggers rate limiting, Salesforce now stops recording individual Login History entries until the rate drops. Integrations relying on Login History for audit or monitoring may see gaps during rate-limited periods. _(v60-auth-017, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Bulk API 2.0 now dynamically splits failed batches into smaller chunks rather than using a fixed chunk size and marking them failed after retries. _(v60-bulk-003, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Flows initiated by bots will use the bot's associated user profile and permission sets to determine object and field-level access, rather than inheriting broader system permissions. _(v60-flow-001, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Four release updates affecting Flow runtime behavior are being re-enforced after accidental reversion in some orgs: REST API flows running in user context, Apex action access modifier enforcement, session ID access disablement, and partial save for invocable actions. _(v60-flow-003, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Process Builder processes with multiple criteria and record updates now correctly evaluate fields that started as null, fixing a bug where the original null value was not properly checked against criteria. _(v60-flow-007, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Chrome's storage partitioning takes effect for Salesforce domains in Summer '24, breaking cross-origin localStorage and sessionStorage access in third-party contexts. Custom components using these APIs across different origins will stop sharing storage. _(v60-lwc-001, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Web Security introduces new distortions for Selection and Document.execCommand APIs, while removing distortions for Element.attributes and several HTMLIFrameElement properties. LWC code using these browser APIs may behave differently under LWS. _(v60-lwc-009, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Web Security now silently converts any open shadow root to closed mode instead of throwing an error, preventing JavaScript access to shadow DOM internals. _(v60-lwc-010, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** 29 additional base Lightning components had their internal DOM structure modified in preparation for native shadow DOM support. Tests that query or assert against the internal element hierarchy of these components will break. _(v60-lwc-013, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Stacked modals from custom quick actions no longer trigger post-save navigation to the newly created record. Instead, users return to the originating record page after saving. _(v60-lwc-014, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Several base Lightning components have altered keyboard navigation and accessibility behaviors: lightning-modal now focuses the header title instead of the first interactive element, lightning-pill and lightning-pill-container switched from arrow-key to Tab-only navigation between focusable elements, and pill removal now only responds to Enter/Spacebar (not Delete/Backspace). _(v60-lwc-017, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** The NavigationMixin.Navigate replace property now affects post-save navigation in quick actions: when false, users return to the originating record page; when true, users navigate to the newly created record after save. _(v60-lwc-018, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce will modify the system-defined trusted URLs governing Content Security Policy for Experience Cloud sites in Winter '25, potentially blocking resources that rely on the current CSP allowlist. _(v60-lwc-020, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Operating Hours object's default sharing setting changes to Private, requiring orgs to verify or manually configure sharing settings. After configuration, specific IndustriesSettings Metadata API fields must be set to true for authenticated and guest users respectively. _(v60-rest-001, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** The legacy Salesforce API Only Systems Integration profile is discontinued for new orgs due to overly broad custom-object CRUD grants; a replacement Minimum Access - API Only Integrations profile ships with tighter defaults. _(v60-rest-007, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** The User Interface API records endpoints now support a handleOwnerChange parameter that returns a 204 status instead of an incorrect 404 when the caller loses record access during creation or update. _(v60-rest-014, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Decision table lookup Connect REST APIs now treat null as a distinct filter value, returning only rows matching the explicit null rather than combining null matches with other results. _(v60-rest-017, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** SCIM Users endpoints now return created and lastModified timestamps in 24-hour UTC format instead of 12-hour format, aligning with REST API conventions for the User object. _(v60-rest-020, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** New orgs created from February 8, 2024 onward no longer automatically expose records shared via Roles and Internal Subordinates to external Experience Cloud users. Pre-existing orgs retain the legacy behavior where such records are visible to portal users until manually remediated. _(v60-sharing-003, Spring '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Bulk REST API calls to invocable actions now use partial-save semantics: a single failure no longer rolls back the entire transaction. Instead, Salesforce retries successful actions up to three times and only rolls back the specific actions that fail. _(v62-rest-016, Winter '25; supersedes v61-rest-019, v60-rest-019)_
- **[behavior-change]** Calling getValidityLength(), setValidityLength(), getNbfClockSkew(), or setNbfClockSkew() on an Auth.JWT instance that was created via Auth.JWTUtil now throws a NoAccess exception, whereas previously these methods were callable. _(v61-apex-011, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** EventBus.publish() now throws System.UnexpectedException when you attempt to publish an sObject that is not a platform event, rather than failing silently or returning an error result. _(v61-apex-014, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Browser vendors are phasing out third-party cookies, which will break authenticated Visualforce pages loaded in iframes on external sites and Lightning Out deployments that rely on Salesforce session cookies rather than token-based auth. _(v61-auth-001, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** New production orgs now enforce MFA by default for direct UI logins. Users logging in with username/password must provide a second factor (authenticator app, security key, or built-in authenticator). A 30-day grace period allows users to skip MFA initially. _(v61-auth-002, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Auth.JWT.getAdditionalClaims() method now returns claims from JWTs created via Auth.JWTUtil, with nested list structures serialized as JSON strings requiring explicit parsing into maps. _(v61-auth-004, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Embedded Login for Experience Cloud sites is now disabled by default. Organizations relying on this authentication method must explicitly re-enable it in the Login & Registration settings. _(v61-auth-009, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** OAuth 2.0 device flow now requires user approval on every flow initiation, even if the user previously authorized the application. Apps relying on cached authorization for the device flow will now see approval prompts on each use. _(v61-auth-013, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Autolaunched flows triggered by Apex will inherit the sharing rules of the calling Apex class when that class uses 'with sharing', instead of running with full system access. _(v61-flow-001, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Experience modals migrate from Aura to LWC rendering, altering navigation and button behavior. The Save & New button disappears on lookup-initiated record creation, post-save navigation stops firing for custom quick action modals, and stacked modal saves return to the originating record page rather than navigating to the newly created record. _(v61-lwc-001, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Chrome storage partitioning activates for Salesforce domains, breaking cross-origin localStorage and sessionStorage access in third-party contexts such as embedded iframes or Canvas apps. _(v61-lwc-002, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** List view URLs now use the list view's API Name instead of its internal ID, and the Recently Viewed list uses __Recent rather than Recent as the filter parameter. Integrations or automations that parse list view URLs will break. _(v61-lwc-003, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce is altering the internal DOM structure and SLDS styling of base Lightning components. Components that rely on unsupported techniques—such as targeting internal DOM elements via CSS selectors, manipulating Salesforce component internals with JavaScript, or asserting on SLDS classes in unit tests—may experience visual regressions or test failures. _(v61-lwc-006, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce has indefinitely paused the automatic rollout of Lightning Web Security that began in Spring '22. Orgs where LWS was not yet auto-enabled will remain on the legacy Locker Service until Salesforce resumes the rollout. _(v61-lwc-008, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Web Security adds new distortions for Window.requestFileSystem and Window.webkitRequestFileSystem, and modifies existing distortions for custom element registration, shadow DOM attachment, shadowRoot access, and iframe/object source setters. _(v61-lwc-009, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Multiple base Lightning Web Components have modified their DOM structure and ARIA attributes for accessibility compliance, which may break tests or code that queries specific elements or relies on particular attribute values. _(v61-lwc-010, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce is restructuring the internal implementation of SLDS styles, custom properties, and Lightning components in LWR and Aura sites. Sites that override CSS on Salesforce components using unsupported techniques may experience visual regressions in future releases. _(v61-lwc-012, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** CustomField metadata retrieval and deployment on Data Cloud objects now returns only a subset of field attributes depending on the custom field's data type, rather than all standard CustomField properties. _(v61-packaging-005, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Flows executed via REST API will run using the calling user's profile, permission sets, and sharing rules rather than system context, limiting data access to what the user is permitted to see. _(v61-rest-001, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** The OpenAPI Spec sObjects REST API now requires a different URI pattern ending in /locatorID/results to retrieve documents, and POST responses return a 202 with URIs instead of the document directly. Repeated requests within 6 hours now return HTTP 429 instead of 202. _(v61-rest-004, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Logout event type now captures session revocations beyond manual logouts, including connected app access revocations and calls to the Salesforce revocation endpoint. _(v61-rest-009, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Orgs provisioned from Summer '24 onward have Connect REST API calls counted against the 24-hour org-wide Platform API limit instead of the per-user/per-app/per-hour Connect limit, except for Chatter-specific requests which remain on the old limit. _(v61-rest-011, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Messaging for Web launchChat() utility API now forces the chat window to maximize on every invocation, whereas previously it only maximized on the first call and respected a user's minimized state on subsequent calls. _(v61-rest-020, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** SOQL parser returns different error codes and messages for malformed queries, replacing INVALID_QUERY_FILTER_OPERATOR with MALFORMED_QUERY and altering the text of various parse-error diagnostics. _(v61-soql-003, Summer '24)_
- **[behavior-change]** Template-triggered prompt flows can no longer reference flex prompt template types; they must use manual inputs instead, requiring migration of existing flows. _(v63-flow-003, Spring '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** Aura quick actions that previously stayed on the originating record page after save will now redirect to the newly created record. LWC modals stack by default, requiring `replace: true` in lightning/navigation to close previous modals and redirect. _(v63-lwc-002, Spring '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** Connect REST API calls are transitioning from per-user/per-app/per-hour throttling to the org-wide 24-hour Salesforce Platform API limit pool. After migration, only Chatter-dependent requests remain under the old per-user quotas. _(v64-rest-011, Summer '25; supersedes v62-rest-011)_
- **[behavior-change]** ConnectApi rate limiting shifts from per-user/namespace/hour quotas to the org-wide 24-hour Platform API limit for most methods, except those requiring Chatter which retain the old model. _(v65-apex-008, Winter '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** Apex batch action results will return in the same sequence as the original requests rather than grouping errors first and successes last. _(v65-apex-014, Winter '26; supersedes v62-flow-012, v61-flow-010)_
- **[behavior-change]** Apex classes used as invocable action parameters will be required to have an accessible no-argument constructor; classes lacking one will fail at runtime once the release update is enforced. _(v66-apex-001, Spring '26; supersedes v65-apex-001)_
- **[behavior-change]** ConnectApi method calls are moving from per-user/namespace/hour rate limits to the org-wide 24-hour Salesforce Platform API limit. Only Chatter-dependent methods retain the old per-user throttling. _(v66-apex-010, Spring '26; supersedes v62-apex-006)_
- **[behavior-change]** Connect REST API rate limiting is shifting from per-user/per-app/per-hour quotas to the standard Salesforce Platform API per-org/per-24-hour model. Only Chatter-dependent requests will continue using the legacy per-user rate limit. _(v66-rest-017, Spring '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** Connect REST API calls are transitioning from per-user/per-app/per-hour rate limits to the org-wide 24-hour Salesforce Platform API limit. Only Chatter-dependent requests retain the old per-user throttling model. _(v66-rest-018, Spring '26; supersedes v65-rest-012, v63-rest-016)_
- **[behavior-change]** An optional release update requires classes passed as invocable-action inputs to expose a reachable zero-argument constructor, and grants access to some built-in classes for that purpose. _(v67-apex-005, Summer '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** ConnectApi method calls now count against the org-wide 24-hour Platform API limit instead of the previous per-user, per-namespace, per-hour quota, except for Chatter-specific methods which retain the old rate limit model. _(v67-apex-018, Summer '26; supersedes v61-rest-007)_
- **[behavior-change]** Order product updates now trigger custom application logic (Apex triggers, validation rules, flows, workflow rules) on the parent Order record. Previously this logic was not correctly evaluated on parent orders. _(v62-apex-009, Winter '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** The lightning:datatable wrapTableHeader attribute now accepts string values ('all', 'none', 'by-column') instead of boolean, enabling per-column header wrapping control. Existing boolean values may need migration. _(v62-aura-001, Winter '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** Named credentials for Event Relay now enforce uppercase AWS region codes. Creating a new credential with a lowercase or mixed-case region (e.g., us-west-2) will fail validation. _(v62-auth-002, Winter '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** Aura quick actions that launch modals now redirect to the newly created record after save, instead of returning to the originating page. LWC stacked modals return to the original page by default, but non-stacked LWC quick actions redirect to the new record. _(v62-lwc-001, Winter '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Web Security now distorts three additional browser APIs: DataTransfer.moz* properties (Firefox), Document.prototype.parseHTMLUnsafe, and Element.prototype.setHTMLUnsafe. Code relying on these APIs will encounter altered behavior under LWS. _(v62-lwc-007, Winter '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** Eight additional base Lightning components (checkbox-group, map, progress-indicator, progress-step, relative-date-time, slider, tile, tree) have modified their internal DOM structure in preparation for native shadow DOM adoption, potentially breaking tests that query internal elements. _(v62-lwc-008, Winter '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** The wrap-table-header attribute on lightning-datatable changed from boolean to string type, accepting 'all', 'none', or 'by-column' values with 'none' as default. _(v62-lwc-010, Winter '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** Newly created platform events now default their Publish Behavior field to Publish Immediately instead of Publish After Commit, which changes when events fire relative to transaction commit boundaries. _(v62-packaging-002, Winter '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** The contentKey field on EnablementProgramTaskCmsContent is no longer functional; the apiName field must be used instead for CMS content references in enablement programs. _(v62-packaging-004, Winter '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** When an LWR site is upgraded to enhanced status, its metadata representation switches from ExperienceBundle to DigitalExperienceBundle and DigitalExperienceConfig types, which affects deployment pipelines and metadata retrieval operations. _(v62-packaging-005, Winter '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** The underlying HTTP library for Salesforce Connect's OData 2.0 adapter is upgraded to OData4J Jersey 2.4.2, which may alter HTTP response handling for external data sources and external objects. _(v62-rest-001, Winter '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** A new service protection limit now caps how many Metadata API deployments can be queued simultaneously when initiated from Apex code. Previously unlimited, this throttle may cause deployment failures if your automation enqueues many concurrent deploy requests. _(v62-rest-003, Winter '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** CORS allowlist rules configured for your My Domain now extend to APIs served from api.salesforce.com, meaning browser-based integrations calling that domain will be blocked unless their origin is explicitly allowlisted. _(v62-rest-004, Winter '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** Several Salesforce CMS Connect REST response bodies have removed properties (channelId, channelName, channelType, domain, domainName, isChannelSearchable, isDomainLocked, domainUrl, resourceUrl, target, channelInfo) and replaced them with new equivalents (id, name, type, isSearchable, managedContentChannelDomain, channelSummary, url). Integrations parsing these responses must update field references. _(v62-rest-013, Winter '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** Starting Spring '25, the ActivationUserGroupId field becomes mandatory on SandboxInfo when creating or refreshing Developer or Developer Pro sandboxes. Orgs using API versions below 60.0 will lose the ability to provision these sandbox types. _(v62-rest-014, Winter '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** When enabled, REST API calls invoking Apex actions now roll back all database changes if the action throws an exception, preserving transactional integrity instead of leaving partial commits. _(v62-rest-015, Winter '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** When digital experiences are enabled in preview sandboxes, sharing rules using 'Roles and Subordinates' now restrict record access to internal users only, renaming the group to 'Roles and Internal Subordinates'. External site users no longer automatically inherit records shared this way. _(v62-sharing-001, Winter '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** A per-user search rate limit now caps SOSL, Apex search, and REST search at 3,000 queries and 200,000 ms cumulative CPU within any rolling 5-minute window; exceeding either threshold triggers an error. _(v62-soql-001, Winter '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** A new Data Access Level setting restricts SOQL queries against Data Cloud data so that results are filtered based on the user's access to parent objects. When enabled, Data Cloud queries honor parent object permissions. _(v62-soql-002, Winter '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** Dynamic SOQL error messages have been rewritten to provide clearer context about what token caused the parse failure, and negative currency literals are now supported in multi-currency orgs. _(v62-soql-003, Winter '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** SOQL error messages and query behavior have been modified in this release, which may break code that parses specific error strings or depends on previous query semantics. _(v62-soql-004, Winter '25, low confidence)_
- **[behavior-change]** The SLDS modal close button blueprint now uses a gray icon with white background instead of an inverse white icon, requiring removal of slds-button_icon-inverse from modal close button markup to match the new default styling. _(v63-lwc-009, Spring '25; supersedes v62-lwc-009)_
- **[behavior-change]** Apex batch action results will return in request order rather than grouping errors first and successes last, potentially affecting code that relies on the current ordering behavior. _(v63-apex-001, Spring '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** The release update that would have guaranteed Apex batch action results are returned in request order has been indefinitely postponed and disabled in all orgs due to performance issues. The toggle to enable this behavior currently has no effect. _(v63-apex-002, Spring '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce reversed its plan to auto-enforce rollbacks when Apex invocable actions throw exceptions via REST API. The update remains opt-in only, preserving transaction integrity by discarding DML if an exception occurs. _(v63-apex-014, Spring '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** The /services/oauth2/authorize endpoint now surfaces Apex exceptions from the HeadlessSelfRegistrationHandler in API error responses via a new apex_error field, rather than only logging them to debug logs. _(v63-auth-006, Spring '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** JWT-based access tokens now create server-side sessions, enabling admins to view and revoke them via Session Management. Integrations using JWT bearer flow may have tokens invalidated mid-flight if an admin terminates the backing session. _(v63-auth-007, Spring '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** Embedded Login settings are now hidden by default for new Experience Cloud sites; orgs relying on this authentication method must contact Salesforce support to re-enable it before configuring. _(v63-auth-012, Spring '25)_

- **[behavior-change]** Email-to-Case flows triggered via Omni-Channel are now executed synchronously rather than asynchronously, which may affect processing order and error handling behavior. _(v63-flow-002, Spring '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** The requiresAsyncProcessing field on FlowStageStep metadata is now ignored because background steps automatically detect whether their associated flow needs synchronous or asynchronous execution. _(v63-flow-006, Spring '25)_
- **[behavior-change]** A Release Update enables stacked modals for Lightning Web Components, changing how modal dialogs layer and interact when multiple modals are opened. _(v63-lwc-001, Spring '25)_

- **[behavior-change]** ICU locale formats replace JDK formats for dates, times, currencies, addresses, names, and numbers. Integrations that depend on specific JDK locale output strings may break when the org switches or when Salesforce eventually enforces the change. _(v65-other-008, Winter '26)_

- **[behavior-change]** Rebate Management payout calculations now use higher-precision decimal arithmetic, which changes the exact numeric values returned by APIs and stored in records. Previously rounded amounts may differ from newly calculated ones. _(v65-rest-018, Winter '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Apex Blob.toPdf() method will switch to using the Visualforce PDF rendering engine, which supports additional fonts and multibyte characters. PDFs generated via this method may render differently after enforcement. _(v66-apex-002, Spring '26)_

- **[behavior-change]** The lightning:combobox component now properly integrates with form validation, allowing browsers to focus it automatically when invalid values are submitted. _(v66-aura-003, Spring '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** Industry-wide TLS certificate maximum lifespans are shrinking dramatically over the next three years, requiring integrations that pin or manually manage certificates to adopt automated rotation. Salesforce will also discontinue proactive certificate rotation announcements for production orgs. _(v66-auth-002, Spring '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** Creating new connected apps is no longer possible as of Spring '26. Developers must use the External Client App framework instead for any new integrations requiring OAuth scopes like chatbot_api, sfap_api, or api. _(v66-auth-007, Spring '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** When the new IP allowlist enforcement is enabled, OAuth refresh token exchanges from IP addresses outside the configured ranges will be rejected, causing existing integrations to fail if they call from unlisted IPs. _(v66-auth-025, Spring '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** Refresh tokens for external client apps and connected apps now expire after 30 days of inactivity, even if the configured policy was 'valid until revoked' or set to a longer period. Each token use resets the 30-day window. _(v66-auth-026, Spring '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce will require users to complete step-up authentication (identity verification) before performing sensitive actions like report exports, even for SSO users who must register a Salesforce-native verification method. _(v66-auth-027, Spring '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** Apex batch action results in Flows will return in submission order rather than grouping errors first, which may break downstream logic that depends on the current error-first ordering. _(v66-flow-007, Spring '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** LWC framework now skips rehydration for DOM nodes that are disconnected, preventing lifecycle hooks such as renderedCallback from executing on detached components. Code relying on the old behavior where detached nodes could still trigger reactive updates may break. _(v66-lwc-003, Spring '26)_

- **[behavior-change]** Apex classes used as invocable action parameters must now expose a visible no-argument constructor. For non-packaged classes this means public; for managed-package classes called from outside the package it must be global. Without this, Flow invocable actions referencing the class will fail. _(v67-apex-008, Summer '26)_

- **[behavior-change]** Aura action responses will no longer include non-public system fields from custom objects. Internal system fields that aren't exposed through the public API get filtered out of returned data. _(v67-aura-001, Summer '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce is requiring more frequent certificate rotation, more frequent domain validation, and mTLS certificate updates—integrations relying on certificates or custom domains must update their credential management processes. _(v67-auth-001, Summer '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** Industry-mandated TLS certificate lifespan reductions require integrations using certificate pinning or manually managed certificates to implement more frequent rotation cycles, and Salesforce will discontinue public certificate rotation announcements after July 6, 2026. _(v67-auth-005, Summer '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** Salesforce introduces step-up authentication that will require periodic re-authentication during sensitive setup actions like report operations. - **[behavior-change]** Apex batch action results in Flows will be sorted to match the original request order rather than arbitrary order, which may affect downstream logic relying on previous ordering. _(v67-flow-001, Summer '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** Apex batch action results returned to Flows will preserve the original request submission order instead of grouping errors first and successes last. _(v67-flow-003, Summer '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** Lightning Web Security introduces additional distortions that restrict or modify how certain web APIs behave within LWC components, potentially breaking code relying on undistorted browser API behavior. _(v67-lwc-006, Summer '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** New orgs have Chatter disabled by default, which blocks creating Customer Service template Aura sites and adding feed components to Aura/LWR sites until Chatter is manually enabled. _(v67-lwc-009, Summer '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** Connect REST API rate limiting has shifted from per-user/per-app/per-hour quotas to the standard org-wide 24-hour Platform API limit for most calls, with only Chatter-specific requests still subject to the older per-user throttling. _(v67-rest-017, Summer '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** Connect REST API rate limiting now follows the org-wide 24-hour Salesforce Platform API limit for most requests, rather than the previous per-user, per-app, per-hour model. Only Chatter-specific requests remain under the old per-user hourly limits. _(v67-rest-018, Summer '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** The checkout-to-order Connect REST endpoint now checks for pre-existing Order Summaries and rejects the request with a rollback if one already exists, preventing duplicate orders during payment retry scenarios. _(v67-rest-019, Summer '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Commerce Subscription Renew Connect REST endpoint now accepts multiple subscription IDs in a single request, enabling bulk renewal without needing to contact support for enablement. _(v67-rest-020, Summer '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Data Clean Room Collaboration Output response body removes the dataSpaceName property, replacing it with a richer dataSpace object containing ID, name, label, and filter fields. _(v67-rest-021, Summer '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** The DoesIncludeBosses field on the Group object now supports queues, allowing integrations to control whether queue-shared records propagate up the role hierarchy. _(v67-rest-022, Summer '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** The Create Standalone Billing Schedules Connect REST API now accepts minimal intent-based payloads for amendments, renewals, and cancellations, automatically computing required fields like unit price and total price from historical context or billing schedule group ID when omitted. _(v67-rest-026, Summer '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** Einstein Conversation Insights data migrates to native Salesforce objects, making call transcripts and AI insights queryable via SOQL and accessible in Flow, Apex, and Prompt Builder for the first time. _(v67-rest-027, Summer '26)_
- **[behavior-change]** A new 'Use Any API Auth' permission now gates SOAP API login() calls. New orgs enforce this by default, meaning users without the permission cannot authenticate via SOAP login(). _(v67-soap-002, Summer '26)_

- **[retirement]** Salesforce is discontinuing its managed OAuth app for Twitter/X authentication. Organizations using Twitter SSO for Experience Cloud sites must configure their own Twitter developer app credentials to maintain login functionality. _(v60-auth-003, Spring '24)_
- **[retirement]** Service account OAuth 2.0 authentication using Exchange ApplicationImpersonation for Einstein Activity Capture connections to Microsoft 365 is being phased out. Microsoft will block new role assignments in May 2024, and Salesforce retires existing connections in Spring '25. _(v60-auth-004, Spring '24)_
- **[retirement]** Salesforce stops hosting the managed Twitter/X OAuth app, so any authentication provider using the implicit consumer key/secret will fail. You must register your own app on the X developer platform and supply explicit credentials. _(v60-auth-008, Spring '24)_
- **[retirement]** The Ant Migration Tool is officially retired and no longer receives updates or support, though it remains functional. Teams still using it for metadata deployments should migrate to Salesforce CLI. _(v60-packaging-002, Spring '24)_
- **[retirement]** Streaming API versions 23.0–36.0 will stop working in Winter '25. These legacy versions lack Durable Streaming capabilities introduced in v37.0 and are no longer receiving fixes or enhancements. _(v60-rest-010, Spring '24)_
- **[retirement]** Salesforce is retiring the legacy single-configuration SAML framework. Orgs still using it must migrate to the multiple-configuration SAML framework before Summer '26 enforcement, or their SAML SSO will stop working entirely. _(v66-auth-020, Spring '26; supersedes v62-auth-010)_
- **[retirement]** Salesforce Functions will cease to operate on January 31, 2025. Organizations using Functions must migrate workloads to an alternative compute solution before that date or lose the capability entirely. _(v61-other-001, Summer '24)_
- **[retirement]** The Engage for Gmail Chrome extension built on Manifest V2 is scheduled for retirement in June 2024 due to Google deprecating Manifest V2. Organizations using this integration must migrate to the Account Engagement Sales Email & Alerts feature within Salesforce. _(v61-other-003, Summer '24)_
- **[retirement]** Legacy standard-volume platform events face retirement in Summer '25. Organizations still using these older event types must migrate to high-volume platform events before the retirement date. _(v61-rest-005, Summer '24)_
- **[retirement]** The Share Visit feature in Consumer Goods Cloud will be removed in Spring '25, eliminating automatic visit sharing. After retirement, visit access reverts to standard platform behavior where only the record owner has access unless custom sharing is implemented. _(v61-sharing-001, Summer '24)_
- **[retirement]** The Classic Knowledge data model is being retired in Summer '25. Custom Visualforce pages or components that reference article types must be refactored to use the Lightning Knowledge data model's record types instead. _(v62-other-003, Winter '25; supersedes v61-other-004)_
- **[retirement]** Shared domain certificates for Experience Cloud CDN are being retired. Sites still using shared certificates will stop functioning when enforcement occurs in Spring '26. _(v64-auth-005, Summer '25)_
- **[retirement]** Salesforce Functions is being discontinued. Organizations currently using Functions must migrate to an alternative compute solution before their subscription expires or lose that capability entirely. _(v66-other-008, Spring '26; supersedes v65-other-009)_
- **[retirement]** Process Builder automations used by Marketing Cloud Connect are automatically converted to record-triggered flows when associated journeys are stopped or published, completing a retirement that began rolling out in early 2024. _(v62-flow-003, Winter '25)_
- **[retirement]** Salesforce Functions, the service allowing Apex to invoke serverless compute on Heroku infrastructure, will cease operation on January 31, 2025. Any org-to-function invocations will fail after that date. _(v62-other-002, Winter '25)_
- **[retirement]** Standard-volume platform events, which have been legacy since API 45.0 (Spring '19) when only high-volume events became definable, will stop working entirely in Summer '25. After that date, publish and subscribe operations against any remaining standard-volume events will fail. _(v62-rest-008, Winter '25)_
- **[retirement]** The Apex class that invokes the Penny Perfect Pricing V1 batch process in the Consumer Goods Cloud managed package will stop functioning after the Winter '26 release. Any scheduled jobs or direct calls to this batch class will fail. _(v63-apex-011, Spring '25)_

Organizations must migrate to org-level OAuth 2.0 before February 2025 or lose sync functionality. _(v63-auth-004, Spring '25)_

- **[deprecation]** The $A.run() method is deprecated in favor of $A.getCallback() for wrapping asynchronous code that accesses components outside the standard rerendering lifecycle. _(v35-aura-006, Winter '16)_

- **[deprecation]** The Auth.SessionManagement methods validateTotpTokenForKey and validateTotpTokenForUser that lack a description parameter are deprecated in favor of new overloads requiring a description argument. _(v36-auth-008, Spring '16)_

- **[deprecation]** The describeFlexiPages() SOAP API call will be deprecated in v39.0; developers should migrate to Metadata API or Tooling API for FlexiPage introspection. _(v38-soap-002, Winter '17)_
- **[deprecation]** The useAppcache attribute on <aura:application> tags is deprecated following browser vendors' deprecation of the AppCache API. Standalone Aura apps using this attribute may encounter cross-browser issues. _(v39-aura-004, Spring '17)_
- **[deprecation]** The Auth.AuthProviderPlugin interface is deprecated in favor of a new abstract class replacement for custom authentication provider implementations. _(v39-auth-004, Spring '17)_
- **[deprecation]** EmailTemplate.EntityType field is deprecated in favor of RelatedEntityType; existing integrations should migrate to the new field. _(v39-rest-006, Spring '17)_
- **[deprecation]** The transform methods in Databinding.ObjectMapper are now deprecated and scheduled for removal in a future release. _(v39-rest-012, Spring '17)_
- **[deprecation]** The force:recordPreview component is deprecated and replaced by force:recordData. The new component returns records in a different structure based on the User Interface API, requiring migration of any code that reads the targetRecord attribute. _(v40-aura-005, Summer '17)_
- **[deprecation]** The useAppcache attribute on <aura:application> is deprecated because browser vendors have dropped AppCache support. Standalone Aura apps using this attribute may encounter cross-browser issues. _(v40-aura-009, Summer '17)_
- **[deprecation]** The langLocale attribute on ui:inputDate, ui:inputDateTime, ui:outputDate, and ui:outputDateTime is deprecated. Validation now restricts langLocale to values matching the user's Language or Locale settings; mismatched values fall back to the user's Language setting. _(v40-aura-010, Summer '17)_
- **[deprecation]** The addHandler() method for dynamically attaching event handlers in Aura components is deprecated; use Component.addEventHandler() instead. _(v40-aura-012, Summer '17)_
- **[deprecation]** The loginURL query parameter is deprecated starting Winter '18. Integrations using this parameter for authentication redirects should migrate to supported alternatives. _(v40-auth-004, Summer '17)_
- **[deprecation]** Using wildcards in aura:dependency tags is now deprecated because they can trigger validation errors when no resources match and degrade performance by sending unnecessary definitions to the client. _(v41-aura-010, Winter '18)_
- **[deprecation]** The SAQL toString(date, formatString) function is renamed to date_to_string() and will be deprecated in a future release; existing usage continues to work for now. _(v41-other-001, Winter '18)_
- **[deprecation]** The SFDX_DISABLE_ENCRYPTION environment variable is deprecated and will stop working in Spring '18. Orgs using this variable must unset it and reauthorize all connected orgs before the Spring '18 release. _(v41-packaging-004, Winter '18)_
- **[deprecation]** Einstein Platform Services APIs have moved from api.metamind.io to api.einstein.ai. The legacy endpoint remains functional but is slated for deprecation. _(v41-rest-005, Winter '18)_
- **[deprecation]** Several Einstein Image Classification REST endpoints for managing labels and examples are deprecated in API version 2.0; labels must now be provided at dataset creation time instead of added afterward. _(v41-rest-009, Winter '18)_
- **[deprecation]** The CustomBrandAsset.ForeignKeyAssetId field is deprecated and replaced by the new AssetSourceId field. _(v41-rest-010, Winter '18)_
- **[deprecation]** The source=lightningSubscribe query parameter on the analytics/notifications endpoint is deprecated across all API versions; callers should migrate to source=lightningReportSubscribe. _(v41-rest-011, Winter '18)_

- **[deprecation]** The api.metamind.io endpoint for Einstein Platform Services is being deprecated and must be replaced with api.einstein.ai in all integrations. _(v42-rest-005, Spring '18)_
- **[deprecation]** The Reports and Dashboards REST API bucket object property 'devloperName' (misspelled) is deprecated starting in v42.0; use the corrected 'developerName' property instead. _(v42-rest-010, Spring '18)_
- **[deprecation]** The force:navigateToComponent event is deprecated in favor of lightning:navigation with pageReference and the lightning:isUrlAddressable interface, which provides cleaner URLs and explicit control over navigable components. _(v43-aura-005, Summer '18)_
- **[deprecation]** Several Aura system events are deprecated: aura:doneRendering (use render event instead), aura:doneWaiting and aura:waiting (use action callback response status instead), and force:navigateToComponent (use lightning:isUrlAddressable with lightning:navigation instead due to XSS vulnerability from base64 encoding). _(v43-aura-010, Summer '18)_
- **[deprecation]** The force:package2 CLI commands for second-generation packaging are being replaced by force:package commands and will be removed in Winter '19. _(v43-packaging-005, Summer '18)_
- **[deprecation]** The Subscription Conversion field on Order and the Full-Term Net Unit Price field on Order Product are now deprecated in Salesforce CPQ. Integrations or code referencing these fields should prepare for their eventual removal. _(v43-rest-001, Summer '18)_
- **[deprecation]** The lens representation in the Wave REST API now uses a datasets array property for multi-dataset support, deprecating the singular dataset property. _(v43-rest-002, Summer '18)_
- **[deprecation]** The orgPreferences format in scratch org definition files is deprecated in favor of the new settings format, with removal planned for Spring '19. _(v44-packaging-006, Winter '19)_
- **[deprecation]** Aura component attributes of type Array, Set, or List now require square brackets around default values. Omitting the brackets is deprecated and may cause unpredictable runtime behavior. _(v45-aura-004, Spring '19)_
- **[deprecation]** The standard__namedPage pageReference type for lightning:navigation is deprecated in Lightning Communities; use comm__namedPage instead. _(v46-aura-004, Summer '19)_
- **[deprecation]** The icon-class attribute on lightning-button-icon is deprecated because Shadow DOM encapsulation prevents external CSS from reaching the internal SVG element. _(v46-lwc-005, Summer '19)_
- **[deprecation]** The SalesWave and ServiceWave scratch org features are deprecated; developers must migrate to DevelopmentWave in scratch org definition files. _(v46-packaging-004, Summer '19)_
- **[deprecation]** The UI_RENDER_TIME field in Einstein Analytics event logs is deprecated starting in API version 46.0; use the EPT field from the wave performance event type instead. _(v46-rest-012, Summer '19)_
- **[deprecation]** The $Site.AdminEmailAddress merge field now returns an empty string for all sites. Code relying on this field to retrieve the site administrator's email must switch to SOQL queries against the Site or User objects. _(v46-vf-001, Summer '19)_
- **[deprecation]** The Jest testing package for Lightning Web Components was renamed from lwc-jest to sfdx-lwc-jest. The old package name continues to function through Winter '20 but should be migrated. _(v47-lwc-004, Winter '20)_
- **[deprecation]** The NavigationLinkSet subtype on Network metadata is deprecated starting in API 47.0 and replaced by the NavigationMenu type. _(v47-packaging-011, Winter '20)_
- **[deprecation]** OrgPreferenceSettings metadata type is deprecated in API 47.0 and scheduled for removal in API 48.0; dozens of new granular settings types replace it. _(v47-packaging-013, Winter '20)_
- **[deprecation]** The uiType property in the User Interface API App response is deprecated in favor of the new appType property, which distinguishes Classic, Community, Connected, and Lightning app types. _(v47-rest-017, Winter '20)_
- **[deprecation]** The RevisionNum field on SourceMember is deprecated in favor of RevisionCounter, which maintains a continuous count even after pushing source to a scratch org. _(v47-rest-018, Winter '20)_
- **[deprecation]** The RenewalChannel field on the Claim object and the FnolChannel field on the InsurancePolicy object are deprecated starting in API version 48.0 and scheduled for removal in API version 52.0 (Summer '21). _(v48-rest-010, Spring '20)_
- **[deprecation]** The FnolChannel field on InsurancePolicy is deprecated and will be removed in API version 52.0. Integrations using this field should migrate before Summer '21. _(v48-rest-011, Spring '20)_
- **[deprecation]** All Aura components in the ui namespace (ui:button, ui:inputText, ui:menu, etc.) are deprecated and will lose official support on May 1, 2021. Existing code continues to function but Salesforce will no longer accept support cases after that date. _(v49-aura-001, Summer '20)_
- **[deprecation]** The force:lightning:test:* commands (create, install, run) are deprecated in favor of the new force:lightning:lwc:test:* equivalents. These older commands will be removed in a future CLI release. _(v49-packaging-011, Summer '20)_
- **[deprecation]** The Cases.getCaseIdFromEmailThreadId() method is deprecated in favor of the new getCaseIdFromEmailHeaders method, which provides enhanced security for Email-to-Case threading. _(v50-apex-013, Winter '21)_
- **[deprecation]** All Aura components in the ui namespace (ui:button, ui:inputText, ui:menu, etc.) are deprecated with official support ending May 1, 2021. The components remain functional but unsupported after that date. _(v50-aura-002, Winter '21)_
- **[deprecation]** The SLDS class .slds-form_compound is deprecated in favor of .slds-form-element_compound for compound form layouts in the Datetime Picker blueprint. _(v50-lwc-007, Winter '21)_
- **[deprecation]** The ContactsToMultipleAccounts scratch org feature is deprecated and must be replaced with the enableRelateContactToMultipleAccounts account setting in your scratch org definition file. _(v50-packaging-007, Winter '21)_
- **[deprecation]** Legacy External Services registrations (both OpenAPI and Interagent hyper-schema formats) are being phased out ahead of planned retirement in Summer '21. Orgs must migrate legacy registrations to the current External Services version. _(v50-rest-009, Winter '21)_
- **[deprecation]** The Einstein Vision REST endpoint for retrieving examples by label ID via query parameter is deprecated and replaced with a path-based endpoint structure that includes both dataset ID and label ID as path resources. _(v50-rest-010, Winter '21; supersedes v50-rest-011)_
- **[deprecation]** All Aura components in the ui namespace (ui:button, ui:inputText, ui:menu, etc.) lose official support on May 1, 2021. After that date Salesforce will not accept support cases, though the components continue to function. _(v51-aura-002, Spring '21)_
- **[deprecation]** The System.Site.getBaseInsecureUrl() method is now deprecated; code calling it will continue to work but should migrate to secure URL alternatives. _(v52-apex-006, Summer '21)_
- **[deprecation]** All Aura components in the ui namespace lose official support after May 1, 2021. They continue to function but Salesforce will not accept support cases for issues with them. _(v52-aura-001, Summer '21)_
- **[deprecation]** Identity Connect versions 2.1 and 3.0.1.2 are deprecated and no longer available for download; organizations using these versions for Active Directory synchronization must plan migration to Identity Connect 7. _(v52-auth-009, Summer '21)_
- **[deprecation]** The Order Summary History component in B2B Commerce is deprecated and replaced by the Order List component, which offers filtering, sorting by date, and finer display control. _(v52-lwc-001, Summer '21)_
- **[deprecation]** The lightning/uiListApi module and its getListUi wire adapter are deprecated and will no longer receive updates. Developers should migrate to lightning/uiListsApi with getListInfoByName instead. _(v52-lwc-009, Summer '21)_
- **[deprecation]** Platform API versions 20.0 and earlier are now deprecated across SOAP API (7.0–20.0), REST API (20.0), and Bulk API (16.0–20.0). These endpoints will be retired and stop functioning entirely when Summer '22 releases. _(v52-rest-003, Summer '21)_
- **[deprecation]** The CollabUserEngmtRecordLink object linking Quip engagement metrics to Salesforce records is deprecated and will be retired. Integrations querying this object must migrate to joining user engagements and document metrics records tables in Tableau CRM. _(v53-rest-013, Winter '22)_
- **[deprecation]** The Hide Personal Information setting is deprecated and will be retired in Winter '23, replaced by the more configurable Enhanced Personal Information Management permission that controls external user access to 20 personal fields on User records. _(v53-sharing-001, Winter '22)_
- **[deprecation]** Several wire adapters and functions in lightning/uiRecordApi are deprecated: getRecordUi, getRecordInput, and refresh. Additionally, refreshApex from @salesforce/apex is deprecated for non-Apex wire adapter usage. _(v55-lwc-007, Summer '22)_
- **[deprecation]** Salesforce is discouraging use of the OAuth 2.0 username-password flow due to security concerns and recommends migrating integrations to client credentials, JWT bearer, or web server flows instead. _(v56-auth-011, Winter '23)_
- **[deprecation]** Several lightning/uiRecordApi wire adapters and functions are deprecated: getRecordUi, getRecordInput, and refresh. Developers should migrate to base record components or alternative methods like getRecord, getRecords, refreshApex, or getRecordNotifyChange. _(v56-lwc-011, Winter '23)_
- **[deprecation]** Salesforce now blocks the creation of new Workflow Rules in production orgs as part of the retirement path, though existing rules can still be edited, activated, or deactivated. Developer orgs retain creation capability for managed package development. _(v56-packaging-003, Winter '23)_
- **[deprecation]** The if:true and if:false template directives are deprecated in favor of lwc:if, lwc:elseif, and lwc:else. Salesforce intends to remove the legacy directives in a future release. _(v57-lwc-007, Spring '23)_
- **[deprecation]** Several lightning/uiRecordApi functions and wire adapters are now deprecated: getRecordNotifyChange (replaced by notifyRecordUpdateAvailable), getRecordUi (replaced by base form components or getRecord/getRecords), getRecordInput (replaced by manual record object construction), and refresh (replaced by refreshApex or notifyRecordUpdateAvailable). _(v57-lwc-011, Spring '23)_
- **[deprecation]** The logGoalAchieved enum on BotInvocation's invocationActionType field is deprecated starting in API 57.0; use the new conversationGoals and conversationStepGoalMappings fields instead for bot dialog goals. _(v57-packaging-003, Spring '23)_
- **[deprecation]** Legacy U2F security keys are being migrated to WebAuthn. Keys registered before Summer '22 require one login before Winter '24 to auto-upgrade; otherwise they must be disconnected and re-registered. _(v58-auth-010, Summer '23)_
- **[deprecation]** The BarcodeScanner functions beginCapture(), resumeCapture(), and endCapture() are deprecated in favor of a unified scan() function and will be retired in a future release. _(v58-lwc-011, Summer '23)_
- **[deprecation]** Several lightning/uiRecordApi functions and wire adapters are now deprecated: getRecordNotifyChange (use notifyRecordUpdateAvailable), getRecordUi (use record form components or getRecord/getRecords), getRecordInput (construct record objects manually), and refresh (use refreshApex or notifyRecordUpdateAvailable). _(v58-lwc-014, Summer '23)_
- **[deprecation]** The Odometer Status picklist field on the Vehicle object is deprecated in favor of the new Odometer State field for storing odometer information. _(v60-rest-016, Spring '24)_
- **[deprecation]** Several User Interface API list-view endpoints are deprecated in favor of consolidated alternatives. The deprecated resources include /ui-api/list-ui/*, /ui-api/mru-list-records/*, /ui-api/mru-list-info/*, and /ui-api/mru-list-ui/* paths. _(v61-rest-015, Summer '24)_
- **[deprecation]** Sender ID email authentication is deprecated and unavailable for new orgs created in Winter '25 or later. Existing integrations using Sender ID (records prefixed with v=spf2.0) continue functioning but the option to enable it in Email Deliverability settings is removed for new orgs. _(v62-auth-001, Winter '25)_
- **[deprecation]** Triple DES (3DES) encryption for SAML SSO is deprecated and will no longer be supported, affecting orgs still using this algorithm for SAML assertion encryption. _(v63-auth-003, Spring '25)_
- **[deprecation]** Triple DES encryption for SAML SSO assertions can no longer be selected when creating new configurations. Existing configurations still work but should be migrated to AES-128 or AES-256 to avoid future enforcement. _(v63-auth-009, Spring '25)_
- **[deprecation]** Einstein Prediction Builder is entering deprecation. Organizations relying on this feature for custom AI predictions should plan migration to alternative solutions. _(v63-other-003, Spring '25)_
- **[deprecation]** Omniscripts built on AngularJS are being deprecated and will lose support, requiring migration to the LWC-based standard designer. _(v63-other-006, Spring '25)_
- **[deprecation]** The enableGuestRecordReassignOrgPref field in CommunitySettings and enableSitesRecordReassignOrgPref field in SiteSettings are deprecated at API 63.0 because the underlying preference is now permanently enabled for all orgs. _(v63-packaging-005, Spring '25)_
- **[deprecation]** The Insecure External Assets event type in EventLogFile no longer captures data because HTTPS is now mandatory for external assets. _(v63-rest-008, Spring '25)_
- **[deprecation]** The Environments field on FlowDefinitionView is deprecated; developers querying flow environment support should switch to the SupportedEnvironments field on the same object. _(v63-rest-012, Spring '25)_
- **[deprecation]** The Place Order and Place Quote Connect REST APIs are deprecated starting in API version 63.0; integrations should migrate to the unified Place Sales Transaction API. _(v65-rest-020, Winter '26)_
- **[deprecation]** Triple DES encryption for SAML SSO will cease to function in Winter '26, requiring migration to stronger encryption algorithms before that release. _(v64-auth-001, Summer '25)_
- **[deprecation]** The isNamedUserJwtEnabled field on ExtlClntAppOauthConfigurablePolicies is deprecated; JWT-based access tokens must now be enabled solely via the same-named field on ExtlClntAppGlobalOauthSettings. _(v64-auth-003, Summer '25)_
- **[deprecation]** The startUrl field on ExtlClntAppSamlConfigurablePolicies is deprecated in favor of the startUrl field on ExtlClntAppConfigurablePolicies. _(v64-auth-004, Summer '25)_
- **[deprecation]** Agentforce Service Agent verification actions that accept unverified Contact Records are deprecated. New secure actions require a verified Contact ID instead, enforcing customer identity verification before sensitive operations. _(v64-flow-003, Summer '25)_
- **[deprecation]** ESLint v8 support for LWC projects ends in Winter '26; from Spring '26 onward, new linting rules and fixes will only target ESLint v9, requiring migration to the flat config format. _(v64-lwc-006, Summer '25)_
- **[deprecation]** The DeliveryMethodId field on CartDeliveryGroup is deprecated starting in API 64.0 and scheduled for removal in API 66.0. Code should migrate to the same-named field on CartDeliveryGroupMethod instead. _(v64-rest-007, Summer '25)_
- **[deprecation]** The AssessmentQstnVerChoice object is deprecated in favor of the new AssessmentQstnVerChoice2 object. Integrations querying or manipulating assessment question version choices should migrate to the replacement object. _(v64-rest-014, Summer '25)_
- **[deprecation]** The planned Winter '26 retirement of Triple DES encryption for SAML SSO has been delayed indefinitely. Existing configurations using 3DES continue to function, though migration to AES-128 or AES-256 remains recommended. _(v65-auth-015, Winter '26)_
- **[deprecation]** SLDS 2 deprecates multiple global styling hooks including color-accent, color-brand-base-100, color-error/info/success/warning-base-100, font-family, and font-lineheight variants. Components using these hooks must migrate to replacement hooks to avoid future breakage. _(v65-lwc-008, Winter '26)_
- **[deprecation]** The Field Service Mobile application will no longer support Android 10 devices. Organizations relying on this platform version for field service workflows should plan device upgrades. _(v65-other-002, Winter '26)_
- **[deprecation]** The enableDashboardCmpRefreshPref field on AnalyticsSettings metadata is deprecated because Lightning Experience dashboard component refresh is now always enabled by default. _(v65-packaging-001, Winter '26)_
- **[deprecation]** Three fields on ConversationChannelDefinition metadata type are deprecated: isInboundReceiptsEnabled, isRoutingWorkResultEnabled, and isTypingIndicatorDisabled. Each has a replacement field that should be used starting in API 65.0. _(v65-packaging-002, Winter '26)_
- **[deprecation]** Data Cloud no longer auto-generates a default retriever when creating search indexes; integrations relying on this automatic provisioning must now explicitly create retrievers. _(v65-rest-001, Winter '26)_
- **[deprecation]** The Manage Loyalty Programs permission set is being retired. Orgs using it must migrate to custom permission sets or profiles before enforcement to preserve user access to Loyalty Management objects. _(v65-sharing-002, Winter '26)_
- **[deprecation]** The enableConsumerSecretApiAccess field on ExternalClientAppSettings is deprecated; OAuth consumer secrets for external client apps can no longer be retrieved via Metadata API and must be obtained through the UI instead. _(v66-auth-014, Spring '26)_
- **[deprecation]** The ability to create new Reorder Portals in B2B Commerce is being deprecated. Existing portals continue to function, but new implementations should use alternative approaches. _(v66-other-002, Spring '26)_
- **[deprecation]** The Field Service mobile application will no longer receive support on Android 11 devices. Organizations relying on Android 11 for field operations should plan device upgrades. _(v66-other-003, Spring '26)_
- **[deprecation]** Billing and Usage Assistant will no longer function in Communications orgs starting Summer '26. Organizations relying on this feature must migrate to alternative solutions before the deprecation takes effect. _(v66-other-010, Spring '26)_
- **[deprecation]** Salesforce is removing the ability to create new branded login pages for Trialforce Source Orgs starting Summer '26, as part of retiring the .cloudforce.com hostname. Existing branded login configurations remain functional. _(v66-packaging-001, Spring '26)_
- **[deprecation]** Claude 3 Haiku model calls through Amazon Bedrock will automatically redirect to Claude Haiku 4.5 starting late February 2026, potentially altering prompt responses and application behavior. _(v66-rest-007, Spring '26)_
- **[deprecation]** The Position and Tip fields on EventBusSubscriber are deprecated in favor of LastProcessed and LastPublished, which use string types to accommodate replay IDs that exceed integer limits. _(v66-rest-012, Spring '26)_
- **[deprecation]** Communications TMF APIs gain Apex lifecycle hooks and GraphQL query extensibility, plus direct invocation via Connect/Apex REST endpoints. The MuleSoft gateway routing option is deprecated and will be removed in Winter '27. _(v66-rest-024, Spring '26)_
- **[deprecation]** Connected apps for Partner Telephony integrations are deprecated in favor of External Client Apps (ECAs). Creating new connected apps now requires explicit approval from Salesforce Support, signaling eventual retirement of the connected app model for this use case. _(v67-auth-021, Summer '26)_
- **[deprecation]** The Billing and Usage Assistant feature in Communications Cloud is now deprecated and will be removed in a future release. _(v67-rest-002, Summer '26)_
- **[deprecation]** Einstein Quick Quote for Enterprise Sales Management has been scheduled for deprecation in Communications Cloud. _(v67-rest-003, Summer '26)_
